# 飞驰！明日之城 - Floor It! To the Golden City

## 目录

- FT-06 乐园在即 / Elysium Is Coming
- FT-07 好哥们，好主顾 / Best Buds, Best Guest
- FT-08 晚祷的叮嘱 / A Warning at Dinner
- FT-09 离巢的蛇 / Snake in the Grass
- FT-10 再见，鼠辈 / See You, Rats

- FT-22 门前足音 / Unanswered Door

## FT-01 周末狂热 / Weekend Fever

**鸵鸟电台**：下午好，旧金山！下午好，乳臭未干的兔崽子、嗜酒如命的老烟枪，以及我漂亮的小心肝儿们！\
**Ostrich Radio**: Goood afternoon, San Francisco, to my dazed-out junkies, my loud and proud mischief-makers, and all my beautiful little heartthrobs!

**鸵鸟电台**：我是你们的老朋友，比你离家出走的老爸更让你恨之透骨，比半夜给你煮通心粉的老妈更爱你的——“老鸵鸟文森”！\
**Ostrich Radio**: It's your oldest and dearest friend, with the straight shooting of your father and tender-loving just like your mama. It's your boy, Vincent, aka "The Old Ostrich"!

**鸵鸟电台**：先听听好消息！自1987年“谐波汇聚运动”结束，死气沉沉的新纪元集市在近日迎来了新生。\
**Ostrich Radio**: Bringing you a balanced dish of good news and bad news! Let's soften the blow with the good stuff first: The New Age Market has finally gotten a little reinvigoration after the Harmonic Convergence.

**鸵鸟电台**：有人说是外星文明发来了最新电波，有人说是玛雅末日的感召……但这都不重要，对吗？我的朋友！\
**Ostrich Radio**: Was it a sign from another world, or the harbinger of a Mayan doomsday prophecy? Who knows? But why worry, my lovelies? Keep those heads in the sand and your ears to the ground.

**鸵鸟电台**：更多的游客，更多的钞票……连我邻居的小男孩都嗅到了这个商机！\
**Ostrich Radio**: Because more visitors means more money! Huuuuge potential for young and old to make some dough!

**鸵鸟电台**：当然，还有一则坏消息——\
**Ostrich Radio**: Now, to hit you with the bad news—

**鸵鸟电台**：昨天，旧金山的“火”从拖车贫民窟一直烧到市政大厅，子弹壳跟我家水龙头一样“叮叮当当”了一整晚！整个旧金山的尿不湿都要卖脱销了！\
**Ostrich Radio**: Yesterday's gangland battles stretched from the sticks all the way to the steps of the People's Palace. And it came with a particularly heavy drizzle of bullet casings to rattle you all night long!

**鸵鸟电台**：昨晚，死人莱格斯和他的神秘学家崽子们，把“东青商会”一脚踹出了旧金山！\
**Ostrich Radio**: Last night, Legers the Dead and his arcanist minions booted the Tung Ch'ing Cham so hard in the ass, that they've been driven right out of our city!

**鸵鸟电台**：如果你们现在去街上抬抬脚，说不定还能捡上几颗完整的金牙，喝上一辈子都没尝过的独角兽口涎！\
**Ostrich Radio**: If you're brave enough to head out into the streets, might still find a few gold teeth left on the ground!

**鸵鸟电台**：有人说，旧金山总该要太平几天了。不不不，我天真的朋友！\
**Ostrich Radio**: Now, the sweet naive souls among you might think that means our fair city will finally have a moment of peace. But you listen to Papa Ostrich here, kiddies, this is only the beginning!

**鸵鸟电台**：死人莱格斯吃得下整个旧金山，自然也需要一些小甜品。\
**Ostrich Radio**: What Legers wants is nothing less than the whole damned city, and I have it on good authority where he's headed next.

**鸵鸟电台**：莱格斯放出消息，关于新纪元集市，他想跟海特街的J谈一桩不能拒绝的好交易。\
**Ostrich Radio**: I'm told his aim is to make a deal with Haight Street's very own Joe, aka "J Brown," for a stake in that juicy New Age Market pie.

**鸵鸟电台**：对此，咱们只能祝这位好哥们睡个好觉！\
**Ostrich Radio**: Here's hoping that it goes smoothly, but if that fails, at least we'll have some quality entertainment.

**鸵鸟电台**：废话不多说，接下来让我们听听《The Golden City》。心肝儿们、混球们，启动你们的小马达，摆起来吧！\
**Ostrich Radio**: Now it's time for The Old Ostrich to duck his head again, leaving you with some solid music to grooove your body and shaaake your booty with our next track: The Golden City.

**酒侍**：这小子的嘴巴比咱们的鞋底还不干净，不是吗？瞧，要点儿什么，伙计？\
**Bartender**: "Papa Ostrich," *sneer* give me a break—anyways, what can I get you, guy?

**杰洛**：一杯龙舌兰。\
**Gio**: Tequila.

他摆摆手，身后的跟随者们四散而去，隐匿到涌动的人群中。\
Gio waves his hand, and the rest of his gang break off into the crowd.

**杰洛**：还有——\
**Gio**: And ...

他从外套内掏出一小捆绑起来的钞票，立在桌子上。\
He pulls a bundle of notes from inside his jacket and puts it on the table.

**酒侍**：干脆又直接……我喜欢跟你这样上道的伙计交朋友。\
**Bartender**: Straight-forward. I like that.

**酒侍**：想知道点儿什么？女侍的电话号码、地下拳击赛的门票，又或是哪个混小子惹了一身——\
**Bartender**: So what are you after? The waitress's phone number, ticket to an underground boxing match, or you after someone specific?

喋喋不休的话语令他烦躁不安。\
The bartender's idle chatter digs under Gio's skin.

**杰洛**：闭上嘴，你这个杂碎！\
**Gio**: You know what I'm after? I'm after you shutting your damned mouth!

侍者被狠狠揪了过去，衣领拧成了皱巴巴一圈。\
He yanks the bartender by the collar, pulling him in close as he growls out his next words.

**杰洛**：他*的，竖起耳朵听好了，把你的小聪明收起来，我只问一个问题——\
**Gio**: Cut the smart s**t with me and listen, 'cause I'm only going to ask once:

**杰洛**：谁——是——J？抬起你的手指，指出来，然后拿着钱滚出我的视线！\
**Gio**: WHERE IS J? Point him out, then get your ass out of my sight!

**酒侍**：喔噢，嘿、嘿……！别紧张，伙计，你就算不给小费，我也很乐意帮你这个忙。\
**Bartender**: Whoa, hey, hey! Easy, man! I'd be happy to; you don't even gotta tip me.

**酒侍**：那个混账欠了我一屁股的债，我巴不得你能拔下他几颗门牙，再把他揍出*来。\
**Bartender**: That bastard owes me money. So, you can go ahead and beat his ass, throw in a kick for me.

衣领缓缓松开了。\
He drops the bartender's collar.

**杰洛**：你最好在说实话。\
**Gio**: You'd better not be playing with me, because that's a good way to get cut.

**酒侍**：我得事先提醒你，他是一个在海特街土生土长的乡巴佬，闭着眼都能在这巷子里，把警察给遛成傻子。\
**Bartender**: But, hey man, little heads up: J was born and raised in Haight Street, and he knows the place better than anyone. Ran circles around the cops. He won't be easy to corner.

**酒侍**：再加上他结交了不少朋友，在这地界找他麻烦总不是个好主意，你猜不准他那些跟屁虫会从哪里绊你一脚。\
**Bartender**: Plus, he's got a lot of friends around, so picking a fight here could go south fast. Never know who's liable to stand beside him.

在杰洛的面色发青前，他机灵地把话锋一转。\
Gio's eyes narrow and dart around the room, but the bartender attempts to change the subject to calm things.

**酒侍**：但你要我说实话吗？——这混账的世道也是该结束了，让J和他那帮跟班见鬼去吧！\
**Bartender**: But you know what I say? The good times are over, so J and all his crew can bite the big one for all I care.

**酒侍**：你是我见过头一个这么有骨气的家伙，不管你有没有打断他的鼻梁骨——\
**Bartender**: Hey, and uh, just so you know, you're the first one with enough guts to mess with him, so whether you're here to break his nose or ...

**酒侍**：这杯算我的，朋友。敬你——和你的老板！\
**Bartender**: Well, this shot's on me, bro. To you, and your boss!

子弹杯轻轻碰撞，在共同的仇人面前，酒精成为了友谊的代名词。\
The clinking shot glasses at last break the ice, as a wry, wolfish grin escapes Gio's face.

**杰洛**：呼，你是个有眼力见儿的混账，脑袋还算灵光……我们很缺这样的小伙子。\
**Gio**: Ha, you're a smart ass. We need more people like you.

**杰洛**：现在尽是一些被街机厅的弹子球和吃角子老虎机搞坏了脑袋的年轻人……你明白，就是那些掏空了老妈的积蓄，跪在门前求份工作的可怜虫。\
**Gio**: Young guys these days are jammed by arcades and slots, you know. These adult children living in their mothers' basements. They ought to be out here begging for a job.

强而有力的手掌搭上了酒侍的肩膀。\
A heavy hand lands on the bartender's shoulder.

**杰洛**：告诉我，伙计，你叫什么名字？\
**Gio**: What's your name, pal?

**酒侍**：维恩，先生。\
**Bartender**: It's Vern, sir.

**杰洛**：很高兴认识你，维恩，叫我杰洛。\
**Gio**: Put 'er there, Vern. Call me Gio.

他们手掌相握，这段友谊看上去已经历了数万种考验。\
Their hands clasp together in a hearty shake.

**杰洛**：好了，现在告诉我哪个杂种是J。等我办完了事，如果你想干一番事业，咱们可以在外面的脂粉街碰头，我去带你通通气儿。\
**Gio**: Alright, now you point me to this J bastard. And afterward, if you're looking to do some hustling, meet me at Rouge Street. I'll take you to the boss.

**杰洛**：不过，这得由你自己把握——老头最近的脾气捉摸不定，谁也保不准。\
**Gio**: But, uh, mind yourself around him, will ya? The old man's been unpredictable lately. Quick to fly off the handle, you know?

**酒侍**：谢谢你，先生，不过……\
**Bartender**: Thank you, sir, umm ...

酒侍欲言又止，把头倾了过来。\
The bartender moves to speak, tilting his head to one side.

**酒侍**：原谅我的好奇，先生。但你能告诉我那个混账犯了什么事儿吗？\
**Bartender**: I probably shouldn't pry, but, what do you want from J?

**酒侍**：如果是为了这地方，据我所知，海特街这地方穷得叮当响，半点油水都捞不着，除了穷鬼还是穷鬼，连那帮假迷三道的骗子都得空手而归……\
**Bartender**: If you wanna take him down over Haight Street, you'll be disappointed. This place's got nothing but struggling folks. You couldn't mug someone for enough to catch the bus.

**杰洛**：还能是什么？就是那该死的新纪元集市，老头子不知道是着了什么魔，非得掺上一脚。\
**Gio**: What else could it be? That damn New Age Market. Don't know what Pops is planning to do with it, but he's got to have it.

**杰洛**：我当然对这地方没有半点兴趣，谁会想到在臭水沟里淘金？\
**Gio**: Not like I'd give a damn otherwise. What kinda schmuck does business in a gutter like this?

**杰洛**：但老头子的态度强硬得很……要按以前，我至少还可以哼一句反调，私底下跟他说几句。可现在，他除了“启明会”的人，谁的话也听不进去。\
**Gio**: But Pops' stubborn about it. Used to be I'd have a say in private, but he don't listen to anyone now except those freaks from the "Order of Enlightenment."

**杰洛**：搜刮穷人、痛揍哭哭啼啼的娘娘腔……这些就不是什么拿得出台面的事，但当这活儿到了你手里……\
**Gio**: Not that I'm crying about it, but robbing folks who ain't got no money, kicking 'em while they're down ... It don't sit right. But orders are orders.

**杰洛**：你就只能把自己当成瞎子，或者——\
**Gio**: So, maybe I'll turn a blind eye, when I can.

他退了一步，本能的警惕令他截住了脱口而出的话语。\
The grin on his face goes sour, and he scans the bartender's face again.

**杰洛**：你不该问太多，小子。\
**Gio**: You ask too many questions.

**酒侍**：抱歉……回到正题吧。你可以往舞池旁边望，瞧见那个穿西装、打领带，打扮得人模人样的家伙了吗？\
**Bartender**: No worries, man. But you were looking for J, right? That guy in the suit, near the dance floor. See him?

话音还未结束，男人已经离开了吧台。\
Gio is already up and walking away before the bartender could finish.

跟随者们犹如群狼般，推开人群，往他走向的地方涌去。\
His followers join him as he moves, advancing like hungry wolves toward their target.

**酒侍**：……\
**Bartender**: ...

卑微与谄媚荡然无存，这位牌桌上的赌徒露出了冷静的面孔。\
The bartender drops his act, and with it, his smile turns fierce.

片刻，邻座沉默的舞者，也起身了。\
At the same moment, the silent woman stands up from another table and makes a graceful exit.

**环状水星**：J，待会见。\
**Mercuria**: See you later, J.

吧台前的酒侍点了点头。\
The bartender responds with an imperceptible nod.

…………\
...

虹色的光将一切映衬得如此梦幻。\
The technicolor lights cast everything in a dreamy glow.

随着躁动的迪斯科舞曲，男孩女孩们摆动着身姿，全然没发现身旁有一群人正悄然聚拢。\
Caught in the ecstasy of the pumping music, the dancers on the floor are unaware of the scene unfolding nearby.

俯下身子的男人屏息着，盯准了猎物。\
The lead wolf fixes his gaze on his target and signals to his pack.

**杰洛**：3、2——1！\
**Gio**: Three, two, one!

他们不约而同地窜了出来，健步如飞地扑了上去。\
On his signal, they rush to the well-dressed gentleman.

**杰洛**：按住他的胳膊儿!\
**Gio**: Hold him down!

如同水牛被豹子扑倒，西装革履的男人狠狠跌倒在地。\
In a flurry of action, the gentleman is thrown from his seat down to the ground.

人群受到惊吓，音乐也骤然停了下来。\
As the violence erupts, the crowded dance floor freezes, and the music stops on a skip.

**？？？**：先生们，这是怎么一回事？！\
**???**: Gentlemen, what is happening here?

杰洛踩在他的肩膀上，俯下身。\
Gio steps hard on the gentleman's shoulder, leaning down on him.

他知道这个混球现在已经是任他宰割的猪了。\
His face is twisted into a predator's smile.

**杰洛**：把他的手拧紧点儿——但别掰断了，这才只是一个开始。\
**Gio**: Tie up his hands, but careful you don't break them, for now ...

**“牙医”Ⅰ**：是，杰洛先生。\
**"Dentist" I**: Sure thing, Mr. Gio.

他的手掌增强了力度，青筋泛起，接着——\
His grip tightens, veins bulging, and then—

“咔嚓。”\
*cracks*

**“牙医”Ⅰ**：……？\
**"Dentist" I**: ...?

男人的手掉落在地，如同一只滚落逃走的轮胎。\
The gentleman's hand pulls loose from his body, popping up through their grip and rolling across the floor.

**杰洛**：我他*，你是怎么——嗯？\
**Gio**: What the hell? What's going on with ... Huh?

一只手轻轻敲了敲他的肩膀，他转过身。\
An unseen hand taps Gio's shoulder. He turns his head.

“砰！”——重重的拳头撞击下颚。\
"Pow!"—A heavy punch strikes him across the jaw.

**杰洛**：呃！\
**Gio**: Urrh!

**J**：啧……这么硬。你的下巴是铁疙瘩做的吗？\
**J**: That hurts. You got rocks in your jaw?

他甩甩涨红的手，旋即拉起倒地的假人。\
J shakes his bruising hand before extending it down to the mannequin gentleman on the floor.

**J**：伙计，相信我，你作为诱饵，已经可以钓完整片太平洋了。\
**J**: Trust me, you're the perfect bait. You draw the fishes in like a magnet.

**先驱者**：——诱饵？！\
**Pioneer**: I'm bait?

**先驱者**：J，你真是个混球，这是第几次了？！我的灵魂也是有痛觉的！\
**Pioneer**: This is terribly unbecoming of you, J! Do you realize how many times this is? My body may be artificial, but my soul can feel pain, too!

**杰洛**：……\
**Gio**: ...

**杰洛**：呵，呸……\
**Gio**: Heh heh. *spit*

他鄙夷地啐了一口鲜血。\
Gio spits a gob of red from his bloody mouth.

**杰洛**：骗子杂种，你果然名不虚传。\
**Gio**: You lying sack of s**t.

同僚们扶起杰洛，他擦拭掉嘴角的红色。\
He wipes his hand across his face, as he is helped up by his followers.

与舞池格格不入的人群紧随杰洛身后，犹如一道不断逼近的盾墙。\
The lackeys all square up beside their leader.

**J**：来势汹汹啊，兄弟们。\
**J**: Not so friendly after all, huh?

**先驱者**：……J，我待会再来算你的账。\
**Pioneer**: We'll continue our conversation later, J.

“哐——”\
"Pop—"

挑衅者的匕首飞落在地。\
Gio's dagger falls to the ground in a ringing clatter.

**J**：杰洛先生，你食言了……你没法帮我把那个混账J的鼻梁骨打碎。\
**J**: Now, who's lying, Mr. Gio? You took my shot, but you didn't even break that J guy's nose.

**J**：不过还是谢谢你的引荐，替我向莱格斯先生问好。\
**J**: Still, thanks for the offer. Give my best to Mr. Legers for me.

局势超出了挑衅者的预期，令他开始懊悔最初的鲁莽。\
Gio is beat, and he knows it.

**杰洛**：呵……莱格斯会喜欢你这样的愣头青的，小子。\
**Gio**: Heh. The old man is gonna like you, smart ass.

**杰洛**：关于新纪元集市，我很期待下次的“和谈”。\
**Gio**: See you next time. We'll have another "parley," you and me.

层层围堵下，他们往后撤着，终于退出了大门。\
He falls back toward the door flanked by his lackeys, before making a hasty exit.

**贝克特**：噗——滚吧，莱格斯的狗崽子们！\
**Becket**: Yeah, yeah, run on home with your tail between your legs. *spit* Legers's losers!

**J**：现在谁才是“牙医”？谁的牙齿才掉了满地？！\
**J**: Looks like he might need a "Dentist," 'cause he just got kicked in the teeth!

**J**：全垒打！朋友们，咱们让他们摔了个大跟头！\
**J**: They'll be home crying into their cereal soon enough! Haha!

**J**：呵……这帮家伙跑得比我四缸的蜂鸟G-R8100都要快上一百倍，我发誓他们如果不干“牙医”这一行，指定都是旧金山田径队的好苗子。\
**J**: The way they're hoofing it, they coulda outran my 4-cylinder Hummingbird G-R8100. They must have missed their calling. They ain't dentists. They're track stars.

欢呼声溢满舞厅，烧烫了的水也不如他们沸腾。\
The dance hall breaks into jeering laughter.

人们从狼藉中捡起酒瓶，不约而同地举了起来。\
Bottles are raised and cheers made in recognition of their triumph.

**贝克特**：哈哈……祝我们的友谊胜过狗的忠诚！\
**Becket**: Hahaha. Cheers! To unbreakable bonds!

**众人**：祝友谊胜过狗的忠诚！\
**All**: To unbreakable bonds!

人们互相搀扶着交杯，舞厅里重新放起了音乐。\
After a cascade of clinking glasses, the music is spun up once more, and the club returns to their dancing.

沸腾延续了很久，直到一位灰头土脸的年轻人凑了过来。\
The excitement continues for some time after, only being broken by the arrival of a disheveled looking young man.

**霍利克**：你瞧，J——我得先走了，救济大厅的门再晚一些就要关了……\
**Hollick**: Look, J, I gotta go. The shelter's gonna be closing up soon.

**霍利克**：我修车铺的合伙人……你知道的——\
**Hollick**: My partner at the shop, you know ...

他沾满黑油的手指揉着鼻子，鼻血已经干硬在了嘴唇上。\
He rubs his stained-black fingers across his face, shaking off some flakes of drying blood.

**霍利克**：他不喜欢我挂了彩的脸，说会吓走那些开好车的客人。\
**Hollick**: He doesn't like it when I come in covered with blood, scares the richie-rich types away.

人们知道时间已经不早了。\
It is getting late.

命运只是在这一刻垂下了它的头颅。\
The celebratory atmosphere wears thin and tired as more people leave.

**J**：没事……没事，哥们儿，是我该谢谢你们，如果有什么我能帮上忙的——\
**J**: It's all good, bro. Thanks for coming today. If there's anything I can help ...

J拍拍他的肩膀，抱住了他。\
J pats his friend on the shoulder before pulling him into a hug.

**J**：J永远忠于你们。\
**J**: You know where to go.

霍利克吸了吸鼻子，把手挽在了J的脖子上。\
Hollick sniffs, returning the hug with a tight squeeze.

**霍利克**：没问题，J，我接受你的好意——\
**Hollick**: Heh-heh. Thanks, bro. But, if you're really such a good friend ...

**霍利克**：我……正好看中了一辆敞篷的野马M3，最近我的手头有点紧，你应该能从口袋里掏出个几百万美金给我解解馋吧？\
**Hollick**: How about you spot me, a quarter mil- or so, so I can buy that sweet new convertible Lamberrari LM50. Since we're such good buddies, right?

**J**：去你*的，我就知道，哈哈哈哈……\
**J**: Yeah, sure thing, buddy, right after I give you a knuckle sandwich, hahahaha.

**霍利克**：哈哈哈哈哈哈，再见——再见，J。\
**Hollick**: Hahahaha, see you around, J!

随着他的离开，其余的人也纷纷向J招呼了过来。\
Waving off the mostly gentle giant, the rest of the group gathers around J.

今天这帮势不可挡的老伙计，是最骄傲的命运之父。\
Spirits are still high as they bask in today's victory.

但明天，他们依旧得埋下头，干一份糊口的活计。\
But tomorrow, they must get back to work.

此时，角落之中，一个身影也终于踉踉跄跄地走了出来。\
The moment shifts as a stumbling dummy drives a playful kick into J's leg.

**先驱者**：把我的手还给我，可恶的家伙！\
**Pioneer**: Would you kindly give me back my damn hand already?

**J**：噢，别、别踹我——马上还给你！\
**J**: Hey, stop kicking me! Just a sec!

**先驱者**：呼呼……\
**Pioneer**: *panting*

**先驱者**：咳、咳……抱歉，我刚才似乎有些失礼。\
**Pioneer**: M-my apologies. Where were my manners?

**先驱者**：希望你没往心里去，但我也得警告你，这事——\
**Pioneer**: Please don't take it personally, but I need to warn you that ...

**J**：喔，不对……等等，等等！咱们是不是还少了一个人？\
**J**: Whoa, wait, wait! Someone's missing.

灯球仍在旋转，理应有人表演的舞台上却空无一人。\
The disco ball continues its spin over the empty dance floor.

**J**：环状水星呢？！……嘿，斯普特尼克女士，你知道她去哪了吗？\
**J**: Where's Mercuria? Hey, Ms. Sputnik, have you seen her?

头顶的灯球，僵硬地转过身。\
His eyes fix on the shining ball, which stops then descends from the ceiling to speak.

**斯普特尼克**：噢，您在找环状水星女士吗？她刚才拾起匕首，看上去很匆忙地离开了。\
**Sputnik**: Oh, Ms. Mercuria? She left in a hurry, carrying that dagger those rough-type gentlemen dropped.

**先驱者**：呃，我们需要跟上去吗……？\
**Pioneer**: Do we follow her?

**J**：不，当然不用。\
**J**: No, of course not.

**J**：你我都知道，她就是这么一个人。\
**J**: She's just doing her thing.

他望着空无一人的舞台，耸了耸肩。\
He shrugs, looking out past the door.

跑、奔跑……他踉跄着，频繁地回望那长巷，气喘吁吁。\
Gio stumbles. He catches his breath before glancing back through the long alleyway.

**杰洛**：该、该死……哈、哈呼……老头子可没告诉我们，这里比蜂窝还闹腾……\
**Gio**: *panting* S**t! The old man didn't tell us what kind of mess we were in for here!

**杰洛**：他的筹码显然给少了。\
**Gio**: I'm not paid enough for this.

**杰洛**：呼……\
**Gio**: *panting*

**杰洛**：？！\
**Gio**: ?!

**环状水星**：你好，先生。\
**Mercuria**: Hey. Gio, right?

他怔住了，雕塑般僵在了原地。\
He stands unmoving, unblinking.

**杰洛**：刀把……\
**Gio**: You're just giving it back?

**杰洛**：真是可笑，你追过来就是为了侮辱我？！\
**Gio**: What's this meant to be, some kinda insult?

**杰洛**：很好。我只是谈判不成功，并不是失去了尊严……狂妄的女人！\
**Gio**: Hey, y-your boss runs me off, now you're giving me back my own knife, like I'm some pity case? Think I won't hurt you 'cause you're a woman? Think again, b***h.

愤怒覆盖了恐惧，驱使着他本能地挥舞手臂。\
Anger overtakes his wariness of the woman, and he swings out his arm.

“叮——”\
"Clink—"

匕首被甩飞在地，从口袋中，他的术杖露出了尖。\
The dagger drops to the ground as he reaches into his pocket, producing a wand.

**杰洛**：蚀肉剜心！\
**Gio**: Vita Void!

**环状水星**：唔……\
**Mercuria**: Umm ...

**环状水星**：这是什么？\
**Mercuria**: What is this?

黑色的术式轨迹刚触碰到她的身躯，便溃散在空中。\
The black arcane symbols dissolve in the air as soon as they touch her.

**环状水星**：黑黝黝的，就像J在铁匠炉里烤的甜甜圈……我还从没见过这样的能量，先生。\
**Mercuria**: The color of your energy is as dark as the coal in J's forge, no, worse, darker than I've ever seen before.

她跳下铁门，拾起了匕首。\
She jumps down from the fence and picks up the dagger.

**环状水星**：你……很害怕，但在害怕之中，还夹杂着一些像火焰一样的色环，它焚烧屋子，将一切都变为灰烬。\
**Mercuria**: You're afraid. But something else besides that, I see a burning energy—the embers of a home reduced to ashes.

**环状水星**：它贯穿了你生活的始终。于是你的妻子和孩子离家出走，欠债人在众目睽睽之下对你卑躬屈膝。\
**Mercuria**: A harrowing darkness that's followed you throughout your life, when your wife and child left you, when your debtors begged on their knees at your feet.

**杰洛**：……！你、你在说些什么？\
**Gio**: W-what're you talking about?

**环状水星**：啊……我明白了，先生，你以这些富有侵略性的黑色能量为生。\
**Mercuria**: Huh, I understand you now, Mr. Gio. Forced to live with this darkness inside you.

**环状水星**：……唔。\
**Mercuria**: Hmm.

她陷入了沉思。\
She seems lost in her own thoughts.

**环状水星**：请别见怪。我只是来提醒你……先生，你忘了这个。\
**Mercuria**: I'm sorry if I scared you, but I'm only here to return this.

匕首被轻轻放入了大衣口袋，寒意也降临在他身上。\
She delicately places the dagger into his coat pocket. He shivers as if hit by a chill wind.

**环状水星**：这副坚韧的血肉之躯中，似乎正蜷缩着一位瑟瑟发抖的男孩。\
**Mercuria**: You're a boy trembling inside this brawny shell of a man.

**环状水星**：全因你正在迈向一条你并不想涉足的道路，杰洛先生。\
**Mercuria**: You're too far down a path that you never wanted to set foot on, Mr. Gio.

**杰洛**：…………\
**Gio**: ...

**环状水星**：如果你需要帮助，请随时来新纪元集市找我。\
**Mercuria**: If you need help, find me in the New Age Market.

**环状水星**：哼♫哼♪……\
**Mercuria**: *humming*

她轻唱着乐曲，跃动着脚步，缓缓走向了来时的肮脏长巷。\
She hums softly, her steps light as she walks back from the dingy alley.

男人呆站在原地，神思恍惚，直到野猫跳到了他的肩头。\
The man stands in place, lost in her words, until an alley cat leaps over his shoulder.

恍然间，他想起第一次开枪，浑身鲜血与脑浆，躲在厕所里颤抖的午夜。\
In his daze, he recalls the first time he fired a gun, the blood and brain matter, and the trembling midnight he spent hiding in the bathroom after.

**杰洛**：呕……！\
**Gio**: *pukes*

## FT-02 娱乐不至死 / Won't Be Amused to Death

**霍利克**：……所以，等我卸下来轮胎，就对集市里那位忧心忡忡又阔绰的太太说——\
**Hollick**: So as I take off the tire, I notice the gal, some rich lady from the market's got a crazy look of worry on her face.

**霍利克**：“您大可去整个海特街打听打听J和他的朋友，如果我有半点假话，就让那帮敲诈你的家伙打断我的下巴。”\
**Hollick**: So I tell her, "Break my jaw if I'm telling a lie. We're good folks here. Don't believe me? Just ask around about 'J and his friends' on Haight Street"!

吧台上，醉醺醺的修车汉摇摇晃晃，煞有介事地吆喝着。\
At the bar, the drunken mechanic sways unsteadily, bellowing out his story.

勤劳的圆形酒保，匆匆擦干桌上的酒渍。\
The diligent satellite, now serving as a bartender, hovers close, wiping up spilled drinks from the table.

**斯普特尼克**：还请、请小心，霍利克先生……您不该再喝了。\
**Sputnik**: P-please take care, Mr. Hollick. You have been drinking way too much.

**贝克特**：哈哈哈哈，得了吧，霍利克。你才没那么有种。\
**Becket**: Hahaha, come on, Hollick, you don't get the balls.

**贝克特**：J可以替我作证，昨天你小子也就鼻子见了点儿血，就像个打完针的胆小鬼一样哭哭啼啼的——\
**Becket**: I saw this guy get a nose bleed yesterday, and he cried like a little baby. Back me up, J!

他用肘关节戳着一旁的男人，但对方毫无反应。\
He jabs J with his elbow, but J fails to react.

**贝克特**：嘿……J？\
**Becket**: Hey, J?

**J**：……什、什么？\
**J**: W-what?

**贝克特**：这可不像你，有什么事还能把你的魂儿从钱眼里勾走？\
**Becket**: Did they bust your head or something? You're off daydreaming while we're talking about some rich bimbo.

**先驱者**：抱歉，贝克特先生……J可能有些事还没想清楚，你知道的……关于“死人莱格斯”。\
**Pioneer**: Sorry, Mr. Becket. I believe J's present concerns may be revolving around, you know, "Legers the Dead."

**J**：噢，那你可是大错特错了，朋友！我才没在想那档子事儿！\
**J**: Nah, way off, Stuffed Shirt!

**J**：喏，抬头。\
**J**: Take a look.

**先驱者**：“绝对‘爆炸性’新闻：秘密录像，真空弹恐将成为新的行刑手段？”——呃，当今好莱坞的天才们已经这么疯狂了吗？\
**Pioneer**: "'Bombshell' News: Uncovered Video Shows FAE Used as New Execution Method?" Hmm, what will the minds of those Hollywood producers think of next?

**环状水星**：我也曾见过这个奇怪视频的画面……在被删除的垃圾邮件、报纸的中缝广告插画里。\
**Mercuria**: Oh, I think I've seen images from this video, from spam mail and newspapers.

**洋葱头**：……我们仍在找寻这名身中真空弹的女性，以证实视频的真实性，如若您有独家消息，可致电：429-7234-7……\
**ONiON**: We're still trying to identify this woman to confirm the authenticity of the video. If you have any information, please call us at 429-7234 ext. 7 ...

**洋葱头**：让我们来到下一则新闻——久无音讯的亲人归家，却无人相认，这是一场群体癔症，还是盗取遗产继承权的阴谋？\
**ONiON**: Up Next: Homebound or Hoodwinked? The Mystery of the So-Called Long-Lost Son!

**洋葱头**：近日，一位陌生男性突然拜访退役士兵埃顿先生的家。\
**ONiON**: We turn to the story of Sgt. Howard Eden, a retired army veteran, and the stranger claiming to be his long-lost son.

**洋葱头**：据埃顿先生称，该名男子冒充自己离家出走的儿子，并在他的膝下痛哭流涕。接下来，就让我们——呲呲呲呲……\
**ONiON**: But, is this a heartwarming reunion or a sinister story of senior exploitation? Let's ... *static noise*

老旧的电视机传来了寿终正寝的残喘。\
The old television emits dying sputters of static before cutting out entirely.

**众人**：噢呜……！\
**All**: Awww!

**先驱者**：唉，我还想听她继续说点儿有意思的胡话。\
**Pioneer**: Oh, too bad. You know, it's good fun watching all her nonsense and sensationalism.

**贝克特**：嘿，严肃点！就算这档节目曾预言“土拨鼠将占领地球”，但说不定其他“胡话”里有真事儿呢？！\
**Becket**: Hey, show some respect! Sure, that whole "How Woodchucks Could Control the World" piece she did was a little iffy, but—who knows what those woodchucks could chuck at us?

**J**：……\
**J**: ...

**J**：不过，伙计们……\
**J**: Alright.

**J**：我确实在琢磨死人莱格斯那档子事儿，他是……什么来头？\
**J**: That Legers thing is really bothering me, okay? What's his story?

醉倒的修车汉打了一个激灵，像位被点名的士兵抬起了头。\
The drunk mechanic jolts awake and upright with renewed excitement.

**霍利克**：我、我听过……那是一个了不得的家伙，警察的眼中钉，地痞流氓眼中的……呃，T-800！\
**Hollick**: I've heard it. Not gonna lie. Kinda sick. Cops hate him, but the street punks love him!

**霍利克**：当时，就在猎人角的那片烂木头林里，有一群人把莱格斯当猪一样宰！\
**Hollick**: They say back in Hunters Point, a bunch of guys was torturing him, had him tied up like a pig.

**霍利克**：到最后，他们折磨得腻歪了，就赏了他的脑袋几发子弹——呜，太可怕了，就是拿枪顶着嗓子眼儿……“啪”一下从喉头，直穿过后脑勺！\
**Hollick**: And when they got tired, they put a gun in his mouth and made him eat it. The bullet went straight through his throat out the back of his head!

**霍利克**：结果，等警察来了，除了一地沾了血的牙齿，连半根头发都没找见。\
**Hollick**: But, when the cops came, they found nothing but a few bloody teeth. He was gone!

**霍利克**：唔……真是太吓人，你们知道吗？莱格斯可是一个彻头彻尾的人类！\
**Hollick**: Scary, right? But here's the thing, yeah, Legers is a pure human! So, what happened? Where did he go?

他绘声绘色，指挥家般挥动着毛发旺盛的手臂，最尽职的演员亦不过如此。\
He waves his arms dramatically, animated and almost cartoonish in his performance.

但理智的批评家总是无处不在。\
But his audience is less than captivated.

**先驱者**：……霍利克先生，你是不是最近看了《活死人出没》？死而复生是好莱坞的陈词滥调，你不应把它套在现实生活里。\
**Pioneer**: Mr. Hollick, I think you've been watching too many of those horrible Romero movies. People returning from the dead, that's hokey cinema, not reality.

霍利克被戳中了要害，面红耳赤。\
Hollick goes red, unable to form any defense.

**先驱者**：我们理应考虑其他的可能性，比如——谋划已久的谣传。借助这则耸人听闻的传言，他的组织能吸引来更多臭名昭著的神秘学家……\
**Pioneer**: I can only assume this "Legers the Dead" made up this rumor himself, perhaps so he might attract more powerful arcanists to his side.

**先驱者**：从魔药瘾君子、走私犯到赌场操盘手……也正因如此，他才能一步步蚕食旧金山。\
**Pioneer**: Potion addicts, smugglers, card sharks ... Getting them all under his thumb until he can gobble up the whole of San Francisco.

**霍利克**：直到他踢到了我们这块儿钢板！\
**Hollick**: And yeah, it's been working. But not anymore, 'cause we ain't gonna sit and watch!

**先驱者**：……我们恐怕不是钢板，先生。这场对峙将会比我们此前碰见过的所有，都要危险……况且他们已经与正盘踞在“新纪元集市”的那帮疯子搭上了肩。\
**Pioneer**: Afraid you're overestimating our strength, Mr. Hollick. Their enterprise is much more dangerous than all our previous rivals. No less so if they're aiming on partnering up with the lunatics in the New Age Market.

**环状水星**：是的……已经连续几天没人参加我的冥想会。大家都簇拥在他们身旁，聚拢着一股……令我不安的喜悦。\
**Mercuria**: Gotta agree with that assessment, Pioneer. It's been days since my last session with a paying customer. Seems like everyone is joining up with them, and their energy is disturbing, to say the least.

**环状水星**：他们一直在到处打探消息，试图搜集一些闻所未闻的材料与书籍……\
**Mercuria**: They've been poking around my shop, looking for some rare sort of books and materials, kinds I never even heard of before.

**先驱者**：正面冲突在当下是最愚蠢的选择……J？\
**Pioneer**: I would advise avoiding direct confrontation, J.

**J**：……我在听。\
**J**: I hear you.

这是他不多有的沉默。\
It is a rare moment of calm consideration for their hotheaded leader.

**J**：我们当然会绕开与他们的直接交锋，伙计……但你我都知道这不现实，选择权并不在我们手里。\
**J**: Avoid confrontation, that's the right move for sure. But it's not gonna be possible. They aren't giving us a choice.

**J**：况且，海特街早就被那帮伪善的警察们抛之脑后……除了我们，谁会管这条街的死活？\
**J**: The cops abandoned Haight Street a long time ago. Ain't nobody that cares about these streets but us now.

**J**：先是流浪艺术家们的拖车营被烧毁，接着是一群占卜师连夜离开……而那帮疯子，却盘踞并扎下了根，无辜的神秘学家们受到蛊惑，秩序分崩离析……\
**J**: Remember? That was when all those artists' trailers were burnt down. After that, the rest of the diviners and such were run off quick. It's only those loonies that have stuck around, misguiding arcanists, making everything worse.

他环视着众人。\
He looks to his friends.

**J**：我们当然该逃，我们应该关门大吉，然后买头一班火车票……就像在听见邻居的女人被混账揍得哀嚎时，大惊失色，然后逃之夭夭。\
**J**: If we were smart, we would have left then and there! Closed up shop, took the first bus out of this city, and ran for our miserable, pathetic lives.

**J**：但我们没有，不是吗？\
**J**: But then, we ain't that kind of smart, are we?

**J**：况且，我们站在这里，也不是因为什么狗屁勇敢，而仅仅是因为——这是我们的家。\
**J**: But, this is our home, so we've gotta make our stand here or we'll never stop running.

一旁的假人欲言又止——\
The mannequin next to him speaks, broaching his words carefully.

**先驱者**：J，你误会了我的意思，我是说这已远超乎了我们的能力范畴。我们最好找——\
**Pioneer**: Please, don't misunderstand me, J. I'm only saying: this fight is beyond our capabilities alone. Should we not consider ask- ...

**J**：停——！伙计！\
**J**: Uh-uh-uh, don't you finish that thought. In fact, don't even think it!

他就像听见了一位十年未见的穷朋友突如其来的寒暄，立马敏锐地打断了话头。\
The sharpness of his tone is clear. The idea is beyond consideration, not to be touched on—not even to be breathed.

**J**：我知道你想说什么，但你也发怵得太快了。用不着什么都扯上他们吧？\
**J**: Look, I know what you're saying, but, I don't know, man. That kind of talk is for cowards. We don't have to get them involved in this.

**先驱者**：你得承认，他们虽然爱打官腔一些，但他们对神秘学家的事总是会很上心。\
**Pioneer**: You have to admit that they care about arcanists, despite all their bureaucracy.

**先驱者**：J，基金会对我们而言，并非是一个差劲的选择。\
**Pioneer**: Turning to the Foundation would not be a bad choice for us, J.

一阵恰到好处的沉默。\
A perfectly timed silence.

吧台之下，圆溜溜的酒保探出了脑袋。\
From beneath the bar, the round bartender floats up as if peeking.

**斯普特尼克**：是的，J先生……我赞同先驱者先生的意见——同时，我、我也不想因为那些匪徒而失去现在的好工作。\
**Sputnik**: Yes, Mr. J. I think Mr. Pioneer might be right. I don't want to lose my job because of these bandits.

**斯普特尼克**：……我很乐意替您指路！\
**Sputnik**: I'll be glad to bring you to the Foundation!

**先驱者**：谢谢您，灯球女士，有您的帮助就再好不过了。\
**Pioneer**: Your assistance would be more than welcome, Ms. Disco Ball.

**先驱者**：而且，J，保利娜就在圣洛夫基金会。你明白……说不定你妹妹会为你走走人情，省去一些——流程上的麻烦。\
**Pioneer**: It couldn't possibly hurt to reach out to Paulina. Maybe she could help us with the red tape. She's your sister, after all.

J挪开了视线，就像躲开问题的孩子。\
J looks away and huffs audibly. It's a childish, almost silly, display.

**J**：不不，我得再跟你声明一遍，这是我们自己的事儿。\
**J**: No, no, no. I'm only gonna say this once, and it's for real: This is our OWN business. Nobody else's, especially not hers.

**J**：她决定加入那帮白袍子的时候，甚至都没跟我事先聊过一句话——我们已经有好多年没见过面了。\
**J**: Paulina made her choice. She could've talked with me, she could have approached us, if that's what she wanted. She had the chance. She's had years, not a word.

**J**：她说她有自己的路子要走，当然也说话算话，从没有回过头。\
**J**: She "has her own life," and she made it out of these streets. She ain't coming back. She ain't even looking back.

**J**：她不喜欢咱们，你明白吗？即便她是我唯一的家人，但她就爱那些大理石地砖，爱高高在上的品味，爱那份所谓的整洁与体面——\
**J**: She's not that little girl tagging around us anymore. She's got fancy marble floors now, got all that "decency" and "good taste" that she never had here.

**J**：她早就不是以前那个追着我们打闹的小家伙了。\
**J**: She doesn't need us.

**J**：你要我现在去求她帮忙，看她的冷眼，还不如让我赤身裸体跟你一块儿站在百货大楼的橱窗里。\
**J**: You think I'm gonna scrape down on my knees for her? Ha, I'd rather stick my foot in hot slag. Least that way I'd have one leg to stand on.

**先驱者**：别这样，认真考虑下我们的建议吧。这跟我给商人的交税建议没什么不同——这些办法可都算省事、轻松。\
**Pioneer**: J, please, just give it some thought. This may be the only way for all of us to survive this.

**J**：——呃，我要去拿一瓶汽水！\
**J**: Er, I need a drink!

他喃喃着离开了吧台，逃离现场的速度堪比一只被踩中尾巴的小狗。\
He mumbles and steps away from the bar.

“砰。”——但谁也没料到，一个矮小的身影不偏不倚地撞在了他的裆下。\
"Crash."—But as he does, a darting figure collides into him at an unfortunate angle for the both of them.

**J**：噢！有什、么……东西撞到我的——\
**J**: AH! Something just hit me in ... my ...

他直立的身躯瞬间萎靡，跪倒在地。\
He crumples over, wincing with pain.

紧接着，一堆硬币撒落下来。\
As he collapses, a handful of coins tumbles to the floor.

**？？？**：糟糕……快跑！\
**???**: Shoot. Run!

慌乱的脚步声从吧台钻出。\
The small boy makes a panicked sprint from behind the bar.

圆形酒保恍然意识到了什么。\
The round bartender stammers out a revelation.

**斯普特尼克**：J先生，吧台里的零钱——全都不见了！\
**Sputnik**: Mr. J, all the money in the bar is, ah, how is it you're saying, "gone"!

**J**：快、快，呜……抓住那个小偷！\
**J**: Ca- ... urgh ... Catch that kid!

吧台上的男人起身，挡住不走运的小偷，提起了他的后脖子。\
Becket moves to block the little thief, grabbing him by the scruff of the neck.

他掀开小偷的兜帽。\
He takes a look at the thief's face.

**贝克特**：哈，我就知道，郊区拖车营的惯犯，猫眼维森。\
**Becket**: Ha, knew it, Cateye Wisen, owner of the most infamous sticky fingers from here to the Market and back.

**贝克特**：小子，你爸爸跟“启明会”那帮人搭上关系又失踪之后，你怎么没跟救济所的那帮人走？那里有吃有喝的，你是想念挨揍的滋味了吗？\
**Becket**: Little dude, I know your dad ran off with those guys from the "Order of Enlightenment." But why didn't you go to the shelter? You trying to get yourself hurt out here?

**猫眼维森**：噗——！你这个混球，有种把我放开！\
**Cateye Wisen**: Let me go, you big jerk!

一口唾沫啐在了贝克特的脸上。\
The would-be thief spits on his face.

**贝克特**：呵，这种狗崽子迟早得放进局子里让那帮穿制服的家伙管教管教——\
**Becket**: Humph, sooner or later, someone is gonna teach you a lesson or two.

**贝克特**：你的神秘学家老妈给你留下这么好一双猫眼，肯定想不到竟然被你用作扒窃去了。\
**Becket**: Don't think that arcanist mom of yours wants you using your "cat eye" to steal things.

贝克特抓住男孩的手，夺走他怀里仅剩的硬币。\
Becket grabs the boy's hand, taking his remaining coins.

与此同时，男孩手背上露出了惊心触目的烟蒂烫痕。\
As he does, he reveals a gruesome cigarette burn on the boy's hand.

**贝克特**：……嘿，小子，我也知道你挺过了一段不容易的日子，但别认为全世界都欠着你。\
**Becket**: I know things seem tough right now, kid. But acting like the world owes you something ... it's gonna bring you nothing but trouble.

**贝克特**：我被机器搅断小拇指，被那帮寄生虫一脚踢开的时候，可没拿着枪、蒙着脸挨个抢商店……你这点儿痛苦又算得上什么？\
**Becket**: When I got my finger chewed up by that machine, I lost everything. I coulda went around sticking up places. I didn't. Think you got it worse than me?

**环状水星**：……\
**Mercuria**: ...

一旁，环状水星拾取贝壳一般，捡起了脏兮兮的硬币，迎面走了过来。\
Mercuria picks up the coins strewn about the floor and walks over to them.

她拍了拍贝克特，示意把他放下来。\
She signals Becket to let the boy go.

**贝克特**：嘿，你难道还想纵容这混小子吗？\
**Becket**: Hey, we gonna let him go just like that?

男孩还是被放了下来，两脚瘫软在地。\
As he releases his grip, the boy falls to the ground.

环状水星蹲下身，轻轻打开他的手掌，把硬币塞回了他脏兮兮的手心。\
Mercuria lowers herself to the boy's level, gently slipping the coins back into his dirty hand.

**环状水星**：去吧，你的朋友还在外面等你呢。\
**Mercuria**: Go on. Your friends are waiting out there.

他们望向门外。一群衣衫褴褛、蓬头垢面的孩子发现了目光，连连畏畏缩缩地躲到了门后。\
They look toward the door. A group of ragged, filthy children are watching them back, retreating timidly as they meet their gaze.

**斯普特尼克**：可，J先生……\
**Sputnik**: But, Mr. J ...

**J**：……没关系，给他们吧。\
**J**: It's fine, Sputnik. Let 'em go.

**环状水星**：这些都是在新纪元集市里失去了家的孩子……他们的监护人丢下了他们，不知所踪，留下他们四处游荡。\
**Mercuria**: These kids lost their homes to the New Age Market. Their parents deserted them. They've got nowhere to go.

**J**：……\
**J**: ...

**贝克特**：……\
**Becket**: ...

**环状水星**：贝克特先生，瞧瞧他们……\
**Mercuria**: Becket, look at them.

**环状水星**：苦难是不会相形见绌的。\
**Mercuria**: You can't compare. It doesn't work like that. Each suffering has its own energy.

猫眼维森颤颤巍巍地站了起来，低下头，喃喃着谢谢，走向门口。\
The boy picks himself up, muttering a "thank you" as he walks uneasily toward the door.

一只手搭在了男孩的肩膀上。\
Before he reaches it, a hand rests on his shoulder.

**J**：我说，小子……\
**J**: Hey, kid.

**J**：——你和你那帮跟班，想不想找点活儿？\
**J**: You and your friends looking for some almost-honest cash?

**猫眼维森**：……！你的意思是——\
**Cateye Wisen**: You mean ...!

**猫眼维森**：谢……谢你，先生。\
**Cateye Wisen**: T-Thanks, J.

**猫眼维森**：我的眼睛很敏锐！我能干很多细活……我擅长数火车、数硬币，我还可以看穿那些出千的发牌员，连水滴都能数清楚！\
**Cateye Wisen**: I got sharp eyes! I can do lots of stuff! Counting coins, cars, finding water drops ... I'm great at spotting cheats and shady dealers!

J拍拍他的肩膀。\
J pats him in a brotherly gesture.

**J**：别着急，小子，先填饱肚子。\
**J**: Easy, kid. Fill your belly first.

**J**：斯普特尼克女士，请替我给他们每人做一份热乎乎的墨西哥卷，多放点肉——该死的，瞧瞧他的手腕，真是比唐人街的筷子还细。\
**J**: Ms. Sputnik, please get these kids some burritos. Dang kid, those arms are like chopsticks. Hey, Ms. Sputnik? Let's make those extra meat.

**J**：还有，就当我改主意了吧，伙计——\
**J**: Alright, man. Consider my second thought, thought over.

他整个人趴在吧台上，对着一张老旧的合影长叹了口气。\
He slumps over the bar, giving a long sigh at an old photograph in his hand.

那是一张过于热情、充满关切的脸，撞上了另一份渴望距离与自由，以及理想的冷漠。\
In the photo, he stares at the girl caringly, while she looks cold, longing for independence and freedom.

但不管如何——\
Regardless—

**J**：唉……\
**J**: *sigh*

**J**：不管如何，到时候她如果翘着腿坐在办公桌前，给我摆出一副高高在上的架子——伙计，我保证，谁也拦不住我跨出那扇门！\
**J**: But get this straight: if I see her fold her arms and give me any of that snooty attitude, we're gone, out the door, no discussion!

## FT-03 小匣子 / A Small Box

风晃荡着窗扇，从破洞里窜了进来。\
The wind sways the window shutters as it blows in through its gaps.

薄弱的木门隔绝不住外面的喧嚣，杯子碰撞、客人的咒骂声连续不断。\
The thin door does nothing to block out the noise beyond it—clattering dishes, clinking glasses, and chattering talk peppered with curses.

蜷缩在床上的女孩吸溜着鼻子，紧紧抱着小熊。\
Curled up on the bed, a girl sniffles, holding her teddy bear tightly.

**保利娜**：呜……可是哥哥……从孤儿院里出来的白袍子先生们说，学校里没有凶巴巴的客人，没有耍赖皮的雇主……\
**Paulina**: *sob* But, but Joe! Those men in white said there won't be any more bad people around the school.

**保利娜**：每个孩子都能吃得饱饱的，就跟爸爸妈妈还在的时候一样～\
**Paulina**: And nobody will be hungry, just like before, like with Mom and Dad.

**保利娜**：他们每个星期都会给孩子们提供巧克力、布丁、热汤和牛排……还有超大、超舒适的屋子……咻溜。\
**Paulina**: They'll give us candy, and soup, and real meat every week, and a big, comfy house. *sniff*

她举起小手，夸张地比划着。\
She raises her little hand, as if reaching out to a dream-like house.

**保利娜**：咻咻……啊嚏！\
**Paulina**: *sniff* Achoo!

**J**：呵呵，快把手缩回去，把被子裹好，保利娜。\
**J**: Heh heh, cover up a little more, Polly. You're gonna catch a cold.

坐在小板凳上的男孩，翻过满是柴油的手心，用手背擦了擦她的鼻子。\
Her brother wipes her nose with the back of his coarse and callused hand.

**J**：保利娜，这些大人是不会说话算话的……如果他们给你糖果，就会取走你的另一样东西。\
**J**: You can't trust anything adults tell you like that. If they give us candy, or soup, or even meat, it's because they want something from you.

**J**：如果他们多给你一份小费，也不是因为他们慷慨，而是因为他们有求于你。\
**J**: Nothing you get in this world is just given away. Least of all from people like them.

**保利娜**：可是，他们确实给了我一个不错的工作，瞧，我现在编那些稻草娃娃就能卖钱。\
**Paulina**: But, but they did give me a fun job! See, now I can make straw dolls and sell them for money.

老旧的木桌上，堆叠着一大堆简陋的娃娃。\
The shabby pile of dolls are stacked up on an old wooden table nearby.

**J**：那是因为他们需要你，保利娜的心灵手巧可是海特街数一数二的～\
**J**: That's 'cause they need you. Our little Paulina is one of the most cleverest kids in all of Haight Street!

**保利娜**：所以他们是坏人吗？\
**Paulina**: So, are they bad guys?

**J**：他们当然是。除了唐吉老爹，那些大人都是一样的坏人。\
**J**: Bet on it. Only good adult I ever met is Mr. Tang.

**保利娜**：唔……好吧——可如果，如果他们说的是真的……你就再也不用洗盘子、卸轮胎，干那些又苦又累的活了……\
**Paulina**: Hmm, okay. But Joe, what if they're not lying, then you don't have to wash dishes, or take off tires or any of that stuff.

**唐吉老爹**：J……嘿，J！过来搭把手，客人需要两打啤酒！\
**Tang Ji**: J, hey, J! Two dozen beers for our guests. Get a move on, lazy boy!

洪亮又高亢的嗓音穿过了木门。\
A loud voice booms through the door, his tone sharp but strangely paternal.

**J**：嘿，保利娜，别为我想那么多好吗？除了这里，我哪儿都不去。\
**J**: Don't overthink it, 'kay kiddo? I'm right here with you, always will be.

**保利娜**：那……我们说好了，如果你要去的话，一定要告诉我……谁也不许一个人离开。\
**Paulina**: Okay. But if you do leave, you have to tell me first! Because we'll always stick together! Deal?

**J**：当然，我们说好了。\
**J**: Deal.

他揉搓着她的头发，替她与玩具小熊盖上了被子。\
He rubs her hair before tucking her and her bear into the blanket.

**J**：晚安，保利娜。\
**J**: Sleep tight, Polly.

一束束毫厘不差的石柱，沉默地融入墙体之中。\
Perfectly aligned stone columns blend into the walls.

地面一尘不染，就连自由落体的光，无一不井然有序。\
The floor is spotless, overly tidy, even the lights above shine in exact symmetrical patterns.

那是跟嘈杂与污水遍地的街头小巷，跟充斥着油烟与老鼠的矮房子，全然不同的存在。\
It is a distant and alien world to them, nothing like the cluttered alleys and unkempt streets of home.

**J**：这帮人还真为自己造了一所宫殿……他们到底把自己当成了什么救世主？\
**J**: This place is Ritz'd up like a palace. Who do they think they are?

**J**：哪有人需要那么干净的地板，他们是每天都牵一条小狗把地板舔一遍吗？\
**J**: Who needs a floor that shines like a mirror? What, they hire a dog to lick it clean every day?

**先驱者**：这座建筑也令我讶异，住在其中之人想必都拥有极高的审美趣味……\
**Pioneer**: Oh. Philistine as ever, J. It's evident the people here must possess exceptional aesthetic taste.

**J**：伙计，事到如今，咱们就别拍他们的马屁了，好吗？我打赌，保利娜住在这样的“防空洞”里，肯定不像在咱们的小屋子里那么有安全感！\
**J**: I'm at my limit of you sucking up to them. This place is built like a fortress, a bomb shelter. Makes me feel like I've got a target on my back. Can't imagine why anyone would feel safer here.

**J**：我有一个艺术家朋友可说过：“干净是对想象力的破坏！”这么大的屋子，虽然看上去阔绰，但其实也——\
**J**: You ask any artist, they'll say "clean kills the soul"! Might look clean and tidy on the outside, but inside—

左顾右盼之时，他丝毫没发现正迎面走来的三位职员。\
He looks around absent-mindedly, failing to notice the three staff members walking in his way.

“砰。”——两个肩膀相撞，又错开。\
Wham—Shoulders collide, sending the small girl sprawling over.

**玛蒂尔达**：嗷！疼死了……真倒霉，怎么又碰上个愣头愣脑的笨家伙。\
**Matilda**: Oouphf! That hurt! Ergh, just what this place needs, another stupid oaf that does not know how to watch where he is going!

**J**：嘿，保持体面，傲慢的小家伙。\
**J**: Hey, mind your manners, short stuff.

**玛蒂尔达**：你说什么？谁是小家伙？\
**Matilda**: Excuse me? D-Did you just call me short stuff?

J的身躯并未因为对方逐步升高的气焰而显露让步的打算。\
J is clearly taking pleasure in the petite girl's annoyed outburst.

**先驱者**：呃，抱歉小姐，我替他向您道歉。\
**Pioneer**: I apologize for my friend, Miss. He ought to mind his own manners.

**玛蒂尔达**：算了，你们看上去像是初次来访，我也没什么好计较的。\
**Matilda**: Hmph. Considering you two look as though you have just wandered in like, how do you say, "lost puppies"? I'll let it go, just this once.

**小队成员Ⅰ**：你们是来分部进行神秘学家登记的吗？我们有两位登记员正在换班，你们得稍等一会儿……\
**Team Member I**: Are you here to register as arcanists? Sorry, we're just in the middle of a shift change. Please wait a moment.

**小队成员Ⅱ**：菲娜不是还在值班么？现在也该到了她能独立办事的时候……\
**Team Member II**: Isn't it Fiona's shift? She should be able to handle this on her own.

**玛蒂尔达**：好了。出发前的准备时间所剩无几了……我们还有重要的事情呢，队员们。\
**Matilda**: There is work to be done, people. Quickly, vite vite!

**小队成员Ⅰ**：好的……\
**Team Member I**: Got it.

她带着他们，脚步飞快。\
She leads the team away with swift half-stomping steps.

**职员菲娜**：您、您好！这里是圣洛夫基金会办事处，请问您需要什么帮助？\
**Fiona**: H-hello! Welcome to the St. Pavlov Foundation reception center. How can I help you?

**先驱者**：我们来拜访他的妹妹——呃，出于一些私人事务的缘由，我们希望能和她直接见面。\
**Pioneer**: Hello, we're here to visit a member of your staff for, um, some private matters. If possible, we'd like to have a conversation with her in person.

职员的笑容略有僵硬。\
The staff member's smile is visibly forced.

**职员菲娜**：……没关系，你们可以先阅读这里的注意事项，并填写表格……噢！\
**Fiona**: Sure, please read the visitor's advisory here and fill out these forms. Ah!

手上一大叠密密麻麻的纸质文件，掉落在地。\
The dense tower of paper tumbles out of her hands, spilling out over the floor.

**职员菲娜**：咳，没问题，这些只是小事情。我很快就递给你们。\
**Fiona**: Um, so sorry, sir. Just let me pick these up.

男人弯下腰，热情地帮她捡拾着。\
J bends down to help her pick up the documents.

**J**：放松点儿，女士。我们只是来找我的妹妹……她是你们圣洛夫基金会的职员，现在呢……估摸还只是一位名不见经传的小家伙。\
**J**: Relax, Miss. It's nothing, just a short visit to my sister. She's like a clerk here or something, nothing important.

**J**：她的名字叫作保利娜·勒萨奇，您可以告诉她，她尊敬的哥哥前来拜访，请她务必腾出时间……\
**J**: Her name's Paulina Lesage. Just tell her that it's her brother, just popping by for a visit.

**职员菲娜**：……\
**Fiona**: ...

一场古怪的沉默降临。\
The receptionist falls silent and pale.

**职员菲娜**：保利娜·勒萨奇……嗯。您能告诉我，您的名字吗？\
**Fiona**: Paulina Lesage ... Could you tell me your name again?

**J**：乔，乔·布朗，您可以叫我J。\
**J**: It's Joe. Joe Brown. You can call me J.

职员焦急地在凌乱的纸张中翻翻找找，终于抽出了一张纸。\
Fiona anxiously shifts through the scattered papers.

她低头看向手中的名单，又抬起头审视着眼前人，如此反复几次——\
She looks down at the list in her hand, then up at the person in front of her, repeating the process several times—

仿佛在确认一件慎之又慎的事务。\
As if confirming something with delicate care.

接着，她毫不迟疑地站起身来。\
Then, she stands, and after regaining her composure, begins walking down the hall.

**职员菲娜**：请跟我来。\
**Fiona**: Follow me, please.

**职员菲娜**：我加入圣洛夫基金会的时候，认识的第一位职员就是保利娜女士……她的聪明伶俐远甚于我，所以也很快就开始担任重要的职务。\
**Fiona**: Ms. Paulina was one of the first people I met when I joined the Foundation. She was so talented, so incredible. It was no wonder they gave her all the big assignments.

**职员菲娜**：她带着骨子里的骄傲，可从不会怠慢别人，所以我喜欢询问她的意见。\
**Fiona**: I could always tell she was very proud, but not in an arrogant way. She never turned her back on people. I always knew I could turn to her for advice.

他们向着走廊的尽头走去。\
They walk to the end of the corridor.

身旁的职员行色匆匆，但每张脸都若隐若现着笑容，仿佛这是节前的最后一个工作日。\
As the staff members move about their work, there is a spirit in the air, light—almost joyful—as if it were the day before a holiday.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：重塑……他们抱头鼠窜，连地窖里的物资都顾不上，你猜他们还能撑多久？\
**Foundation Staff I**: Haha, it's the first time that we swept Manus that badly. They even forgot the rest of their supplies in the basement. What are they gonna do without those?

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：而且我们尚有余力，听说……“剃刀”小队已经开始追查基金会失踪的那批重要资产了……\
**Foundation Staff I**: Now that we have some spare manpower to chase after them, I heard that team "Razor" started searching for the Foundation's lost assets.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：这可是头一回，我们能重拾旧案。\
**Foundation Staff I**: After all this time, we're finally back on the trail.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：我不知道，朋友……虽然这是个好消息，但那些新闻也闹得太沸沸扬扬了，有不少人得意过了头，擅自离开基金会，把舆论搞得乱糟糟的……\
**Foundation Staff II**: I don't know, man. Good as it seems to be. I'm worried the news is getting out of control! Now rumors are spreading everywhere. It could get dangerous!

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：不然上头也不会把我们从总部调过来，跟着伯纳德先生，去解决这些层出不穷的“问题”了……\
**Foundation Staff II**: Otherwise, why would we have been assigned here with Mr. Bernard to get to the bottom of this?

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：嘘——小声点儿。\
**Foundation Staff I**: Shh, zip it.

**职员菲娜**：咳咳……\
**Fiona**: Ahem.

门口攀谈的人发现了陌生的访客，连忙躲开目光，作鸟兽散了。\
The people chatting by the door take notice of the unfamiliar visitors, shifting their gaze as they make way.

**J**：你们这里是发生了什么天大的好事？每个人脸上都乐呵呵的，跟一群收到小费的服务员似的。\
**J**: What, you guys having a party or something? Never seen an office so ... "smiley."

**先驱者**：我喜欢这股阳光的劲儿，百货大厦的男孩女孩们都是这副面孔……而且一般来说，他们也会给别人带来好消息。\
**Pioneer**: Feels like a sales day at the mall, all those eager girls and boys running past the window. A mood like this usually comes with good news.

**职员菲娜**：还请不要在意这些人的话，他们私底下的讨论并不代表基金会的共识，也可能会误导你们……\
**Fiona**: Please don't pay them any mind. They're, uh, just chit-chatting, doesn't really mean anything. It might mislead you even.

她从口袋中拿出钥匙，插入门扇的锁孔。\
She takes a key from her pocket and inserts it into the lock.

可一瞬间，她没有转动把手——只是恍惚地站在那里，似乎有些抵触。\
But she doesn't turn the handle. Her hand rests on it reluctantly.

**职员菲娜**：呼……\
**Fiona**: *panting*

**职员菲娜**：请跟紧我，先生们。\
**Fiona**: Gentlemen, come in, please.

由近至远，一束束灯光从头顶降临。\
Beams of harsh light descend from above, stretching near to far.

这是一个空旷而寂静的空间。\
The space is vast and silent.

**职员菲娜**：您或许不知道，此前，我们经历了数百场无功而返的实验，白白耗费了时间与资源，像无头苍蝇，徘徊在无根无据的迷宫之中。\
**Fiona**: Despite all the smiles, it hasn't been easy for us recently. Our time and resources have been stretched thin. We've suffered a lot of losses.

**职员菲娜**：如今就算我站在这里，也总会神情恍惚。\
**Fiona**: It still feels a little unreal that we're still standing.

**职员菲娜**：人们前仆后继，奉出了他们最珍贵的东西，才得以达到如今这个崭新的局面。\
**Fiona**: A lot of good people sacrificed everything they had to get us where we are.

无数个透明的匣子，摆放在墙柜之中，邮票大小的照片贴在上面。\
The walls are lined with transparent cabinets, each marked by a stamp-sized photo.

照片旁的标签编号，数字犹如计时器般，增加、进位——\
Next to the photos, the label numbers increase like a timer, progressing digit by digit.

由零到一，由一到零，循环往复……\
The numbers grow, ticking over from tens to hundreds and further.

**职员菲娜**：咳咳……抱歉，我似乎说了一些令你们困惑的话。\
**Fiona**: Ahem. Excuse me, I suppose that's also just idle chit-chat. Maybe I don't know any more than they do.

**职员菲娜**：我只是想说……保利娜是我见过的最优秀的职员——而她的家人有权知道这些。\
**Fiona**: I only just wanted to say, since you're family, that Ms. Paulina was one of the best people I've ever met, an asset to everyone here at the Foundation.

她停住了脚步，站在一面毫不起眼的墙柜前。\
She stops before yet another column of cabinets, no different from the many behind and in front of them.

如果不是那些照片，不会有任何一个人觉察出这些墙柜的区别。\
Each one the same as every other, except for the photo.

**职员菲娜**：先生们——圣洛夫基金会所有的殉职人员……都在这里。\
**Fiona**: Gentlemen, this is where the remains of all those that died in the service of the St. Pavlov Foundation are kept in memorial.

**职员菲娜**：而保利娜……就在你们眼前。\
**Fiona**: I'm so sorry that I have to be the one t-to tell you, but, Paulina is here, too.

不是墓碑，亦不是棺柩，只是一只又窄又小的透明匣子。\
There is no grave, no coffin or epitaph. Just a transparent cabinet to serve as her headstone.

那样稀松平常，与小女孩藏着秘密的宝箱并没有不同，就好像只是一出玩笑。\
A plain and ordinary box, void of any sentiment.

**J**：……\
**J**: ...

**J**：……呃。\
**J**: Umm ...

**J**：你明白你在说什么吗，女士？\
**J**: You better know what you're saying, Miss.

他不想认出那件东西——但他比任何人都清楚，他已经看见了。\
He pretends not to see it, but he knows exactly what is there.

那抹，简单又熟悉的蓝丝带。\
That unmistakably familiar blue ribbon.

**先驱者**：……呃，女士，能请你给我们一些独处的空间吗？\
**Pioneer**: I'm sorry, Fiona, dear. Would you mind giving us a moment of privacy?

**职员菲娜**：……我在外面等候各位。\
**Fiona**: I'll be waiting outside.

她的身影渐趋渐远，直到消失不见。\
Her figure grows more and more distant, receding back through the space until vanishes altogether.

……\
...

**先驱者**：伙计，告诉我，你在想什么？\
**Pioneer**: J, are you going to be alright?

**先驱者**：……\
**Pioneer**: ...

**先驱者**：J，告诉我！我能为你做些什么……需要我把匣子打开吗？\
**Pioneer**: Talk to me, J! Is there anything I can do for you? Maybe we can take a look, just to be sure.

**J**：不，不要，什么也不要做，该死的，你什么也不要做！\
**J**: No, don't-don't do anything. Damn it! Don't you f**king do a damn thing!

他在努力克制。\
He struggles against himself, failing to hold himself back.

**J**：她怎么可能，怎么可能待在那么小、那么小一个匣子里……？！\
**J**: How can all that someone is, was, be in a box like this? It's so small?!

**J**：我发誓，他们在糊弄我——\
**J**: This is some kind of sick joke!

**先驱者**：J！\
**Pioneer**: J!

**先驱者**：冷静一些！！！\
**Pioneer**: Easy, J. Easy.

先驱者紧紧抓住他的臂膀，双眼直视着他。\
Pioneer grips his arm tightly, staring directly at him.

那是一段沉默、凝滞的时间。\
The atmosphere is filled with heavy, unspoken tension.

直到J终于抬起眼，与他对视。\
Until J lifts his gaze to meet the mannequin's own.

**先驱者**：……呆在这儿，让我去核对，把照片给我。\
**Pioneer**: Do you have her photo? You stay here. I'll go double-check.

J颤抖着手，从兜里掏出了那张皱巴巴的旧合影。\
With trembling hands, J pulls out the crumpled old photograph from his pocket.

**先驱者**：……呼。\
**Pioneer**: *deep breath*

他深呼一口气，拿着合影，比对着匣子上的相片。\
He holds the photograph, comparing it closely to the one on the box.

讶异瞬间爬上了他的脸。\
Then a strange look of astonishment washes over him.

**先驱者**：J……J！\
**Pioneer**: J ... J!

**先驱者**：这是怎么一回事？过来！伙计，站起来看看！\
**Pioneer**: ... This can't be right. Come here, J. You need to take a look at this!

地上的男人行尸走肉般地走了过去，紧接着——\
J walks toward him like a zombie, and then—

**J**：她们的脸……他们在搞什么？\
**J**: Wait, this? What the heck?

**J**：这根本就不是同一个人？！\
**J**: This isn't Paulina?!

仿若有一盏灯突然打从他的脑袋旁亮起。\
It is as if a light suddenly flickers on over his head.

**J**：你知道吗？我总算是弄明白了！这或许该死的就是一场骗局！那个门外的家伙根本就不想让咱们拜访保利娜！\
**J**: So, then, what? This was all some kind of bulls**t?! That woman out there just decided to mess with my mind? Or did she not want us to see Paulina?

**先驱者**：……也许是他们贴错了照片？\
**Pioneer**: Maybe they got the photo wrong?

**J**：不，我现在看清楚了，瞧瞧那只手上的戒指！我从没听过保利娜在什么时候订了婚！\
**J**: No, no. Look at that ring on her finger! Polly wasn't married. She couldn't be. She would have told me.

**J**：保利娜根本不想见我！所以才拜托她的朋友演了这么一出戏，却没想到她露出了个大马脚。\
**J**: Unless, she just doesn't wanna see me at all. So maybe she put her friend up to all of this, but this, this just gives her away!

**J**：她以前跟我说过，就算死在外面也不跟我回去。\
**J**: Polly said it herself: She'd rather die than stay with me and never live at all. I knew then she'd never look back.

**J**：天呐，太愚蠢了。我就不该到这儿来。\
**J**: Man, this was stupid! Never should've let you talk me into coming here.

**先驱者**：噢，我见过很多不对付的兄妹，他们顶多也就是彼此互踹一脚，打个小报告争宠。但你们，你们的关系可真是糟糕到了一个地步……\
**Pioneer**: I know that sometimes brothers and sisters don't get along. But I thought that only meant little fights, quarrels over toys. This is something much worse.

**J**：我们得趁早离开这地方……呃，我一想到保利娜正在某个地方盯着我们的一举一动，捧腹大笑，就恨不得把这儿掀个底儿朝天。\
**J**: We're leaving. Now. Ugh, I can't stand the idea that she's just looking at me through a monitor, maybe even laughing at her pathetic loser brother. Get me out of here before I turn this place upside down!

……\
...

**职员菲娜**：J先生，您感到好一些了吗？\
**Fiona**: I apologize. I'm sure this loss must feel ...

男人掩面而泣，先驱者拍着他的肩膀，就仿佛安慰一位丧夫的妻子。\
J hides his face, making an exaggerated show of his tears, while Pioneer gently pats his shoulder.

**J**：呜呜呜……抱歉，我的泪都快流干了，这打击实在是，让我痛彻心扉。\
**J**: *sob* Mhmm. Such heart-wrenching news. I'm crying my eyes out.

他带着哭腔一颤一颤，就差一条丝绸手帕给他拭去不存在的眼泪。\
It is an oddly captivating performance. If Haight Street didn't work out, perhaps he ought to head to Hollywood.

**先驱者**：但如今尘埃落定，我们就不便在这里打搅你们的工作了……J，我们走吧。\
**Pioneer**: Oh. But there's nothing we can do now. Sorry for bothering you. We'll be on our way out now. Let's go, J.

他们互相搀扶着，谁见了也得心碎。\
Propped up on one of the mannequin's shoulder, the heartbreaking act is nearly flawless.

**职员菲娜**：请等等……先生们，你们还需要做个访客登记。\
**Fiona**: Please wait, gentlemen, you need to fill the visitor's log form first.

**职员菲娜**：以及……我找找……唔，应该就是这个！\
**Fiona**: And, let me see, this one.

她抽出一张又黄又旧的纸张。\
She pulls out a yellowed and worn piece of paper.

**职员菲娜**：请您在这上面签下作为唯一家属的您的名字……\
**Fiona**: Please, sign your name here as her next of kin.

**J**：殉职人员家属……同意书？这是什么意思？\
**J**: Consent form ... to document that I've confirmed the death of a Foundation staff member ... What is this?

他诧异地抬起头，却突然想到脸上没有涟涟泪水，于是又低了回去。\
He looks up with disdain, catching himself as he remembers his supposedly weeping face is dry, and buries it back down again.

**J**：咳、咳……呜，为什么还要让我签字？您没看见，我已经无法再承受更多的打击了吗？\
**J**: Why do I have to sign? Don't you understand I can't take any more of this?

**职员菲娜**：还请您谅解，这是我们的工作……我们得确认那些殉职的职员得到了家属的认领，并依此给您发放一笔抚恤金……\
**Fiona**: I'm sorry, but please bear with me. I thought we might confirm her belongings with you. It's standard policy, though usually within the foundation. Then I could ask my superiors. Maybe they'd let you take these home.

**职员菲娜**：请在这里签下您的姓名与地址……\
**Fiona**: Here, I'll just need your name and address.

**J**：什么……？你们的玩笑太过界了，女士。\
**J**: What? That's just sick, Miss.

他的表情骤变，像吃了一个霉果子。\
His expression changes abruptly, rising up into a bitter scowl.

**J**：你的意思是让我为了一叠钞票，签署一份死亡证明？证明我的妹妹为了你们所谓的崇高理想死在了半途之中——即便她自打娘胎起就不长那样！\
**J**: You're really asking me to sign some papers? For what? So you can hand me off some old junk and pretend this never happened? You think that's enough to get me to stop asking questions? Where is she?!?

**J**：伙计，我们的灵魂可还没被打折抛售！\
**J**: Did you really think it would be this easy, sis? That I didn't care?

他拽住先驱者，头也不回地离开了。\
He grabs Pioneer and runs off without looking back.

**职员菲娜**：先生——先生！\
**Fiona**: Sir! SIR!

**职员菲娜**：……\
**Fiona**: ...

**职员菲娜**：……安保人员，拦住那两位没有登记的先生，他们还没签署保密协议！\
**Fiona**: Security, stop those two gentlemen! They haven't signed the confidentiality agreement!

还没等安保人员反应，他们已经窜进了沙丁鱼般的人潮中。\
Before security can react, the duo have already escaped into the crowd.

**J**：借过、借过，朋友们，把你们高贵的手肘抬回去！\
**J**: 'Scuse me! 'Scuse me! Man, move your ass or get moved!

他们犹如裹了油的野猫，滑溜溜地窜过熙熙攘攘的职员。\
They dart through the bustling halls, dodging employees with cat-like grace.

**先驱者**：他们是怎么一回事？就好像我们是没付钱的顾客一样，怎么一个个全扑上来了？！\
**Pioneer**: What's going on? They're after us like we are trying to ditch a bill for dinner.

**J**：该死……我跟你说过了，这帮政府的混蛋都一个样儿，谁不服他们那可笑的说辞，谁的脑袋就会开瓢！\
**J**: Told you these Foundation creeps are all the same! Soon as you don't buy what they're selling, they start trying to get you shot!

**J**：总之，我宁愿让我妹妹，亲自站在我眼前告诉我“滚远点，J”，也绝不会同意保利娜这个跟我断绝关系的法子！\
**J**: If she wants to cut me loose, then she can damn well say it to my face, but not like this, not this bulls**t!

他们很快离开了走廊。\
They wind through the twisting corridors, until at last they find an exit and dive through.

走廊上一阵不安的骚动……人们聚拢，涌动。\
There is a wave of uneasy commotion in the hallway as people gathered in a throng.

一位高大的男人穿过人群，人们肃静了。\
A tall man moves through the crowd. As he passes, the throng goes silent.

**伯纳德**：发生什么事了，菲娜？\
**Bernard**: Fiona, can you tell me what happened here?

## FT-04 新客人 / A New Guest

床铺上是被叠得整整齐齐的衣服，行李箱则是半张开嘴的状态。\
Neatly stacked clothes lie on the bed, the suitcase open and empty.

时近出发的前夜，她在屋子里来回转悠、收拾。\
On the eve of her departure, she paces back and forth in the room, tidying as she goes.

**玛蒂尔达**：77号公路……唔，《UTTU》的编辑怎么爱在那种偏僻的地方活动，真令人捉摸不透……他们真的知道有关兀尔德的消息吗？\
**Matilda**: Route 77 ... Hmm, I don't understand. Why would the editor of UTTU visit such a desolate place? What could this mean about Urd?

**玛蒂尔达**：不管如何，至少我还可以顺便去拜访妈妈一趟，哼哼。\
**Matilda**: Alright then, at least I can drop by and visit Mama. Humph.

**玛蒂尔达**：妈妈这次肯定会大吃一惊，伟大的玛蒂尔达如今取得的成就，能令所有家族成员都为之骄傲！\
**Matilda**: That will most certainly be a surprise! What their Matilda has achieved will make the whole family proud!

**玛蒂尔达**：“瞧瞧是谁的宝贝女儿当上了圣洛夫基金会的特派调查员？布翁尼家族的荣光，如今传到了绝顶聪明的玛蒂尔达手里！”\
**Matilda**: "My daughter, my Matilda, a special investigator for the St. Pavlov Foundation! Now little Matilda adds another star to the Bouanich family line!"

**玛蒂尔达**：哼哼♫♪♬～\
**Matilda**: *humming*

“咚咚咚——”\
"Knock, knock, knock ..."

敲门声不合时宜地传来。\
The sound of knocking comes at an inconvenient time.

**小队成员Ⅰ**：玛蒂尔达小姐，能请您出来一下吗？我们的任务，被取消了……\
**Team Member I**: Ms. Bouanich, a moment of your time? Unfortunately, it seems our mission has been canceled.

**玛蒂尔达**：什么？发生了什么？\
**Matilda**: Canceled? Why?

**小队成员Ⅰ**：您或许已经听说了关于菲娜的事情……\
**Team Member I**: You may have heard what Fiona did.

**玛蒂尔达**：嗯……外面的动静不小，我听说她由于刚刚出任登记员，对我们接待神秘学家的流程尚且不太熟悉，所以……\
**Matilda**: Well, I had heard the chatter about it certainly, but she only just started as a receptionist. It is no matter if she is a little unfamiliar with the processes and ...

**小队成员Ⅰ**：是啊，她记错了规定，误将“暴雨”后早已取消的《殉职家属探访规定》，套用在了两位不明就里的拜访者身上。\
**Team Member I**: Per regulations since the first "Storm," families of the deceased employees are no longer informed of their deaths, but she made a mistake, or forgot.

**小队成员Ⅰ**：那两位神秘学家，在没有签署任何保密条约的情况下逃出了圣洛夫基金会。\
**Team Member I**: And the two arcanists she received earlier got away from her near the memorial hall. They didn't even fill out the proper forms.

**玛蒂尔达**：太糟糕了。这是一起相当严重的情报泄露事故……\
**Matilda**: Ah, not good. That could indeed represent a serious intelligence leak.

**小队成员Ⅰ**：嗯，鉴于这个年代的信息传播速率，伯纳德先生认为……我们迫切需要稳定舆论，尤其是对那些记者与媒体。\
**Team Member I**: And Mr. Bernard asked that we get ahead of the narrative, before it gets to the press, given how fast the news spreads in this day and age.

**小队成员Ⅰ**：为了防止情报泄露范围进一步扩大，我们需要尽快找到那两名拜访者。\
**Team Member I**: New orders are for us to find these two visitors and prevent the information from further spreading.

**玛蒂尔达**：我们？\
**Matilda**: Us?

**玛蒂尔达**：——我明白了。也就是说，追踪《UTTU》编辑的任务将会分派给其他调查员……\
**Matilda**: Of course. So then, our present task tracking down the editor of UTTU will be reassigned to some other team.

**小队成员Ⅰ**：是的，因为根据信息，那两位逃跑的神秘学家……\
**Team Member I**: Correct, ma'am. Tracking down these two arcanists was given top priority, and ...

**小队成员Ⅰ**：曾与我们打过照面。\
**Team Member I**: Those two were the same ones you ran into earlier today.

占卜师、魔药学家……诸多神秘学家齐聚在一起，构成了这场盛大的集市。\
Fortune-tellers, alchemists, and arcanists of all stripes gathered together, creating a sprawling marketplace.

从魔精栓绳到炼金术珍本，再到琳琅满目的药草……商品眼花缭乱，往来的游客络绎不绝。\
From magic-infused cords to rare alchemical texts, and a dazzling array of herbs. Its goods have attracted a steady and constant stream of visitors.

**集会演说家**：朋友们，经过“谐波汇聚运动”之后，天启的预言数次破灭，我们目睹了末世论的荒谬，并发现世间除了灵性信仰与科学理性——尚存有第三种共处的真相。\
**Public Speaker**: My friends, after the Harmonic Convergence, we discovered the failure of prophecy and eschatology, and the new possibilities of coexistence between the faith in pneuma and science!

**集会演说家**：谁言神明仅此一位，谁言神明已死？朋友们，我们是时候放下信仰之间的争端，摒弃高高在上的神明，而相信我们本为一体，神即是你，神也即我……\
**Public Speaker**: They claim there is one god, and god is dead. But is that so? Friends, it's time to abandon the disputes of religions, and to know that we are one. God is you, god is me.

演说家在熙来攘往的人群中间，自顾自地宣讲着，对无人驻足与倾听毫不在意。\
In the midst of the bustling crowd, a speaker gives a lecture out to no one in particular, seemingly unconcerned if anyone is listening at all.

**玛蒂尔达**：根据可靠的情报，那两个在基金会捣乱的家伙，正躲在一位名叫环状水星的能量疗愈师的帐篷里……\
**Matilda**: We've got information that our escaped visitors have gone into hiding with an energy healer called Mercuria.

**玛蒂尔达**：这种喧闹的地方不宜进行大规模的行动，我们要尽量悄无声息一些。\
**Matilda**: It's crowded here. I'd rather not attract attention to ourselves, so keep your heads down.

帐篷孤零零地躲在角落里，仿佛是一块水流中的顽石，将喧闹隔绝与外。\
A solitary tent stands out in the corner, a refuge from the bustling crowd.

**小队成员Ⅰ**：这个帐篷仿佛是临时拼凑的……连木头招牌都被吹翻了，它有些不对劲——我几乎感知不到任何术法的波动。\
**Team Member I**: Some kind of temporary tent. And a sign lying on the ground. Something's not right. I barely sense any arcane fluctuations here.

**小队成员Ⅱ**：这……会不会是一出陷阱？玛蒂尔达小姐。\
**Team Member II**: Could it be a trap?

**小队成员Ⅱ**：这个集会里到处都是不在登记名册里的神秘学家，我们无法甄别其中有哪些人是危险分子，况且其中还有不少人类游客……\
**Team Member II**: This market is filled with unregistered arcanists, not to mention the human tourists. There are sure to be dangerous ones among them.

**玛蒂尔达**：嘘……！\
**Matilda**: Shh!

敏锐的调查员似乎听到了近乎呢喃的声音。\
With her sharp ears, Matilda notices a faint whispering sound emanating from inside the tent.

**？？？**：我也许不该过来……“启明会”的人会把我切成碎片，再丢进猪圈——\
**???**: I shouldn't have come. They're gonna slice me up and feed me to the pigs!

帐篷内传出男人的啼哭，声音浑厚、痛苦，但不属于他们所调查的任何人。\
The deep, painful cries of a man break the quiet of the moment. Irrelevant though it may be, it draws the investigator in.

女孩轻抬脚步，犹如靠近一只盘旋沉睡的蟒蛇。\
The girl shifts her feet cautiously, as if approaching a sleeping, coiled python.

她悄悄揭开帐篷的一角，凑上了眼睛。\
She delicately lifts a corner of the tent's opening and peers inside.

**？？？**：那些猪会啃掉我的脑袋，连渣儿都不剩……他们就是这样对待所谓“启明会”的叛徒的，就是这样……\
**???**: Pigs will eat everything, all the bones, your head, not a hair left. That's how they treat traitors!

**？？？**：到时候就连老头子也救不了我……他不会站我这边，他不会的……\
**???**: Pops won't save me then. He won't stand at my side. No.

女孩以手覆上他颤抖着祈祷状的双手，犹如抚慰一只受伤的狼犬。\
A mysterious girl places her hand over the hulking man's trembling hands.

**环状水星**：但你还是过来了，杰洛先生。即便双脚发软、打颤，你还是选择前来寻求一个答案。\
**Mercuria**: But here you are, Mr. Gio, shivering like a new leaf. Because you're ready for an answer.

**环状水星**：——关于你自身的答案。\
**Mercuria**: The answer to yourself.

她嗅了嗅他周围的空气。\
She sniffs the air around him.

**环状水星**：还有，你这次带来了奇怪的味道，以及一股浑浊的能量……它很微弱，向来只属于病入膏肓者。\
**Mercuria**: Hmm. You brought a strange smell with you, and a weak, faltering energy, like that of someone gravely ill.

**环状水星**：你……最近常去医院吗？\
**Mercuria**: Have you been to any hospitals?

**杰洛**：不，我最近一直跟随着莱格斯，并且只和活人打交道……我们向来拒绝任何瘾君子和染病的倒霉鬼。\
**Gio**: No, just following Legers. Nowadays, only visits we have are with the living or the dead ones, not much in between. We don't deal with addicts or sick dogs.

**杰洛**：啊！这不重要，我知道你又想趁机兜售一些疗愈的香料，但我对那些没有兴趣……如你所说，我只是为了寻求自身的答案而来！\
**Gio**: Wait, shut it. Before you start, I'm not buying any of your goddamn spices or candles! I'm just here for an answer.

**杰洛**：关于那团焚毁屋子的火苗，将我的妻子、孩子……你到底是为什么知道？这说不通，这说不通！\
**Gio**: How did you know about the fire that took my family? How?

**杰洛**：你是吉普赛人的祭司吗？你是专门窥梦的占卜师吗？你得回答我，你得回答我！\
**Gio**: Are you some kind of psychic? Or a prophet? Tell me! TELL ME!

他甩开手，发疯似地啃咬着手指。\
He jerks his hands away, only to begin gnawing at his nails.

**杰洛**：不，不对……我不该站在这里，我该把你的头割下来，送给老头子……这样我在这里的原因就能够解释了。\
**Gio**: No, no. I shouldn't have come here, unless ... Maybe I chop off your pretty little head and give it to him. That'd be my excuse.

几乎只有一瞬，匕首抵在女孩的喉咙上。\
In an instant, he presses the dagger against the girl's throat.

**玛蒂尔达**：……！\
**Matilda**: ...!

偷窥者情不自禁要冲上前去。\
Matilda fights the urge to rush forward to help.

“呲。”——地面上的蜡烛瞬间熄灭。\
"Whoosh."—The candle illuminating the room is snuffed out.

**环状水星**：先生，你知道在你手中的是什么吗？——一把小刀，廉价却实用的商品？一把割喉的利器，铲除异己的工具？\
**Mercuria**: What have you got? What do you see in your hand? Is it a knife for my throat or a diamond-covered key?

**杰洛**：闭嘴，别再说那些神神叨叨的话！你只不过是火焰底下幸存的女巫，是一个骗子！\
**Gio**: Shut up! Stop babbling! You're just a witch who survived her burning, a liar!

他的手在颤抖。\
His hand trembles again.

**环状水星**：请不要颤抖，杰洛先生——盯着它，盯着由你的火焰所淬出的匕首。\
**Mercuria**: Breathe, slow and true. Look at it again. This is a dagger forged in your own dark flame.

他的眼睛凝视着匕首，就像第一次见到它一般。\
He looks at the dagger, as if seeing it through new eyes.

**环状水星**：只有当我们长久注视一件事物，事物“解释”的外壳才会逐渐脱落……\
**Mercuria**: Everything has a shell of "meaning." But hold your gaze on it, and it all strips away.

**环状水星**：令你浮想联翩的文字将只是几抹涂画，匕首也只是锻造之下的金属物，请抓住这种“没有意义”的感觉。\
**Mercuria**: Until those words become strokes of black, and that dagger becomes a cold sheet of metal.

香炉裹挟着魔药的气味，袅袅升起，萦绕着两人。\
Her incense burner releases a puff of strong scented potion into the air.

匕首转瞬间失去形体，化成熊熊燃烧的火焰。\
All at once, the dagger transforms into a blazing fire.

它犹如嘶嘶吐信的毒蛇，爬上男人惊恐的脸庞。\
It slithers up the man's arm, toward his face, roiling and coiling like a snake.

**杰洛**：呃……啊！\
**Gio**: Urgh! AHH!

**玛蒂尔达**：这……这是怎么回事？！\
**Matilda**: W-what's going on?!

**环状水星**：意义只是黏在鞋底的口香糖，当你让它脱落，你的行走将不再受到束缚，你也便不再受到意义的蛊惑——事物会显现出原初的面貌。\
**Mercuria**: "Meaning" is a cage. Cast off its shackles, and nature reveals itself to us.

**环状水星**：别害怕，抓住脱落的感受……跟我一起闭上眼睛。\
**Mercuria**: Don't be afraid. Hold that feeling. Now close your eyes with me.

你看见了吗？在那黑暗的中央，正有一扇门矗立于此。\
Do you see it? A door surrounded by darkness.

**杰洛**：我看见了，它……在发抖，它在害怕我的靠近。\
**Gio**: Yes. The door is shaking, like something's behind it. No, it's scared.

不要直视它，告诉我，它将通向什么地方？\
Don't try to picture it. Take away the shell. Just tell me by the impression: Where does it lead you?

**杰洛**：那扇门，它通向我的——家？\
**Gio**: It goes home?

**杰洛**：是火光，它、它烧起来了！\
**Gio**: Fire! The door's on fire!

**杰洛**：我听见了喊叫……它通向那座熊熊燃烧的屋子……里面是我的妻子萨菲娜，以及尚在襁褓中的孩子……不、不！求求你，救救他们，请救救他们！\
**Gio**: No, I-I don't wanna go there. Not there. Someone's screaming. Savina! My-my baby! No, no! Help them! Help them, please!

**环状水星**：请冷静！杰洛先生，请环顾四周，有谁跟你在一起？\
**Mercuria**: That's over now. Look around. Who is with you?

**杰洛**：……是老头子，以及另一群人，他们手执火把与狗链，站在那儿……\
**Gio**: Pops and others. They're standing there, with torches and chains.

**环状水星**：他们是谁？\
**Mercuria**: Who are the "others"?

**杰洛**：我不知道，我不知道……他们个个都被一双手蒙住了眼睛。\
**Gio**: I don't know. I don't know. Their eyes are covered by hands.

**杰洛**：不对，那不是手……那是他们所佩戴的面具！\
**Gio**: No, not hands. Those are hand-shaped masks!

**玛蒂尔达**：是重塑之手？！\
**Matilda**: Manus Vindictae?!

一束光忽然从头顶照射而下，景象恍然消失。\
A beam of light breaks in from above, expelling the smoke and darkness of the scene.

蜡烛重燃，现实回到了所有人眼前。\
The extinguished candle catches flame once more, and all present return to reality.

**J**：喔，这是从哪里来的丫头？你妈妈从没教你别擅自揭开别人的门帘吗……？\
**J**: Hey, who's this girl? Didn't your mom teach you not to spy on people?

一只手从身后，将恍惚中的女孩提溜了起来。\
A hand stretches from behind and lifts the investigator up to her feet.

**玛蒂尔达**：你……！\
**Matilda**: You!

身后传来了急匆匆的脚步声，两位职员及时赶了过来。\
Behind them, urgent footsteps reach the scene.

**小队成员Ⅰ**：玛蒂尔达小姐！\
**Team Member I**: Ms. Bouanich!

**J**：等等，你是……之前基金会的那个丫头？！糟糕——！\
**J**: Dammit, you're the girl from the Foundation?! Ain't that just my luck!

J像被蜜蜂蛰了似的，把这块烫手的山芋给甩了出去。\
J flings the girl from his hand like a hot potato.

**玛蒂尔达**：抓住他！\
**Matilda**: Catch him!

## FT-05 审讯节目 / "Interrogation"

“哐当——”\
"Bang—!"

**J**：呃……！\
**J**: Urgh!

他单膝跪在地上，抬起被包裹的剑状物，一道道术法不停撞击其上，令他的身躯节节后退。\
He falls to one knee, lifting the long-wrapped shaft that has been on his back, as spells continue to strike him, forcing him into a step-by-step retreat.

**小队成员Ⅰ**：J先生，请你配合我们的调查……我们并不打算伤害你或你的同伴，如若你继续这样反抗下去，我们将不得已采用更为强硬的手段。\
**Team Member I**: Mr. Brown, we have need of your cooperation. We do not wanna hurt you or your friends, but should you continue to resist, we'll be forced to take necessary action.

**玛蒂尔达**：难以置信，真是粗鲁的家伙……作为神秘学家，回击手段竟然全是贴身肉搏。\
**Matilda**: Unbelievable, so rude! Even as an arcanist, all he does is this vulgar hand-to-hand combat.

**玛蒂尔达**：而且还背着那样一把碍手碍脚的东西，真让人搞不懂。\
**Matilda**: Still, that long stick he carries most certainly isn't a toy.

**玛蒂尔达**：如果你乖乖配合，玛蒂尔达可以考虑考虑在调查报告中降低对你的风险评级……\
**Matilda**: Ahem. Gentlemen, if you would be willing to come quietly and play nice, I will consider lowering your risk rating in our report.

她一边劝说着，一边找寻着之前透露出重塑之手情报的男人。\
She tries to reason with them, keeping in mind her desire to search for the man who mentioned the Manus Vindictae.

先前持着匕首的男人已不知所踪，那把匕首正安然无恙地躺在地上——没有火焰的痕迹。\
But he is already gone, and the dagger lies undamaged on the ground.

两名职员俯低了身子，一步步靠近这头气喘吁吁的猎物。\
Her teammates gain ground on the would-be warrior, who has sunken to his knees.

**J**：咳、咳……我得说……我也不想搞到这个地步，朋友们，我也希望我能乖乖求饶。\
**J**: *coughs* I gotta say sometimes I wish I could take a knee and surrender.

**J**：但，呸……\
**J**: But ... *spit*

一口带着鲜血的唾沫被吐在地上。\
He smiles through bloodied teeth.

**J**：唉，可惜我从小到大，肚子挨了不少拳头，也还没学会举起双手——这项了不起的技巧。\
**J**: Sadly, even after all those hard-knock lessons, I never learned once how to raise the white flag.

手伸向怀中，正准备握住那把小巧又敏捷的博伊刀的刀柄——\
He reaches into his pocket, ready to grasp the handle of his small and agile Bowie knife.

**环状水星**：J……放下它，战争已经结束了。\
**Mercuria**: Put it down, J. Your fight is over.

**小队成员Ⅰ**：？！\
**Team Member I**: ?!

**小队成员Ⅰ**：这……这是曼德拉药草，是什么时候……？快遮住口鼻！\
**Team Member I**: This-This is the smoke of burning Mandrake! Cover your nose and your mouth!

**小队成员Ⅱ**：屏住呼吸，离远一些，玛蒂尔……达，小姐……\
**Team Member II**: Ms. Bouanich, hold your breath. Stay away from the smoke.

宛如中了麻醉的大象，他们腿脚一软，倒在了地上。\
But the smoke is already too thick. One by one, they give way, collapsing harmlessly to the ground.

**玛蒂尔达**：糟了……！\
**Matilda**: Oh, no!

局势转眼间变化。\
The situation changes in the blink of an eye.

她不禁后退了一步，却发现帐篷已紧紧闭上。\
She moves automatically, falling back to the entrance, only to find that the tent has been shut tight.

**玛蒂尔达**：唔……\
**Matilda**: Umm!

**J**：哼……\
**J**: Hmph.

被绑住的女孩与“绑匪”，像是两只争抢栗子的松鼠，不屑一顾地瞅着彼此。\
The bound girl and her "kidnapper" look at each other with disdain, like two squirrels fighting over a chestnut.

**玛蒂尔达**：你们要知道，绑架基金会调查员与违抗调查，是非常严重的罪行……尤其是你们绑架的还是圣洛夫基金会最优秀的骨干成员——玛蒂尔达·布翁尼小姐！\
**Matilda**: You should know that kidnapping a Foundation investigator and interfering with an official investigation is a serious crime, especially when you've kidnapped the one and only Matilda Bouanich, a pivotal figure in the St. Pavlov Foundation we're talking about!

**J**：什么优秀的骨干成员。一个没有经验的小家伙，刚好成了我们的漏网之鱼——这可不是什么光荣事迹。\
**J**: Pivotal, eh? Ha. A whiny little pup happens to stay standing from a little smoke. Yeah, I don't see anything worth being proud of.

他伸出手指，在女孩额头上“啪”地弹出了声儿。\
He extends a finger to give the girl's forehead a sharp flick.

作为第一个拷问用刑，相当适用。\
As the first approach to an interrogation, it proves surprisingly effective.

**玛蒂尔达**：喂！\
**Matilda**: Hey!

**玛蒂尔达**：给我停下，你这个无礼的家伙！这是严重的冒犯！\
**Matilda**: Stop it! This is rude and-and indecent!

**J**：告诉我，保利娜现在是不是还躲在基金会的某个小房间里，为了让我签署保密协议，才把你们派了过来？\
**J**: Tell me, did Paulina send you to ask us to sign this bogus confidentiality agreement? Let me guess. She's probably still hiding in the Foundation office, right? Too scared to see her own flesh and blood.

**玛蒂尔达**：你到底在说什么胡话？……我们根本没有理由那样做，我们过来是为了带你和那个假人回去，你们已经严重违反了《圣洛夫基金会访客协议》的保密守则！\
**Matilda**: What are you talking about? Who's hiding in our office? We're here to bring you and that mannequin back to the Foundation. This is a serious violation of the Visitor's Advisory!

**先驱者**：J，我想我们得换个问法——玛蒂尔达小姐，你有什么证据能够证明J的妹妹已经殉职？\
**Pioneer**: J, I think we should ask this another way: Ms. Bouanich, what proof do you have that Paulina Lesage is dead, as your receptionist claimed?

**先驱者**：你们先前所提供的照片与本人大相径庭，我们无法相信那些荒谬的证据。\
**Pioneer**: The photo on the box isn't hers, just some lookalike or airbrush job. So how can we believe anything else you say?

**玛蒂尔达**：……！\
**Matilda**: ...!

**玛蒂尔达**：你是说，你们认识的保利娜也是——\
**Matilda**: You're saying the Paulina you know isn't the same as the one in this photo?

**玛蒂尔达**：……\
**Matilda**: ...

眼前的人看似不羁，但眼神却格外关切。那是对至亲才会有的沉重的情绪。\
J seems so nonchalant, yet his eyes are filled with concern—a gravity reserved only for great love.

**玛蒂尔达**：可恶，怎么说才好……总之，请相信，我们绝对没有任何要欺瞒你们的理由。\
**Matilda**: How can I explain this to you? Please be assured that we have no reason to lie to you at this juncture.

**玛蒂尔达**：倒不如说，这一切本就不该让你们知道……\
**Matilda**: Actually, you shouldn't have found out about any of this in the first place.

她沉默了很久，似乎在思考当下要如何才表达得适当。\
She falls silent for a long time, pondering how to best express herself.

**玛蒂尔达**：我并不了解你们所认识的保利娜。但至少，曾经在基金会与我们共事过的保利娜，确实已经牺牲了。\
**Matilda**: Maybe, I'm not familiar with your Paulina. But I do know that there was a woman at St. Pavlov's named "Paulina Lesage," and I know that she died.

**玛蒂尔达**：至于照片与本人不符的问题，总部正在着手调查同类事件——但解开这个谜团，还需要一段漫长的时间。\
**Matilda**: As far as the claims of "different photos, mementos," it's complicated, and there is, eh, little I can say freely, but headquarters is working on it and many other similar cases.

**玛蒂尔达**：我的职级并不足以知晓全貌……而且因为保密的必要，玛蒂尔达不能透露任何消息给你们。\
**Matilda**: I don't have the kind of clearance to know what's really going on, and even if I did, I couldn't tell you, for everyone's safety.

那一双双盯着她的眼睛，没有任何波澜。\
He looks entirely unmoved.

**J**：哈……我懂了。这个调查员也只是个被蒙在鼓里、一无所知的小家伙。\
**J**: Ha. So our little prize investigator is also in the dark.

**J**：伙计，咱们还是留点力气去把他们打包送回圣洛夫基金会大门口吧。\
**J**: Maybe we can just go ahead and jot all these questions down and send them back to the Foundation.

**J**：正好让过路人都看看基金会的风采！\
**J**: Or maybe we set up shop here, just let any old passerby take a good look at them!

他将椅子拎起来——\
He lifts the chair.

**玛蒂尔达**：啊，喂，等等，再等一等！！！\
**Matilda**: Hey, wait! Wait a second!

“人质”陷入了思索。片刻，她不情不愿地抬起了头。\
After a moment, the "hostage" looks up reluctantly.

**玛蒂尔达**：那么，只要我证明了这位女士已经真的牺牲……\
**Matilda**: I-If I could prove this Paulina of yours is, in fact, deceased ...

**玛蒂尔达**：你们就愿意乖乖跟我回去，对么？\
**Matilda**: Then will you come back with us, do the proper paperwork, yes? Then we can be getting out of your hair for good.

从口中轻飘飘地，她提出了一个交易。\
With a light tone, she proposes a deal.

所有人都陷入了犹豫，沉默。\
Yet all involved suddenly grow hesitant and quiet.

**J**：……\
**J**: ...

**先驱者**：……只要你的证据足以让我们信服。\
**Pioneer**: The burden of proof lies with you, Special Investigator.

**玛蒂尔达**：好吧，你们最好说话算话……我并不想打击你们，但如果你们非此不可……\
**Matilda**: Alright. But I will hold you to your word, mannequin. Before we begin, I should say, I don't do this lightly, but if you need to know, don't say I didn't warn you.

身上的绳索被解开了。\
She is released from her ropes.

她推开两人，抚平桌台上的黑色天鹅绒布，将水晶球放置于中央。\
She pushes the others aside, smoothing out the black velvet cloth on the table, before placing a crystal ball in its center.

**玛蒂尔达**：我是水晶占卜师。你们应该很清楚这个能力代表着什么。\
**Matilda**: I am a diviner, one that uses crystals. I suspect that sort of practice may already be familiar to you.

**玛蒂尔达**：请交给我一件象征保利娜女士身份的、她曾使用或拥有的物件，这个物件必须要与她的过往有着深刻的联结。\
**Matilda**: I'll need an object that symbolizes Ms. Lesa-, Paulina, or something related to her. It must have a deep connection to her, something she once owned or often used.

**玛蒂尔达**：我会循着它的气息，揭开迷雾，为你们找寻到她存在的痕迹或所在……\
**Matilda**: I will then begin my scrying using this object to the fog in my crystal orb and reveal to us her current existence.

**玛蒂尔达**：但若等我揭开迷雾，发现在那之后空无一物……这通常便意味着只有一个可能。\
**Matilda**: But if we find nothing beneath the fog, I am quite sure you understand what this means.

**玛蒂尔达**：——而那时，你们就必须得跟我走了。\
**Matilda**: And then, I will be needing you to return with me.

**玛蒂尔达**：另外，据我所知，能量疗愈师通常拥有敏锐的灵性感知力，可以洞察神秘学家在占卜时能量的流动……\
**Matilda**: And as I've heard that energy healers are able to detect the flow of pneuma ...

**玛蒂尔达**：这位女士，她应该可以在场证明我的占卜。你能做到吗……女士？\
**Matilda**: The madame here will be able to prove the authenticity of my divination, no?

**环状水星**：我刚才已经见到了能量从你朋友们的手心，流向了术杖……于我而言，这不可能隐藏。\
**Mercuria**: I'll see it. Yeah, like I saw the arcane energy flowing from your little friend's hand to their wand just now.

**先驱者**：J？\
**Pioneer**: J, what do you think of all this?

他把肩膀靠在柜子边，没有靠近，只是远远地答复。\
J leans against the edge of a nearby cabinet, keeping his distance and responding from afar.

**J**：保利娜肯定没想到她最信任的基金会帮手，如今将亲自揭穿她的谎言……我这个笨妹妹，这下该知道她哥哥对付她绰绰有余。\
**J**: My sister's little minion back at the Foundation already exposed the lie. Still, seems only fair I get to spy on her back. We'll see who's laughing now, sis.

**J**：没问题，小家伙——拿去吧。\
**J**: Alright, Frenchie. This is hers. Take it.

一只软绒绒的玩具小熊，松散的绒毛已脱落了不少。\
A plush teddy bear, its fur now well-worn and patchy.

那是她为这个家族留下的最后一件礼物，他当然保留着。\
It is the last thing she had from their parents, and one of the last things he has of hers.

一切皆已就位，女孩抚平胸膛的躁动，缓和下呼吸。\
Everything is in place. Matilda eases the tension in her chest with a deep breath.

**玛蒂尔达**：开始吧。\
**Matilda**: Then let us commence.

双手覆上水晶球，她紧闭双眼。\
Her hands scour the crystal ball as she closes her eyes.

缺少了月光与潮汐的加持，她的气息有些许紊乱。\
Absent moonlight and tides, her regular breathing becomes erratic under the stress.

但没有关系，如今她只需要证明一个生命的存在……甚至不需要一个确切的所在。\
But all that is no matter to her. The only thing she has to do is find one person, and she does not even need to find her. Only prove that she exists, or that she does not.

**玛蒂尔达**：牵引物品的丝线，追寻这位所有者的迹象……请回应我的叩问。\
**Matilda**: Thread that binds all, show me the trace of the one to whom this belongs. I bid you to respond!

水晶球透过手指，散发出了微弱的光亮。\
The crystal ball emits a faint glow through her fingers.

一团沉甸甸的迷雾升起，充溢水晶球。\
A heavy mist rises, obscuring the inside of the ball.

**J**：……！\
**J**: ...!

**玛蒂尔达**：褪去薄雾，褪去隐匿者的外壳，请显现她的实相——\
**Matilda**: Lift the fog. Reveal what existence lies hidden from us.

**玛蒂尔达**：尽在我们眼中。\
**Matilda**: Give us your vision. Sight beyond sight!

**玛蒂尔达**：……\
**Matilda**: ...

许久，涌动的迷雾已然褪去……\
Time passes as the swirling mist slowly, achingly dissipates.

女孩的双手离开了水晶球，眼睛瞥向别处，不再说一句话。\
Matilda withdraws her hand from the crystal ball. She silently shifts her eyes away.

摆放在一旁的小熊仍炯炯有神地盯着水晶球。\
The little bear beside her appears to have its eyes fixed on the ball.

**J**：——嘿？小家伙，我们可还没有看见任何结果，你怎么突然撂摊子了？\
**J**: What, all that and you just stop? This thing busted or something? Nothing happened.

**环状水星**：J……\
**Mercuria**: J ...

**环状水星**：……这次占卜，正如她之前所说，已经宣告结束了。\
**Mercuria**: The divination is over. The energy is gone, just like she said.

而男人不以为然。\
J feigns ignorance.

他知道这次他很冷静。\
Still, he is far calmer than any thought he should be.

**J**：天呐，饶了我吧，你们这帮基金会的把戏还没用腻歪吗？\
**J**: You come all this way, for what? Just another Foundation trick?

**J**：这次又是什么糊弄人的把戏？！你对这颗水晶球动了什么手脚……嗯？为了让她躲下去，你们有必要——\
**J**: So, what is it this time? Did you mess around with the orb? Some kind of protection skill? I don't have time for these games.

**先驱者**：J！\
**Pioneer**: J!

假人的声音震耳欲聋，响彻回荡。\
The mannequin's voice is deafening.

**先驱者**：……她已经不在了。\
**Pioneer**: It means she's really gone.

**环状水星**：抱歉……J。\
**Mercuria**: Sorry, J.

**J**：…………\
**J**: ...

没有惊诧或是愤怒，远处的J如此平静——\
He keeps up his stone-calm face, giving no sign of anger or astonishment.

连面容也没有丝毫变化。\
There is no change in his expression at all.

不是心如死灰，也绝非恍惚。\
It is both emotional and emotionless at the same time.

**先驱者**：你……还好吗，我的伙计？\
**Pioneer**: J, are you still with us?

**J**：不，我没事。\
**J**: Yeah, yeah, I'm fine.

嘴唇并不震颤，身体没有摇晃。\
The words hang stiffly on his lips.

**J**：原来是这样……\
**J**: So I guess it's legit.

他望向水晶球。\
He looks into the crystal ball again.

他的嘴唇几不可见地微张，想言语些什么，又合了回去。\
His lips parting, as if wanting to speak, but nothing comes out.

那是什么？那是……什么？\
As if wanting to ask a thousand questions at the same time.

他撇过头，望见远处喧闹的人群中，正有位年轻的女孩戴着花环舞蹈，悠悠地旋转——\
He turns his head again, his eyes drifting out to the crowded market, to a girl dancing in the midst of the crowd, a girl adorned with a crown of flowers.

旋转。\
She twirls gracefully.

掌声此起彼伏，喜悦充盈着人们的脸。\
The crowd applauds, their faces joyful—happy.

他想他是时候该声泪俱下，或者向全世界挥空拳头，甚至砸烂那颗真相的水晶球。\
He wants to cry, or scream, or even to take that ball in his hands and smash it to pieces.

但他没有。\
But he does nothing.

他站在那里，接受着这股前所未有的沉静。\
In a swirling storm of grief, despair, and rage, he finds his center.

无人察觉，剔透的水晶球底部，出现了一道细微的裂痕。\
Unnoticed by any present, a faint crack appears at the base of the crystal ball.

## FT-06 乐园在即 / Elysium Is Coming

她往行李中塞着一件件必备物，就像逃亡前夜的难民，一刻也不想停留。\
Her luggage is half-packed and already overstuffed. She's rushing, haphazardly throwing things in as she goes, unwilling to pause for even a moment.

**保利娜**：蠢货、傻瓜、不可理喻的独裁者！天杀的，我早就该知道，从那张嘴巴里冒出来的每一句话，都不应该相信！花言巧语，满嘴跑火车！\
**Paulina**: That smug, know-it-all, manipulative bastard. How is it that I still need to learn not to trust anything that comes out of that-that stupid lying jerk's mouth?

**保利娜**：“没收到信件”、“没有人访问”、“没有消息”……这也没有，那也没有！\
**Paulina**: "No mail today, sis," "Nah, no visitors yet, Polly," "Haven't heard a word" ... Just another pack of lies, and I bought 'em.

一叠落灰的圣洛夫基金会职员邀请函放在桌面上。其中仅有一件拆封，并被好好折了起来。\
On the desk lies a crumpled stack of invitations from the St. Pavlov Foundation. Only one was ever opened.

**J**：嘿，保利娜，把门打开！你他*在干什么？\
**J**: Hey, Polly, open the door! What are you even doing in there?

**保利娜**：滚远点，J！你以为你是我的什么人？你到底自大到了什么地步，以为自己可以干涉我的命运、我的选择、我的未来？\
**Paulina**: Leave me the hell alone, Joe! Who the hell do you think you are to decide my choice, my future, my fate?

**保利娜**：让你那满是污言秽语的嘴巴离我远一点！我今天就要离开这个发霉的鬼地方！\
