**Paulina**: Don't talk to me. Don't ever talk to me again! I'm leaving, today!

门外传来铿锵有力的回应。\
A fierce response booms through the door.

**J**：他们所谓的伟大使命就那么令你着迷？你难道还不清楚你上当了吗？保利娜！\
**J**: Whatever—Why are you even this obsessed with this "mission" of theirs?! They're fooling you, sis, don't you see it?!

**J**：只有两种人会投身于他们所谓的“愿和平与我们同在”的可笑理想！\
**J**: Only two kinds of people that buy the "Peace Be with Us" kind of bulls**t they're selling.

**J**：一种是像你这样的傻瓜！对世界上的一切了解都来自于书本上的芝麻小字！\
**J**: The first kind are those like you, Polly. Stupid kids that don't know nothing 'bout anything except what they've read in books.

**J**：另一种就是依托着这个可笑理想，企图分一杯羹的混账！他们榨取傻瓜的信任，为他们自己的地界添砖加瓦！\
**J**: And the others are the ones fleecing you. Taking all you got, and spitting you out, all so they can have more money, more control.

他掏开肺腑一般，愤怒地呐喊。接着，终归冷静下来。\
He pours out his anger, inadvertently realizing the weight of his own words.

**J**：抱歉……我没能控制自己。\
**J**: Pol- ... I'm sorry, alright. I flew off the handle. I made a mistake.

**J**：对他们来说，一滴水无足轻重，一滴鲜血也微不足道，哪怕是一片瓦砾也可以随手丢掉。\
**J**: But these guys, Paulina. You think they care about you? About anyone? You're just another penny in their pocket, a coal for their furnace. They'll burn you up and replace you, easy as that.

**J**：你会说那些慷慨激昂的话，是因为你并不真正了解生活本身。\
**J**: You think you're going out there, do something big, because you don't even know what life is yet.

**J**：当你看到书上写着“一个为伟大理想牺牲的圣洛夫基金会职员”时，你只是看见了那些字眼……妹妹。\
**J**: You just read about it in your books, telling you some s**t about "A Foundation member paying the ultimate sacrifice for others," and think that makes them some kind of hero. You don't know what that kind of sacrifice means, sis.

**J**：你不理解当那名职员面对死亡时的颤抖，你也不理解他在想什么。如果他在后悔呢？他会写出来给你看吗……？\
**J**: Do they say how those "brave" Foundation goons really felt facing death? They aren't going to tell you they were afraid, that they hated everyone who put them there, that they probably s**t themselves before they bit it, just wishing they could go home. They don't put that in books, do they?

**J**：你理解的只是那几捆书本和那些字，而不是真相！\
**J**: You read what they want you to think. It ain't the truth, Polly.

**J**：而我即便读不懂那些书，拼不出那些该死的句子！——但我所理解，我所从经验中得到的是……就是这个世界本身！\
**J**: Maybe I'm not smart like you, sis. I can't read the things you read, can't learn like you. But I learned the hard way.

**保利娜**：够了，我才不在乎你说什么！\
**Paulina**: Enough, J. I really don't give a crap about what you've learned "on the streets." I don't want to hear it.

**保利娜**：我宁愿死在外面，也不要在这里发臭！\
**Paulina**: I'd rather take my chances and die out there than stay here and never live at all.

门被狠狠踹出一个洞，打了开来。\
J kicks the door hard, smashing a hole straight through it.

他走进了门扉。\
He steps in through the now-open doorway.

**玛蒂尔达**：……真可恶，我一点也不想去做那个宣布坏消息的人。\
**Matilda**: I feel sorry to be the, how do you say it, "bearer of bad news"?

**玛蒂尔达**：但这样至少能让他们愿意与我们合作，不再去扩散消息……\
**Matilda**: But at least now they are willing to cooperate, no?

**玛蒂尔达**：只是……\
**Matilda**: Only ...

她用脚尖撵着地上的尘土，仿若一个手足无措的孩子。\
She taps the ground with the tip of her shoe.

她从未想过，完成任务原来并没有那么值得骄傲。\
There is an unwilling feeling of shame rather than pride at her work in this moment.

**玛蒂尔达**：那两个职员怎么还没醒过来？帐篷里重塑之手的情报很有意义，我们得赶紧回去汇报才行……\
**Matilda**: Why my team members haven't awakened yet? We really must report our information on the Manus Vindictae back to the Foundation.

她不安地走动，渐行渐远。\
She paces forward and back.

**玛蒂尔达**：自从阿尔卡纳被证实死亡以后，重塑之手的人就完全变了个样，像群鼹鼠全躲了起来……\
**Matilda**: After Arcana's death, the remnants of the Manus Vindictae all scattered into the wind, nowhere to be found.

**玛蒂尔达**：他们甘愿放弃大量物资，将自己隐匿在这个新时代里……基金会也一直没能找到他们的去向。\
**Matilda**: They even abandoned all their stashes and resources just to hide in this era. And it seems they succeeded. There has been no trace of them so far.

**玛蒂尔达**：哼……而我所得到的这个讯息，或许正是帮助我们揪出重塑余党的关键。\
**Matilda**: Well, not yet. But I think perhaps with this news, Special Investigator Matilda Bouanich will be the one to at last find the key.

**玛蒂尔达**：这一趟调查，一定能让上级对我更加刮目相看，说不定，还能申请将十四行诗指派到我的小队里……\
**Matilda**: I am very certain that my exemplary intelligence gathering will be rewarded by our leaders. Oh, perhaps, they might even place Ms. Sonetto on my team.

一位男人从旁擦身而过，跌倒在地。\
A man bumps into her and then tumbles hard to the ground.

**玛蒂尔达**：嘿，小心点儿！我这个肩膀已经受够意外事故了……\
**Matilda**: Hump. Mind yourself, please. I have had quite enough of these bumping accidents today.

趴在地上的男人恍若未闻，眼睛失去了聚焦，跌跌撞撞地起身。\
She speaks, but he is oblivious to her words as he rises clumsily to his feet.

接着，就在他仰起头的一瞬间，一股狂欢的、狰狞的喜悦再度爬上了他的脸庞。\
His face is a wild contortion of joy and madness, lacking any awareness.

**敲铃人**：启示就要来了，“受苦者”的启示就要降临了！\
**Bell-Ringer**: The enlightenment! Soon comes the Sufferer's enlightenment!

**玛蒂尔达**：？！\
**Matilda**: ?!

在他不经意露出的脖颈处，是一个熟悉的图案。\
There is a familiar pattern on his neck.

她怔在了原地。\
She freezes in place, taking in the shock.

**玛蒂尔达**：重塑……之手？！不、不对，可他并没有变成他们的模样……！\
**Matilda**: A Manus's sign? But certainly, they didn't transform into those monsters.

未等她迈步追上去，四周便涌动了起来。\
Before she can take a step to follow, her surroundings begin to stir.

起初，是一个人；而后，是不断从四周冒出来的奔跑者，是此起彼伏的脚步声。\
They come one by one; then more emerging, all pouring in one direction as if drawn in by a funnel.

**众人**：启示……是启示！\
**All**: Enlightenment. It's the enlightenment!

集会中的人们，犹如觅光的飞蛾纷涌向同一处漩涡。\
The crowd stampedes across the grounds.

周围顷刻间几乎变得空空荡荡，仅余一些零星的摊贩无动于衷。\
The moment passes, and her immediate surroundings empty, leaving behind only herself and a few indifferent vendors.

**玛蒂尔达**：这是怎么一回事？\
**Matilda**: What is happening?

**玛蒂尔达**：不管了！……我得找到刚才那个家伙！\
**Matilda**: I need to follow that man!

她跟上人群的脚步，试图凑过去，却被拥挤的人圈排斥在外。\
She attempts to follow him, pushing through against the crowd, but the heavy press of bodies is like a wall.

**玛蒂尔达**：可恶……让一让！你们这些汗涔涔的家伙！\
**Matilda**: Please! Pardon me! Ouphf. They're all so sweaty.

**玛蒂尔达**：嗯……？\
**Matilda**: Hmm?

一个瘦小的身子，正狡黠地在人们腿边流窜。\
She catches sight of a nimble shadow moving through the crowd.

**猫眼维森**：大声嚷吧，笨蛋们……都把手举高一点，让你们的口袋敞开大门。\
**Cateye Wisen**: Yeah! Yeah! Chant louder, you stupid jerks. The higher you lift those arms, the easier it is to reach into those pockets.

他示范了一条明晰的“捷径”。\
She spies him as he darts under legs and through the throng—a shortcut of sorts.

**玛蒂尔达**：嘿嘿，一条不错的“小路”。只需要暂时不引人注意一些……\
**Matilda**: A clever way to get around, if not so very decent. But then, I suppose decency is far from the most important thing now.

她蹲下来，亦步亦趋。\
She crouches down and follows his lead.

这是一次巧妙的“偷袭”，所有人的目光正聚集在那位老人身上。\
No one takes notice of her. All eyes are drawn to an older-looking man as he begins to speak.

**？？？**：……我们的世界已在荒谬的海洋中沉浮多日——\
**???**: Our world drowns ever deeper into depravity.

**？？？**：无数的可怜人沉溺于现象与理智的牢笼，拒绝承认最后的审判日与救赎，将自己出卖在那些当啷作响的游戏厅与邪恶的音律之中。\
**???**: The multitudes, trapped in their cages of materialism and logic, refuse to acknowledge the coming day of Judgment and salvation. Instead, they sell their souls to violence, gangs, and vile music.

**？？？**：他们捧腹大笑，他们痛哭流涕，他们言不由衷……他们将灵魂抛给与自己毫不相干的故事和骗局，遗忘了自己的归途，也不再关切命运的去向。\
**???**: Though they may laugh or cry, they know nothing of the truth, and speak only lies. Held hostage to their worldly possessions, but forgetting the value of their souls.

**？？？**：而“受苦者”——却不以为意，祂发现了我们羔羊的灵魂，誓要将救赎给予迷途的孩子们。\
**???**: But the Sufferer didn't abandon us. THEY know where the souls are hidden. THEY will save our lost children, save us.

**？？？**：为此祂甘愿坠入汪洋，为此祂甘愿忍受着灼烧的痛楚，乃至接受降临于祂的死亡。\
**???**: THEY suffered burning pain, even faced death for us.

道道泪痕在脸上刻下痕迹。\
He allows a line of tears to etch down his face.

但他字字铿锵，脸上全然没有悲伤，仅是犹如佩戴着铜制的面具一般。\
Yet, his words are spoken firm, and he shows no hint of emotion. Indeed, his face is almost mask-like in its stillness.

**？？？**：如今，祂的子嗣齐聚一堂……我们深知救赎的真相只握在我们手中。警察与政府，族群与国家只是一出历史的卑劣谎言，唯有“受苦者”的再临是一切的救赎。\
**???**: And now, together we are THEIR children. Only we possess the truth of salvation. Police, governments, communities, and nations are only the deceitful constructs of history; our salvation lies solely in the return of the Sufferer.

**？？？**：而经各位子嗣的帮扶，献予“受苦者”的诞生庆典将至，如此欢喜，如此赞美！\
**???**: But now, we must stand shoulder to shoulder, as we anticipate our coming celebration of the Sufferer. We await, we rejoice!

**众信徒**：如此欢喜！如此赞美！\
**Believers**: We await, we rejoice.

**？？？**：“受苦者”的赞颂已至圆满，接下来，让我们迎来一位新加入的子嗣——\
**???**: The Sufferer has heard us, know this, children. Now take heart, for we have another lost lamb who has cast aside the world to join us.

肃静的人群里，一个男人走到台前，跪坐了下来。\
From the silent crowd, a man hobbles forward and kneels.

**？？？**：……\
**???**: ...

**？？？**：莱格斯，“受苦者”亲吻了你千疮百孔的身躯，将你纳入了祂的子嗣之中。如今，你是否愿意以鲜血来证明你的忠诚与牺牲？\
**???**: Legers, the Sufferer has bestowed THEIR blessings onto your broken body, and welcomes you to be THEIR child. Would you present THEM your loyalty with the shedding of blood?

**玛蒂尔达**：鲜血？！\
**Matilda**: Blood?!

**莱格斯**：……我祈求，我崇奉。\
**Legers**: I would, and I pray.

他手执匕首，锯木一般划拉着手心，鲜血流淌——\
He holds up the dagger, drawing a long sharp cut across his palm, and lets the blood stream down.

**莱格斯**：呃……！\
**Legers**: Urgh!

斑斑血迹滴落在地，形成了一个诡谲的符号。\
The blood stains the ground below, forming a mysterious symbol.

**？？？**：如此欢喜！你已被应允了赴往“乐园”的资格，我虔诚的孩子。\
**???**: Rejoice! For the passage to Elysium has been promised to you.

**？？？**：诸位，时刻已到！紧跟敲铃人的脚步，“乐园”的门扉即将开启！\
**???**: All, it is time! Follow the Bell-Ringer, the gate to Elysium shall soon be opened!

他举起双臂，周围响起狂热的回应。\
He raises his arms, and the crowd responds with fervent cheers.

**玛蒂尔达**：？！\
**Matilda**: ?!

双臂掀开的袍子之下，是明晰无疑的答案。\
As he lifts his robe, the answer becomes unmistakable.

**玛蒂尔达**：那是……！重塑之手的印迹！\
**Matilda**: That's the sign of the Manus Vindictae!

**玛蒂尔达**：不行、不行……我得立马离开这里！把这个消息带给基金会！让开，让开！可恶，怎么越来越挤了！\
**Matilda**: I must return to tell the Foundation. I need to get out now! Move, move away! Crap! It's getting crowded!

意料之外的喧嚣，正使人群躁动着。\
The uproar stirs the crowd into an agitated frenzy.

**敲铃人**：不，不可能……我的钥匙，门扉的钥匙去哪了？使徒大人，请、请稍等片刻！\
**Bell-Ringer**: No, it can't be! Where is the key to the gate? Apostle Matheus, p-please wait a moment.

**使徒米修斯**：……！\
**Apostle Matheus**: ...!

高台之上的人，瞥见了意料之外的参与者。\
From the platform, the speaker catches sight of the darting figures.

**使徒米修斯**：诸位，环视你们四周！仪式之中，正有叛徒与不虔诚者！\
**Apostle Matheus**: Be vigilant, all! There are deceivers among us!

**玛蒂尔达**：糟糕……\
**Matilda**: Crap!

她的脚步更快，把头埋得更低了——\
She quickens her pace, rushing without caution through the crowd.

“咚！”——两个小脑袋撞击在了一起。\
"Thud!"—Two heads collide.

**猫眼维森**：疼、疼疼！\
**Cateye Wisen**: Ouch!

**敲铃人**：他们在那儿！\
**Bell-Ringer**: Behold, the deceivers among us!

手指指向的地方，人们不约而同地让出了一个圆圈。\
Where the finger points, the crowd instinctively makes way, leaving the two surrounded in an empty circle.

从眩晕中缓过来的女孩，终于察觉到了糟糕的处境。\
As Matilda returns to her senses, she realizes the dire nature of their predicament.

**玛蒂尔达**：糟……糟了。\
**Matilda**: Not good.

**猫眼维森**：该死、该死、该死！你是从哪里闯过来的丫头？……你就没打听过这是谁的地盘吗？你把这一切都搞砸了！\
**Cateye Wisen**: Dang it! Dang it! Dang it! Where did you come from?! Didn't anyone tell you whose turf this is?! Ahh, we're in so much trouble.

男孩的兜里满满当当，他以不协调的姿势奔跑着。\
The boy's pockets are stuffed full, jingling as he moves and making him run in an awkward, clunky manner.

**玛蒂尔达**：哈、哈、哈……什么？！玛蒂尔达小姐想去哪儿就去哪儿！明明是你这个小偷罪有应得，还把我拖下了水！\
**Matilda**: *panting* What?! I can go wherever I please. Y-you rude little boy! I-I should have let them catch you.

轮胎的嗡鸣声从身后愈发接近，很快赶上了两人。\
An engine growls behind them, gaining ground on them fast.

**玛蒂尔达**：为什么他们还会骑这个？哈、哈呼……\
**Matilda**: Where did they get this vehicle?! *panting*

这场马拉松式逃跑的结果没有任何悬念。\
Their capture now appears inevitable.

**贝克特**：混小子，你可没说会把动静弄得这么响！这可是惹了一群狼狗……！\
**Becket**: Son of a gun, kid. What did I tell you about making a mess! These freaks are mad!

机车上的男人一把提起男孩，放到后座上。\
The man on the motorcycle grabs the boy, pinning him to the back seat in a fluid motion.

**贝克特**：坐好了，我要拧油门了！\
**Becket**: Sit back, rubber's hitting the road!

**玛蒂尔达**：？！\
**Matilda**: ?!

**猫眼维森**：哈哈哈，先走一步，跟屁虫！\
**Cateye Wisen**: Hahahaha, so long, suckers!

**玛蒂尔达**：喂——喂！等一等，你、你该不会要把我丢在这里吧！\
**Matilda**: Damn! Wait! Are you really just leaving me here?!

她的双腿感到发软，呼吸一次比一次更重。\
Her legs are giving out from exertion, huffing with labored breaths.

**？？？**：——你好。喔，这是从哪来的贵族淑女？我们见过面吗？\
**???**: What brings you out here, short stuff? Starting to wonder why we keep running into each other.

另一辆嗡鸣的摩托车放松了油门，缓缓跟在她的身边。\
Another engine roars, and then the throttle eases as it pulls up alongside her.

**玛蒂尔达**：是、是——你？！你，哈、哈呼……应该按照玛蒂尔达的命令，在帐篷里乖乖等着！\
**Matilda**: It's you?! You should have listened to me and waited in the tent! You, you oaf!

**J**：拜托，如果我现在还在那儿待着，你就该被他们绑起来送进烤炉里变成烤火鸡，连酱汁都淋好了！\
**J**: You've got a funny way of saying thanks, French Fry. If I listened to you back there, you'd have been stuck here and hung out to dry.

**玛蒂尔达**：哼！玛蒂尔达可是在第一防线学校的体、体育测试里拿过全优的健将，才不需要你的帮助！\
**Matilda**: I got straight As in SPDM's P.E. tests! I-I do not need your help!

**玛蒂尔达**：我靠自己就能甩掉这群笨手笨脚的家伙！\
**Matilda**: I can take care of these kooky cultists all by myself.

**J**：悉听尊便，女士～\
**J**: As you wish, my lady!

他从未如此听劝，晃开了距离。\
He is more than happy to accommodate her, putting a sizeable distance between them before slowing again.

**信徒**：把格拉瓦库斯放出来！\
**Believer**: Release the Glawackus!

笼子里龇牙咧嘴的魔精，泄洪般奔涌而出。\
The magical critters snarl and bare their teeth from the cage, before bursting out.

**异种格拉瓦库斯**：嘶#&……%！\
**Glawackus Mutant**: *roar*

**玛蒂尔达**：？！\
**Matilda**: ?!

**玛蒂尔达**：格、格拉瓦库斯，不、不可能——原始种的鼻子远没有这么灵敏，这是他们驯化过的特殊品种！\
**Matilda**: Glawackus?! No, they don't have such an acute sense of smell. It must be a kind of mutant they tamed!

**J**：需——要帮忙吗？淑女。\
**J**: Knight in shining chrome; at your service. Just say the word.

**玛蒂尔达**：离我远点，别沾上我的气味！优先保护好自己——！\
**Matilda**: Please keep your distance, sir. It is me they are after! You must keep yourself safe!

**玛蒂尔达**：我可是圣洛夫基金会屈指可数的特派调查员，肩负着保护你们这些笨蛋的职责。\
**Matilda**: I am an investigator of the St. Pavlov Foundation, and it is my duty to protect civilians!

**J**：……\
**J**: ...

那是如此相似的话语。\
Her words feel strikingly familiar.

以及同样匆快的步伐。\
And also familiar hurried steps.

**玛蒂尔达**：火光灼——\
**Matilda**: Fuego Bu—

**玛蒂尔达**：嗷？！\
**Matilda**: Huh?!

被打断施术的女孩，一脸错愕地被提到了后座之上。\
Her incantation is interrupted as she is lifted unwillingly onto the back of J's motorcycle.

**J**：平起平坐，小家伙……我也想少费些功夫，但你的腿脚看起来都要跑出火星子了。\
**J**: Get on, Frenchie. Really don't wanna get involved, but you were starting to look like a lost puppy, so I'll forgive you.

**J**：如果你想要保护他人，相信我……最好的主意是先学会如何接受他人的帮助。\
**J**: You know, Short Fry, if you're trying to protect someone, you should learn when to accept their help.

**J**：勇气这回事儿——得先承认自己的力所不及，不耻于借助他人的臂膀开始。\
**J**: No one gets anywhere in this world alone. Not even at your big-shot Foundation.

风呼啸而过，后座的女孩愣愣地伸出了脑袋。\
The wind howls past as they pick up speed. Matilda sticks her head up to speak.

**玛蒂尔达**：……你、你说什么？玛蒂尔达什么也听不见——风太大了！\
**Matilda**: What did you say? I cannot hear you! The wind is too loud!

**J**：我——说，你得学会借助他人的帮助！\
**J**: I said, take the help!

**玛蒂尔达**：什……么？\
**Matilda**: WHAAAAT?

**J**：……\
**J**: ...

**J**：我说你别他*——\
**J**: I said take ** ...

脏话到了嘴边，又被吞了回去。\
A number of profanities tingle on his tongue, but for the moment, he swallows them back.

**J**：我说你别忘了把脚抬高，前面要过泥潭子了——！！！\
**J**: Hold on to your socks, water ahead!!

## FT-07 好哥们，好主顾 / Best Buds, Best Guest

机车缓缓驶入街巷，紧紧尾随的教众们已不知去向。\
The motorcycle slows as it enters the alley, having lost their mad pursuers.

熟悉的人们纷纷伸出了脑袋，啧啧称奇。\
Familiar faces poke out from nearby, marveling at the new arrivals.

**管道工**：哈哈哈，J，你这是打哪儿拐了个小女孩回来，你难道不知道这帮吹牛打屁的糙汉子可没空帮你带孩子吗？\
**Plumber**: Hahahaha, J, where did you get this chick? I hope you aren't looking for a babysitter!

**女侍者**：J——替我向先驱者先生问好！多亏他推荐的高跟鞋，那个好莱坞派头的导演一下子就看中我了！\
**Waitress**: Hey, J, you say hi to Pioneer for me! Those heels he recommended helped me land a big role.

**乞丐布莱恩**：G——您是叫G先生吗？我一直在找您……托您的福——这个徽章，救济院的特里斯终于愿意给我一张床，他说我明天就可以去做那份刷碗的工作了……\
**Brian the Beggar**: Hey, uhm, Mr. G, right? It's me, Brian. I've been looking for you. All thanks to you and that badge you got me. They finally gave me a room down at the shelter. They even offered me some dishwashing work tomorrow!

**乞丐布莱恩**：永别了，天台和臭水沟！谢谢您，朋友，谢谢！\
**Brian the Beggar**: No more sleeping in tents or under the overpass! Bless you, Mr. G. I owe you my life!

J停下车子，伸出手，紧紧握住了布莱恩颤抖的手掌。\
J stops his bike, reaching out to grip Brian's hand.

**J**：噢，别这样，布、布——布莱恩！……你也帮我要到了那位漂亮妞的电话号码，不是吗？咱们这都是互帮互助，没有谁亏欠谁的！\
**J**: Oh, come on, Bri-Bri ... Brian! Weren't you the one that helped me get that girl's number? You help me, I help you! That's the deal.

远处，一位牵着魔精的男人走了过来。\
From the distance, a man leading a critter approaches.

**魔精保姆**：嘿，我的好主顾J！你要借的最新一期《摩托女郎·特定本》到了！\
**Critter Babysitter**: Hey, if isn't my favorite customer, J! I got the latest edition of Motor Babe, you interested?

**魔精保姆**：全是货真价实的好货——\
**Critter Babysitter**: I swear they're not pirated!

J笑容可掬，踢起了脚撑，迅速拧紧油门。\
J offers only a warm smile as a reply, before kicking up the stand and twisting the throttle on his bike.

**J**：回见，朋友们，回见！\
**J**: See ya, guys!

**魔精保姆**：嘿，嘿，J……我在跟你说话呢，你还要不要这份杂志了？\
**Critter Babysitter**: Hey, HEY! I'm talking to you, J! Want it or not?

**玛蒂尔达**：……那个家伙是不是正在喊你的名字？\
**Matilda**: Isn't that man calling you?

**J**：抱歉，我没听见，机车的嗡鸣声实在是太大了！\
**J**: What are you saying? Sorry, this kitten here purrs pretty loud!

**玛蒂尔达**：还有，你背后的这把怪东西都硌疼我了，你为什么就非得一直带着它？\
**Matilda**: Um, this thing you have behind your back, is it not troublesome? Why do you take it with you?

**J**：噢……这是我老爸留下来的东西，已经跟了我很多年啦！\
**J**: Oh, my dad gave it to me. Carried it around for years.

**玛蒂尔达**：它到底是什么……东西？\
**Matilda**: What is it?

**J**：抓紧！……小家伙，我们就要到了。\
**J**: Hold on tight! We're almost there.

……\
...

它们安详地躺卧在桌面上，周围的男人们摩挲着胡须，琢磨着它们的老家身在何处。\
Items are strewn on the table, as those present stroke their chins pondering over them.

**猫眼维森**：这就是我从那个敲铃人的口袋里掏出来的所有东西了……除了屁*，相信我，我已经把能掏的东西都掏了一遍了。\
**Cateye Wisen**: Here's everything that was in that Bell-Ringer guy's pockets. Think I got everything, except anything that he was wearing under that get-up, but there ain't enough money in the world to get me to rifle through some s**t-stained cultist undies.

**猫眼维森**：噢！霍利克，你敲我的头干嘛！\
**Cateye Wisen**: Hey! Hollick, what was that for?!

**霍利克**：呃，J说过，你每说一句脏话，就得给你一个“榔头”，让你长长记性。\
**Hollick**: Sorry, kiddo, J said I gotta knock you on the head any time you cuss.

**J**：嗯……我是说过这话……咱们都得嘴巴放干净点儿。瞧瞧，这不是还有位淑女正站在我们旁边么？\
**J**: Exactly, Hollick. We gotta teach this potty mouth some manners, especially when there's a lady present.

**先驱者**：……没想到我一直以来不受待见的绅士主张，竟然在这个时候通通实现了，感谢您的指导，玛蒂尔达小姐！\
**Pioneer**: Well, seems I have you to thank, Ms. Bouanich! Years of wasted effort trying to cultivate gentlemen out of these cads, and you manage it in hours!

一旁的女孩正捣鼓着复杂的仪器，丝毫没有理会这边的盛况。\
The girl nearby is fiddling with a complicated device, unfazed by their commotion.

**系统音**：欢迎使用SPF-I型便携联络装置。\
**SPF-I**: SPF-I Portable Contact Device activated. Welcome.

**系统音**：……验证成功。登录人员：玛蒂尔达·布翁尼。目前开放权限等级——B。\
**SPF-I**: Verification success. Registered user: Matilda Bouanich. Access level: B.

**玛蒂尔达**：成功了！哼哼，今非昔比，如今作为特派调查员的玛蒂尔达已经拥有了更高的权限！\
**Matilda**: It worked! Humph, I have a higher rank now. I won't be making the same mistake twice.

**系统音**：“紧急支援申请”——抱歉，目前紧急支援小队正被派遣于其他调查任务中，您的周边未发现异常神秘学波动。\
**SPF-I**: "Emergency Support"—Apologies, as there have been no abnormal arcane fluctuations detected, the emergency support team is currently occupied.

**系统音**：请汇报具体讯息，以核实评估是否具备紧急支援的条件。\
**SPF-I**: Please provide further details, so that we can evaluate the necessity of emergency assistance.

**系统音**：哔、哔、哔——您的讯息已送达。\
**SPF-I**: *beep* Message sent.

**系统音**：系统将以支援优先级排序，为您安排支援。\
**SPF-I**: Support will be arranged in order of priority.

**玛蒂尔达**：唉……早知道就提前申请给我的小队多派一些成员了……\
**Matilda**: *sigh* I knew I should have applied for an expansion to our team.

**玛蒂尔达**：这个蠢机器真是什么忙都帮不上……为了准确地传达情报，还得让我仅有的两位队员将调查报告带回去做进一步评估。\
**Matilda**: They will be of no help at all. I will have to send my entire team back just to deliver my report to the Foundation.

**玛蒂尔达**：只能寄希望于他们能够加快支援申请的进度了……\
**Matilda**: So we must count on them to bring support back.

**J**：哦？申请支援？\
**J**: Oh, yeah? Support?

**J**：所以你也打算掺和一脚？哈哈哈哈，不得不说，我开始欣赏你这个气势汹汹的小家伙了。\
**J**: You wanna be a part of this, French Fry? You finally taking an interest in all of this? Hahaha.

**玛蒂尔达**：才不是掺和一脚！你可是搞错了，圣洛夫基金会将以独立的方式处理这件事，我们不会让你们这些平民参与其中。\
**Matilda**: This is a central part of our mission! The Foundation will deal with this, without letting nosey civilians like you get involved.

**玛蒂尔达**：你们只需要为我们提供重要的线索就够了。玛蒂尔达会带领她的小队，出色地解决这些难题～\
**Matilda**: If you must insist on helping us, I suggest you provide what information you know, and then, I, Special Investigator Matilda Bouanich, will solve the problem and save the day!

她正伸手打算拿起桌上的钥匙。\
She reaches out to the key on the table.

但一张宽大的手掌，迅速盖到了钥匙之上——\
But a large hand covers it before she can grab it.

**J**：我不接受你的提议，小家伙。\
**J**: Yeah, not going to do that.

**J**：在座的所有人，没有谁会把命运交到别人手里。\
**J**: There isn't one of us here on Haight Street that would stand aside while someone else "saves us."

**J**：如果你想要消息，你就得答应我们——我们能亲自解决麻烦。\
**J**: You wanna get a clue about this place, then the first thing you gotta know is that we deal with our own problems.

他并没有将手挪开的意思，直直盯着她。\
He makes no move to remove his hand, staring at her intently.

**玛蒂尔达**：呃——\
**Matilda**: Umm.

**玛蒂尔达**：这已经有违调查员守则，需要经过特殊批准……\
**Matilda**: This would defy regulations. I would need to file for a special approval.

**J**：小家伙，不管你能不能保证，我可以看在你尽职的份儿上为你开个绿灯。\
**J**: Well, you can have the key, little Investigator Bouanich, since you're so dedicated to your job.

**J**：但是，不管最后结果如何——\
**J**: Whether you get your "special approval" or not ...

**J**：我不会把那些让海特街千疮百孔的混账亲手让给你。这不是为了狭隘意义上的复仇——\
**J**: We're going to be the ones to take down those bastards.

**J**：而是因为，海特街的人，只相信由自己亲手伸张的道义。\
**J**: It's not about vengeance. It's that the people here, they'll never trust someone to do this for us. We have to do it ourselves.

**J**：我们早就不寄希望于法官、警察、圣洛夫基金会……所谓给予公平、正义的这些家伙，在海特街，我们宁愿相信过街老鼠。\
**J**: Judges, police, your Foundation ... One rat's nest after another promised to bring us change, and then left us to the wolves.

**J**：至少它们挨过打，也挨过失望的折磨。\
**J**: Nah, worse than rats. At least they know how life here really works.

**J**：它们不会扭头忘记穷人的祈求，也不会自以为是什么拯救他人于水火的救世主。\
**J**: At least they see us. At least rats don't claim to be our saviors.

他挪开了手，将钥匙递给了她。\
He withdraws his hand and allows her to take the key.

**J**：我们只相信一起蹚过阴沟的人。\
**J**: We can only trust someone who's been through the trenches with us.

她接过钥匙，沉甸甸的，仿佛有某种沉重的东西依附其中。\
The key feels heavy in her hand, as if something weighty were attached to it.

**玛蒂尔达**：……谢谢。\
**Matilda**: Thank you, J.

**玛蒂尔达**：这就是重塑之手所谓……通往“乐园”的钥匙。\
**Matilda**: This must be the key to Manus's "Elysium."

**J**：环状水星……\
**J**: Mercuria, would you?

他抬了抬头，示意她把说明接续下去。\
He looks up, signaling for her to continue with the explanation.

**环状水星**：玛蒂尔达小姐，他们借由钥匙，躲藏在某处……一个只属于他们的狂欢之地。\
**Mercuria**: Yeah. This will be the key to wherever their hideout is, a place of dark revelry. They've kept it a close secret.

**环状水星**：我曾瞧见那些返途的人，回来以后都陷入了某种可怖的神往……\
**Mercuria**: But I've seen those that have come back from that place. They're transformed into something unnatural.

**环状水星**：自那之后，他们的灵魂与身躯被完全拴上了锁链……\
**Mercuria**: Their flesh and their spirit ... it wasn't their own anymore.

**环状水星**：我见过最自负的商人在他们脚下卑躬屈膝，而其中一位最虔诚的信徒，一位母亲……将尚在襁褓中的孩子饿死在垃圾堆里。\
**Mercuria**: Big-shot businessmen groveling and sobbing at the feet of their Apostle; and the most loving mother I know, she abandoned her kid by a dumpster.

**环状水星**：许多从集市归来的友人，一个个失去了意志，像着了魔似的在街区中乱窜。\
**Mercuria**: The friends we've lost ... It's like they're gone. They aren't them anymore. They're possessed.

**环状水星**：再之后，他们便完全失去了踪影，成了盖棺定论的失踪者。\
**Mercuria**: Until one day, they just vanish. Never to be seen again.

她摇摇头。\
She shakes her head.

**玛蒂尔达**：你的意思是说……除非我们先找到属于钥匙的唯一的那扇门，把他们从老鼠洞里揪出来——\
**Matilda**: So, we must find this gate, and flush out their nest of vipers before they can open it once more.

**玛蒂尔达**：否则，整个行动都将化为泡影？\
**Matilda**: Otherwise, our mission here and your chance to avenge your friends will fail.

她差点儿要站起身来。\
She bursts up from her seat before falling back down.

**J**：不，还远不止这些……他们为了后天的庆典，已经摆出了前所未有的阵仗。\
**J**: Gets even better from there, French Fry. That ceremony of theirs is set for the day after tomorrow. They're planning something big, bigger than anything they've thrown at us before.

男孩抢答般举起了手。\
The boy raises his hand, eager to answer.

**猫眼维森**：我还听见那些哭哭啼啼的傻大个，嘟嘟囔囔地说什么“最后的启示”。\
**Cateye Wisen**: Yeah, I heard that big guy mumbling stuff like "the last revelation" or something.

**猫眼维森**：他们那副可怜兮兮的样子就像在电玩厅里输光了饭钱的穷鬼一样，哈哈哈哈。\
**Cateye Wisen**: Kinda weird seeing a big dude crying like that, hahaha.

**玛蒂尔达**：“最后的启示”……是指重塑之手在集市最后一次开启“乐园”之门的意思吗？\
**Matilda**: "The last revelation"? Perhaps then this is the last time Manus plan on opening the door to their "Elysium"?

沉默席卷而来，所有人都知道这意味着什么。\
Everyone knows what is implied.

**环状水星**：届时，我们将会失去他们所有人的去向。\
**Mercuria**: And then, they will be gone, perhaps for good.

**环状水星**：J……你知道有不少我们曾经的朋友加入了他们。告诉我……等到那天，如果曾经的朋友将刀尖指向你，你会怎样阻拦他们？\
**Mercuria**: J, you got a lot of friends there still. What'll you do when they point their knives at you?

**环状水星**：如果这群迷途的羔羊，将心甘情愿地跳往悬崖……你觉得我们又该怎么办？\
**Mercuria**: How do we keep their sacrificial lambs from leaping off the cliff?

他并不躲避。\
He does not shy away from his answer.

**J**：……我们总得取舍，环状水星。我从不妄想能救所有人，或者说，我早就放弃了那种不切实际的幻想。\
**J**: Not my business to save someone who doesn't wanna be saved. Never even really thought of saving everyone, not in a long while. It's not worth the pain.

这令多数人心中沉重的答案，却令她前所未有地释怀。\
While the answer weighs heavily on the others, it brings her some relief—borne out of trust, if nothing else.

**环状水星**：……我明白了。\
**Mercuria**: I see.

另一方的支持来得很快。\
The girl from the Foundation pipes up.

**玛蒂尔达**：我暂且……赞同这个家伙说的话。\
**Matilda**: Unfortunately, I cannot disagree this time.

**玛蒂尔达**：而且，我们总可以提前做点儿什么准备！圣洛夫基金会的支援还在途中，在此之前，我们都不要打草惊蛇……\
**Matilda**: Still, we have time to make preparations in advance! Support is on the way, so until then, we must stay below their attention.

**玛蒂尔达**：我打算潜入他们，多收集一些讯息，说不定还能把那扇门找出来。\
**Matilda**: I'm thinking that maybe we may try collecting more information by infiltrating their followers. Perhaps then, we will have a better chance to find this "gate" of theirs.

她扶住了下颚，陷入了思索。\
She supports her chin as she stares out strategizing in her mind.

**环状水星**：别担心，玛蒂尔达小姐，我明天会为你介绍我的朋友与我所扎根的新纪元集市。\
**Mercuria**: Sure, Tildy. Tomorrow I'll show you around the New Age Market. You can meet some of my friends, figure out how to fit in.

**环状水星**：不过，你确实得换一身装束，不管我的朋友有没有跟那帮人产生过纠葛……\
**Mercuria**: Uh, but maybe a change of outfit first. Who knows who might recognize you.

**环状水星**：呵呵，圣洛夫基金会的人员在这里都不太受到待见。\
**Mercuria**: And the St. Pavlov Foundation is not the most welcome organization around here.

**玛蒂尔达**：噢……对了！而且环状水星女士恰好认识那位叫作杰洛的先生，我们还可以从他口中拿到不少线索和消息！\
**Matilda**: I see. Thank you very much, Ms. Mercuria. Oh! And I remember you know that, Gio! We might collect some further information from him!

**环状水星**：杰洛？抱歉，我……不认识你所说的这位先生。\
**Mercuria**: Gio? I don't know who you mean.

她并没有开玩笑的意思。\
Her voice is sincere.

**玛蒂尔达**：可、可我应该没有记错，他就是你刚才接待的那位客人……\
**Matilda**: But, but, do you not remember? It was just as I arrived, you had a visitor, and you called him Gio.

**环状水星**：不……玛蒂尔达小姐，我先前并没有接待任何客人。\
**Mercuria**: I haven't had any visitors all day.

**玛蒂尔达**：J，你也没有看见吗？\
**Matilda**: Ah. That cannot be. J, you saw him, yes?

他别过脸。\
He meets her eyes with a blank expression.

**J**：呃……我只看见了一个小家伙，不怀好意，偷偷摸摸地窥视着帐篷……\
**J**: Only thing I remember is some weirdo investigator poking her head into this tent.

这场匪夷所思的记忆错乱，并没有得到应有的解答。\
Matilda stammers in bewilderment at their answers.

**玛蒂尔达**：……\
**Matilda**: ...

## FT-08 晚祷的叮嘱 / A Warning at Dinner

**使徒米修斯**：应淌的鲜血，应亡的亵渎者……诸位的奉献，已尽收入我的眼中。\
**Apostle Matheus**: Blood must be shed, and our blasphemers eliminated. You have proven your unwavering devotion.

**使徒米修斯**：绿椅子罗杰、小瘟疫迈耶……以及我们的人类兄弟——死人莱格斯先生，欢迎你们莅临“受苦者”的殿堂……\
**Apostle Matheus**: Roger the Green Chair, Meyer the Petty Plague, and our human brother, Legers the Dead, welcome to the Hall of the Sufferer.

**裹布中的人**：呃……唔！呜呜呜！\
**Wrapped Man**: Arrgh ... Uggh! *sob*

角落的笼子中，团状的裹布渗出红色，传来含糊不清的呜咽声。\
A bundled person wrapped in red-stained cloth writhes in a cage, giving out vague, muffled sobs.

他走入阴影，温柔地抚摸着这颤抖的躯体。\
The Apostle steps into the shadows, gently caressing the trembling body.

**使徒米修斯**：嘘……嘘，瞧，多缺礼数——你打扰了我们宝贵的宴席，孩子。\
**Apostle Matheus**: Shush, child. It is rude to disturb our precious feast.

笼子顷刻间陷入了死寂……但那因瑟瑟发抖而响起的磕碰声却仍断断续续。\
The bundle quiets at the touch, though the trembling continues, causing the binds to clink and chafe.

**使徒米修斯**：很好很好，保持安静。\
**Apostle Matheus**: Very well. Remain silent.

他撤身离开了笼子，将双手搭在绿椅子罗杰的肩膀之上。\
He withdraws from the cage and places his hands on Roger the Green Chair's shoulders.

**使徒米修斯**：兄弟姊妹们……你们所拢集的财富，与吸纳的神秘学家子嗣，为“受苦者”的复苏庆典作出了崇高的奉献。\
**Apostle Matheus**: Brothers and sisters, our arcanist siblings and your bountiful offerings gathered have greatly enriched the coming ceremony of the Sufferer.

**使徒米修斯**：我们的信徒日渐虔诚，我也为此满心欢喜——可欢愉遍地，悲恸与憎恶却仍不止息！\
**Apostle Matheus**: We rejoice to see such devotion from the faithful, yet we are troubled by the sorrow and abomination now filling the world!

**使徒米修斯**：——就在昨日，有两名擅入者破坏了降下启示的仪式，并窃走了一把通往“乐园”的钥匙。\
**Apostle Matheus**: Yesterday, two intruders broke the ritual of revelation, and stole from us the key to the gates of Elysium.

**使徒米修斯**：那是“受苦者”苦痛的牺牲前，留予我们何其珍贵的、与世隔绝的“乐园”！\
**Apostle Matheus**: The precious gift of Elysium granted by the Sufferer before THEIR agonizing sacrifice has been blocked from us.

**使徒米修斯**：你们理应知晓，钥匙之事不应泄露。\
**Apostle Matheus**: You should have kept the secret of the key.

寂静，漫长的寂静。\
A prolonged silence follows.

**绿椅子罗杰**：您、您可以将这位泄密者交给我！绿椅子的酷刑能为您撕开他胸膛里的秘密，并把告密者的血肉都还予您！\
**Roger the Green Chair**: L-let me use my green chair to grill this shameful rat! I'll make him talk, spill the secrets he hid, and present his flesh to you as an offering!

**使徒米修斯**：哈哈哈……多么讨喜的兄弟，我的罗杰。\
**Apostle Matheus**: Well, well, Roger, such a caring brother.

**使徒米修斯**：但不、不，我不需要你的帮助，子嗣们已凿尽了他的肺腑，发现他那可怜的胸膛中并无半点秘密——这只是一位虔诚但冒失的同袍。\
**Apostle Matheus**: Your offering is appreciated, yet our siblings have already torn his chest apart and still no secrets—Just another careless fallen brother.

**使徒米修斯**：我只是以此告诫诸位，献予“受苦者”的复苏庆典在即，我一直关切子嗣们的一举一动——你们并不孤独，亦不特殊。\
**Apostle Matheus**: This is our final warning: the ceremony for the Sufferer draws near. I would keep a close watch on every one of our flock. Let not one among you linger alone, nor be held above suspicion.

**使徒米修斯**：此刻，这位泄露了秘密的同袍——敲铃人，正在你们眼前……告诉我，你们谁想给予他最后一丝怜悯与施舍？\
**Apostle Matheus**: And the Bell-Ringer who gave out our secret is here, in front of you. Tell me, which one of you would bestow on him our final mercy?

他晃悠着笼子的钥匙。\
He fidgets with the key of the cage purposefully.

**裹布中的人**：呃呜呜呜……\
**Wrapped Man**: *sob* Urghhh ...

沉默不语的莱格斯，俯身站起。\
Legers stands, breaking his silence.

“叮——”\
"Clink—"

笼子的门被打开，颤抖的肉块跌落在地，蛆虫般在地上扭动。\
The cage door opens. The trembling lump falls to the ground and wriggles like a helpless maggot.

**莱格斯**：吁……\
**Legers**: *whistle*

**异种格拉瓦库斯**：嘶……嘁嘁嘁嘁。\
**Glawackus Mutant**: *roar*

两只影子般的生物，翻过天花板的吊灯，从墙上如同蜘蛛般爬了下来。\
Two shadowy creatures descend the wall from above with predatory motions.

**莱格斯**：把他带走，孩子们……拖得远一些，吃干抹净，别为尊敬的先生留下血污。\
**Legers**: Good, eat your fill, children. Until it's done. Not a single stain left to offend our Apostle.

魔精撕咬着裹布，将肉块拖行着，在地毯上留下一道血痕。\
The drooling critters tear at the wrappings, dragging the body across the floor, leaving a trail of fresh blood.

像是将猎物带回巢穴的蛛类，它们流着口涎，与撕心裂肺的嚎叫一同消失在了黑暗里。\
They deliver a heart-rending howl before disappearing back into the darkness with their feast.

**使徒米修斯**：谢谢你，莱格斯先生……诸位，就座吧，请享用这场难得的盛宴！\
**Apostle Matheus**: Our thanks, Brother Legers. All, be seated, and enjoy the feast!

……\
...

宴席结束，多余的宾客已经散去。\
The banquet ends, and the remaining guests have now dispersed.

**使徒米修斯**：……莱格斯，你最晚与我们同座，所尽的贡献却远甚于其他人。\
**Apostle Matheus**: You may be just a recent convert, still you have more than proven your devotion with your zealous contributions.

**使徒米修斯**：可如今，孩子，是什么遮蔽了你的双目，绊住了你的脚步？……你对新纪元集市失去控制，已将我们陷于窘境。\
**Apostle Matheus**: But my child, something still blinds you, fetters you. That which deprived you of your control of the New Age Market? A thing that threatens to hobble our fast-approaching ceremony.

**使徒米修斯**：连同圣洛夫基金会也肆意游荡，把你的领地当作了后花园。莱格斯，你的威信已在诸位当中竭尽。\
**Apostle Matheus**: Trespassers from the St. Pavlov Foundation, treading across our sacred sanctuaries as if they were their gardens. This failing of yours could reflect poorly in our esteem for you.

**使徒米修斯**：这是一次劝诫，莱格斯，庆典已近，我们并没有太多耐心——把钥匙拿回来。\
**Apostle Matheus**: Brother Legers. The coming of the ceremony cannot be delayed, and we will soon run out of patience. Retrieve the key.

**莱格斯**：……是的，我明白。\
**Legers**: My word is my bond. I will find it.

使徒以手帕擦了擦嘴角。\
The Apostle wipes the corner of his mouth with a handkerchief.

**使徒米修斯**：现在，庆典所需的一切事务虽已齐备，但我们在虔诚的子嗣当中，仍未找寻到一个真正能够担任祭司之职的灵性者。\
**Apostle Matheus**: All is now prepared, but we still seek the one who will lead us through the ritual, a child overflowing with pneuma. Yet, not a single soul now among our flock is qualified.

**使徒米修斯**：我们需要一位真正的祭司——他需得指引着子嗣超脱，带领他们抛却尘世的束缚，真正与“受苦者”融为一体。\
**Apostle Matheus**: We must seek the one who will guide the faithful on the transcendental path, to forsake the world, and become one with the Sufferer.

**使徒米修斯**：——你明白这意味着什么。\
**Apostle Matheus**: I'm sure you understand what is expected of you.

**使徒米修斯**：这是我亲授的使命，不容许第三个人知晓。\
**Apostle Matheus**: Speak to no one about this sacred mission.

**使徒米修斯**：去为我们，也为你自己，寻觅一位合适的祭司，莱格斯。\
**Apostle Matheus**: Find the one worthy of our ceremony for us, and for yourself, Legers.

## FT-09 离巢的蛇 / Snake in the Grass

**疗愈师库伯**：要我说，这位可爱的小姐——远道而来的法国亲戚，应当由我携着！瞧瞧这漂亮的衣裳，若是再配上水晶耳坠和时髦的术杖，谁都得为她回首，对吗，亲爱的？\
**Cooper the Healer**: So this lovely young lady is family all the way from France, Mecuria? Well, let me be her guide to the wonders of America! Look at her pretty outfit, add some crystal earrings and a stylish wand, I bet she'll be knock-out, am I right?

**玛蒂尔达**：呃……谢谢你的热情接待，但、但玛蒂尔达肩负着重要的逛街……任务！很高兴认识你，库伯……女士。\
**Matilda**: Umm, I appreciate your hospitality, madame, but I, I have a very important mission, a shopping mission! So much shopping to do. So, nice to meet you, Ms. Cooper.

**商贩梅克卢**：放开这个可怜人吧，库伯教授——\
**Maich the Peddler**: Let go of the poor girl, Cooper.

**商贩梅克卢**：还是让我带这位小姐见识一下那些从遗迹里出来的珍品，那些古老神秘学家所遗留下来的智慧比你那些徒有其表的玩意儿，美妙多了！\
**Maich the Peddler**: It's time I show her some real treasures. I'm sure they are much more suited to her than your old trash.

**商贩梅克卢**：而且，那位“长生不死的商人”出没在新纪元集市的消息已经坐实……据说她的手上可多了不少“旧东西”，谁会不想去大饱眼福一番？\
**Maich the Peddler**: Oh, and I oughta tell you, the "Merchant of Eternity" says she'll soon come to the New Age Market, and she's bringing her stock of treasures. It's gotta draw in the crowds.

**疗愈师库伯**：哼！少来了，梅克卢。温妮弗雷德女士才不会理您这样散发着腐朽味儿的老古董……\
**Cooper the Healer**: Ah, give it up, Maich. There's no way Eternity will like that old junk.

一场争执近在咫尺。\
The two vendors square up. They appear to be on course for either a confrontation or an embrace.

**环状水星**：呵呵……我喜欢你们聊天的样子，就像两团光晕缓缓融在一起，不分彼此。\
**Mercuria**: Heh heh. Will you two ever just fess up and admit you're friends?

两位争执的人陷入了羞耻的沉默。\
The two gawk at her words, looking at each other before falling into embarrassed silence.

**商贩梅克卢**：咳、咳……好了，环状水星……别揶揄我们了……你跟这位小姐要是有什么忙需要帮，直接提就是了。\
**Maich the Peddler**: Ahem, fine, fine, Mercuria, you don't have to poke fun, just let us know how we can help you.

她像是一位随时准备慷慨解囊的富翁敞开钱包。\
She responds with a greedy sort of look, as if opening up her purse strings.

**环状水星**：一扇门，梅克卢。我们需要找到你曾经所说的，那扇门的所在。\
**Mercuria**: A door. We're looking for a door, or a gate, the one you mentioned before.

**商贩梅克卢**：……\
**Maich the Peddler**: ...

她的喉咙被扼住了。\
She chokes out her next words.

**商贩梅克卢**：门……吗？抱歉，你得给我点时间回忆回忆。对了！你、你可以先带玛蒂尔达小姐到处逛逛，我一整天都在这儿，哪都不去。\
**Maich the Peddler**: A ... door? Sorry, I need time to ... recall it. Hey, why don't you show Ms. Bouanich around, and I'll stay here to gather my ... memories, not going anywhere.

**商贩梅克卢**：瞧，我现在还在收拾这些……乱七八糟的东西——我的脑袋没法同时干两样事儿。\
**Maich the Peddler**: I'm still trying to rack my brain, and this old thing can only manage one thing at a time.

她的借口并不高明。\
It is an unconvincing excuse.

然而，她们的脚边确实垒满了书籍、占卜盘……与零零散散的日用品。\
But the moment gives Mercuria pause to examine her surroundings, books, tools, daily necessities, all in various states of being packed away.

**环状水星**：这是你们的行李吗？\
**Mercuria**: Is this your luggage? You're packing up?

**疗愈师库伯**：是的……我们打算在“庆典”之前离开。\
**Cooper the Healer**: Yeah. We're leaving this place. Before the wackos hold their "ceremony," if we're lucky.

**疗愈师库伯**：我们本为了躲避宗教与政治的纠缠，寻找到一片能互不干涉的土壤，可如今那些纷扰已经如疾病传染到了这片土地。\
**Cooper the Healer**: When we came here, it was to find some safe place away from these people and their conflicts, but now they followed us here as well.

**疗愈师库伯**：我们失去了很多朋友，很多。\
**Cooper the Healer**: And we've already lost too many friends.

她低下了头，仿若哀悼。\
Her head falls low and limp.

**疗愈师库伯**：我们诚心希望你们也能……尽早离开这里。\
**Cooper the Healer**: I suggest you follow us out, before whatever is going to happen here happens.

**玛蒂尔达**：可……你们怎么能这样轻易放弃赖以生存的地方……\
**Matilda**: But, is this not where you made your living? Can you so easily walk away?

**玛蒂尔达**：我还以为……海特街的人都是像J那样顽固不化的傻大个呢……\
**Matilda**: I thought everyone on Haight Street would be just as stubborn as J.

**玛蒂尔达**：不过也是，这起码还算一件明智的事情……\
**Matilda**: But I think it's a wise choice.

**商贩梅克卢**：“明智”，呵……\
**Maich the Peddler**: "Wise"? Huh.

她重复了一遍。\
She repeats the words as if insulting herself.

**商贩梅克卢**：不，你弄错了。我们从不属于海特街，也不属于新纪元集市，我们甚至不占有任何物品。不管到哪儿，我们也只是在上面留下短暂的足印。\
**Maich the Peddler**: Don't make me laugh. Haight Street, New Age Market, none of this is ours really. Even the clothes on our back. All we own are the footprints we leave behind, until they're washed away by the tides of time.

**商贩梅克卢**：玛蒂尔达小姐，我们早已习惯了跟蒲公英一样生存，我们对纷争没有兴趣。\
**Maich the Peddler**: We live our lives on the fringes of a world that is not kind to us. We're used to it. Fighting for every street, it's not worth it.

**玛蒂尔达**：唔……可你们那些朋友——\
**Matilda**: Um, but your friends ...

“砰！”——梅克卢使劲将箱子合上。\
"Bang!"—Maich slams the suitcase shut.

**商贩梅克卢**：他们有自己的命运！！！\
**Maich the Peddler**: Maybe you ought to stop nosing around where you don't belong.

**环状水星**：抱歉……\
**Mercuria**: I'm sorry.

她轻轻拉住了旁边的女孩。\
She gently tugs Matilda to her side.

**环状水星**：我们走吧，玛蒂尔达小姐……梅克卢女士尚有她自己的事情要完成。\
**Mercuria**: Come on, we should get going. Maich has got things to do.

**玛蒂尔达**：……\
**Matilda**: ...

她们转过身，融入了另一片人群之中。\
They turn around and blend into the passing crowd.

直到她们的身影再也不见。\
Until they disappear within the milieu.

**疗愈师库伯**：你知道你不该那么对那个女孩……\
**Cooper the Healer**: You shouldn't be so hard on her.

**疗愈师库伯**：我们都明白，你说服不了自己。我们的信条并不总是忠贞于我们的所思所想。\
**Cooper the Healer**: You've had a hard enough time convincing yourself of what you have to do.

她坐下来，握住梅克卢颤抖的手。\
She sits down to comfort Maich.

**疗愈师库伯**：去做你该做的事。\
**Cooper the Healer**: Let's just focus on what's next. Nothing more.

**玛蒂尔达**：唔……说好了时间，环状水星女士怎么还没回来……明明只是临时接待客人而已。\
**Matilda**: Hmm. What's keeping Ms. Mercuria? There were only a few unexpected patrons; she should have already returned.

她朝着环状水星的帐篷走去，里面的三个影子在火光下格外显眼。\
She walks toward Mercuria's tent, where three shadows linger conspicuously in the firelight.

**商贩梅克卢**：等等！玛蒂尔达小姐！\
**Maich the Peddler**: Wait, Ms. Matilda!

**玛蒂尔达**：嗯？你也是来找环状水星女士的吗……？\
**Matilda**: Hmm? Oh, are you looking for Mercuria?

**商贩梅克卢**：嘘……！\
**Maich the Peddler**: Shh!

她恍然失色。\
The peddler is pale with anxiety.

**商贩梅克卢**：不，不是的……！我专程为你而来。\
**Maich the Peddler**: N-no, I'm looking for you.

**商贩梅克卢**：我必须向你承认，我扯了个谎……玛蒂尔达小姐。为了解救我的朋友们，我其实……曾对那扇门进行过详密的调查。\
**Maich the Peddler**: I have to admit something, Ms. Bouanich. I lied to you about the gate, but I have to, to protect my friends.

**玛蒂尔达**：可我不明白，这……对你来说有什么好隐瞒的？\
**Matilda**: What do you mean? Why do you feel you have to lie?

对方摇了摇头。\
The woman shakes her head ruefully.

**商贩梅克卢**：我只是认出了你——圣洛夫基金会的人，所以觉得可以将这个交付给你……你们。\
**Maich the Peddler**: Because I wanted to give this to you in private. I know you're from the Foundation, and I think I can trust you.

**商贩梅克卢**：我希望你能为环状水星着想，让她别涉险其中……因此才要隐瞒。\
**Maich the Peddler**: I know Mercuria better than anyone. If she knows the information I have, she will risk everything to help her friends.

她犹豫着下一句话，接着还是说出了口。\
She hesitates over her next words.

**商贩梅克卢**：我知道她的脾性，远甚于你们。\
**Maich the Peddler**: So please, don't tell her this. Don't put her in danger.

**玛蒂尔达**：但这恐怕并不取决于我……\
**Matilda**: I do not think I can make this decision for you.

**商贩梅克卢**：我当然明白……我不打算以监护人的态度去控制我的朋友，所以……我只能提出自己的希望。\
**Maich the Peddler**: I get your concern, but she's my friend. I don't want to put her on a dangerous path.

**商贩梅克卢**：那么……\
**Maich the Peddler**: So ...

她靠近玛蒂尔达的肩膀。\
She leans closer still.

万籁寂静中，窃窃私语融入风声，几不可闻。\
Whispers mingle with the wind, barely audible.

环状水星的帐篷另一侧，赶来了另一个急匆匆的脚步。\
Quick and light steps approach Mercuria's tent.

**猫眼维森**：唔……那帐篷里有三个家伙呆着？！我就说嘛！头儿一定在这里！\
**Cateye Wisen**: Hmm, there's three guys in that tent. I knew the boss was here!

**猫眼维森**：不过，还有一个人……是霍利克吗？听说他也在集市打听消息……\
**Cateye Wisen**: But who's the third dude? Hollick? I heard he was in the market collecting information.

他的手正揭开帘布，却撞上了一个高大的身躯。\
His hand has only just lifted the curtain when he feels the weight of a tall figure behind him.

**猫眼维森**：什么……你怎么会在这里？\
**Cateye Wisen**: What?! Why are you here?!

**猫眼维森**：莱格斯的走狗！！！\
**Cateye Wisen**: You're that big guy, Legers's lackey!

**杰洛**：？！\
**Gio**: ?!

被察觉的恐惧，令他慌不择路地远离了帐篷。\
Gio turns back, afraid of being seen.

男孩背向着帐篷，俯下身子，以冷冽的眼神盯着他。\
The boy, now facing away from the tent, stares at the man with cold calculation.

裤兜里，小刀蓄势待发。\
He reaches into his pocket to a waiting knife, ready for action.

但男孩并未注意到，背后帘布之上，另一只宽大的手掌正伸过来……\
But the boy fails to notice a hand reaching out from behind the curtain …

**猫眼维森**：唔……@#￥*&\
**Cateye Wisen**: Uggh ...

夜幕被隔绝于外，灯光迷离的舞厅已聚集了一众好男好女。\
The night outside is kept at bay by the soft glow of lights from the dance floor.

人们贴近着彼此，暧昧的目光交织，手臂交缠又摆动——\
People press close to each other, exchanging suggestive glances, arms entwining and swaying.

喧闹之中，坐在吧台的女孩格格不入。\
Amid the intoxicating scene, the small girl at the bar is noticeably out of place.

**玛蒂尔达**：唔……该怎么办呢？如果把钥匙与门的消息告诉了J，那也同样没法瞒住环状水星女士了……\
**Matilda**: Oh. What should I do? If I were to tell J about the key and the gate, then Ms. Mercuria will soon know it, too.

**玛蒂尔达**：根据调查员守则，现在等待基金会的支援才是最安全的方式……可万一事态恶化，更多无辜的平民将陷入危险……\
**Matilda**: According to the investigator's manual, waiting for support is the safest action. But if this situation escalates any further, more civilians might be involved.

**玛蒂尔达**：到底要不要让环状水星女士加入计划呢……？\
**Matilda**: Perhaps then I should let Ms. Mercuria join, no?

**玛蒂尔达**：唉，而且J今晚都去哪儿了，连个人影都没冒出来，真是一个没有危机感的家伙……\
**Matilda**: *sigh* Where did J go? He's not returned once all night. That man has no sense!

**玛蒂尔达**：待会就轮到环状水星女士上台了……我必须得在此之前决定下来。\
**Matilda**: Ms. Mercuria will go on stage soon. I must decide before she goes.

她趴在桌子上，琢磨不定，两手推移着小杯子。\
She leans on the table, adrift in her own mind, rocking a small cup back and forth with her hands.

**先驱者**：玛蒂尔达小姐，你看起来像是在考虑某只股票抑或某项不动产投资的风险……还请让我给你一杯热可可，帮你展展眉头，你现在可还没到皱眉头的年纪。\
**Pioneer**: Ms. Bouanich, it seems as though you're having a bit of trouble selecting between putting your money in stocks or real estate. Why don't you take this cup of hot chocolate to smooth out your furrowed brow? You're too young to have such a serious face.

他伸手紧了紧领带，像是一位准备邀舞的绅士。\
He adjusts his tie performatively.

**先驱者**：作为海特街专业的投资与服装顾问，我曾为不少出人头地的朋友提供过帮助……你大可以向我咨询以钱生钱之道。\
**Pioneer**: You know, besides my modeling career, I'm also a professional investment and costume advisor, and the success of my friends is my best advertisement. Feel free to reach out for a consult if you're interested in making your money make money.

**玛蒂尔达**：谢谢。唔……好吧，一向无所不知的玛蒂尔达确实遇到了一些……投资上的难题。\
**Matilda**: Thank you. Actually, I do have a problem that, as you say, relates to money.

**玛蒂尔达**：我听说在一座魔窟里，有两袋金子，它们的重量惊人，而不管是谁都没法同时带出来……\
**Matilda**: It seems I have now two bags of gold in a cave, surprisingly heavy, and no one person could take both of them out alone.

**玛蒂尔达**：可里面又有个吃金子的魔鬼，等得越久，落进它肚子里的金子就越多……所以我等得越久，到手的金子就越少。\
**Matilda**: However, there is a dragon devouring the gold. The longer I am hesitant, the more it eats and the less I can take.

**玛蒂尔达**：可我……又不想让身边唯一的朋友在我的牵涉下，和我一同进入魔窟——呜哇，我到底在说些什么呀！\
**Matilda**: But I don't want my friend to risk their life for it. Ahhh, what am I talking about?!

**玛蒂尔达**：请你还是把玛蒂尔达说的这些话忘掉吧……\
**Matilda**: Please forget it, forget everything.

女孩埋下了头，啜吸着热可可。一旁的顾问却严肃地扶着下颚。\
Matilda lowers her lips back to the cup, sipping her hot cocoa. Her advisor lifts his chin seriously and ponders her words.

**先驱者**：……玛蒂尔达小姐，可这两袋金子并不唯你所独有，不是吗？\
**Pioneer**: Ms. Bouanich, am I right to infer that these two bags of gold don't properly belong to you?

**先驱者**：如果你的朋友做出抉择，那你最该做的，是收起高尚的怜悯，就像你尊重自己的抉择一样，尊重你的朋友。\
**Pioneer**: So then, if your friend decides to go with you, then you should respect them and their decision. They want to take on that risk with you.

**先驱者**：你瞧，我在年轻时也做过不少糟糕的建议……我曾让一位食不果腹的赌徒输掉了住所，也同样曾让一位父亲重新赢得了妻子与孩子——而他们不过是同一个人。\
**Pioneer**: I admit, I've offered some poor advice since I first awakened. My suggestions at times have lost a gambler his home, but they also helped a father win back his wife and children. Surprisingly enough, they were the very same man.

**先驱者**：若你担任顾问像我这样久了，就会明白，我们的想法从不能改变他人将行的道路，将着的衣装。\
**Pioneer**: When you provide as much advice as I have, you realize that our words can't really change another person's fate.

**先驱者**：这就是为什么我爱那些站在橱窗前，衣衫褴褛，可眼中始终熠熠生辉的顾客。\
**Pioneer**: That's why I love watching window shoppers, the ragged folk that can't make it in, because they have the light of life in their eyes.

**先驱者**：即便他们身无分文——但我明白，总有一天，总有一天……他们会来取走这件属于他们的衣装。\
**Pioneer**: Penniless as they are, I know that one day, some of them will return and take the clothes that they only dreamed of wearing before.

**先驱者**：而我最喜欢做的，只是在那天，将那件衣服指给他们中到来的那一位——\
**Pioneer**: And my favorite thing is to point it out to them when the day finally comes, and say:

**先驱者**：“瞧，它就在那儿等您。”\
**Pioneer**: "It's been waiting there for you."

音乐骤然停止了——\
The music stops.

**玛蒂尔达**：嗯？\
**Matilda**: Hmm?

一只手揭开晶光粼粼的帘子，从舞厅的走廊里伸了出来。\
A hand pulls aside the glittering curtain.

人们出了窍般，目光齐聚，眼睛跟着她的步伐挪移。\
People seem entranced, their eyes following her every move.

环状水星赤脚踏上舞台，手臂犹如鸟儿般，高举于灯下——凝滞，相片般定格。\
Mercuria steps barefoot onto the stage, her arms raised like wings beneath the lights—motionless, frozen like a photograph.

**先驱者**：嘘……开始了。\
**Pioneer**: Shh. The performance is about to begin.

起先——是一个音符，撞击上另一个音符。\
At first, one note collides with another.

其后，音乐犹如浪潮般倾涌而来，声浪将所有人包裹在一团共振之下。\
Then, the music rises like a crashing wave, enveloping everyone in its vibration.

可没有人摇摆，亦无人赞颂或质疑，人们只是目不转睛地盯着她。\
Yet no one sways or cheers as it washes over them; people simply stare at Mercuria with rapt attention.

手中碰杯的人们，悬置着酒杯；痴迷于电子游戏的男人，命数随着声效一条条减少——\
Those drinking from their glasses and mugs pause midair; from the arcade slack-jawed boys usher in a cascade of digitized voices repeating, "Game Over."

而她的臂膀，时而如同扑展而上的羽翼般颤动，时而同泥壤深处的种子般，沿着光蜿蜒而上，破土而出——直至顶点，回归死亡般的寂静。\
She flourishes her arms, stretching them up toward the light, like a hopeful seed emerging from the soil, until she reaches a sensual peak, and the music stops at a cut.

**环状水星**：……\
...

“啪——啪啪啪……”\
"Clap—clap, clap …"

那整齐如一的掌声不绝，盖过了喧闹，令舞厅犹如教堂般的肃穆。\
The applause rises up over the room, reaching a crescendo until falling silent.

**玛蒂尔达**：我不明白，他们为什么能这么着迷。她的每个动作都没有踩在节奏上……这些是毫无根据的舞蹈，我感觉——很不舒适。\
**Matilda**: I do not understand. She is not dancing with the rhythm, and her movements, they are so bizarre.

**先驱者**：呵呵，你听过“陶醉”的意思吗？这个词来自于希腊，意即“从当下离开”。\
**Pioneer**: Ms. Bouanich, do you happen to know the meaning of the word "ecstasy"? It originates from the Greek word "ekstasis," meaning "standing outside" or "transcending oneself."

**先驱者**：人们已经被那些层出不穷的电视广告、吃角子老虎机、电子游戏……被这一切的一切摆弄太久……\
**Pioneer**: People have been controlled by the commercials, slot machines, arcades for so long, so long that they've lost sight of themselves.

**先驱者**：灵魂如果被躯体所奴役，便会产生叛逆之心——人们正是为此而来。\
**Pioneer**: Souls too long constrained become rebellious, seeking something real outside the boundaries of convention, and the illusions of flash and neon.

**先驱者**：为了见证一场不随音乐而摆动的舞蹈，为了学会不随他们眼前的“鼓点”翩翩起舞。\
**Pioneer**: So, they gather here, for a dance that is free from the limits of rhythm and timing.

**先驱者**：她理解那些在时代中诚惶诚恐的人。\
**Pioneer**: She understands the heavy burden of time.

**先驱者**：但她同样明白，她不是他者命运的编织者，她跟我一样，只能将选择权交还给顾客、求助者……\
**Pioneer**: But she also understands that she doesn't decide the fate of others. Like me, she provides another option, but in the end, we can only make decisions for ourselves.

**先驱者**：所以她只以自己的方式，带着他们短暂远离喧嚣的一切。\
**Pioneer**: Her dance offers to break them away from the reality of time and the weight of decision, even for just one song.

原本踮着脚尖的舞者将脚跟落地。她鞠了一躬，走下舞台。\
The dancer, who has been on tiptoe, lowers her heels to the ground. She bows before making her exit.

舞厅重回喧闹，就像她从未来过。\
The dance floor regains its excitement.

不安的灵魂再度回归于娱乐与快感的怀抱。\
Its restless souls returning to the embrace of the night's pleasures.

**玛蒂尔达**：我……明白了，看来我必须去告诉她。谢谢你，先驱者先生。\
**Matilda**: I see. Then I must tell her! Thank you, Mr. Pioneer.

“哒、哒哒——”她的脚步那般轻快。\
"Tap, tap-tap—" Her footsteps are light and quick.

**玛蒂尔达**：环状水星女士竟然没有去休息室……噢，她走得这样焦急，我得快一些赶上去。\
**Matilda**: She's in such a hurry, but why is she not heading to the lounge? I must catch up with her.

**玛蒂尔达**：哈、哈哈……嗯？她、她去哪儿了？\
**Matilda**: *panting* Huh? Where is she?

弯腰喘息的女孩，却望见了远处熟悉的身影。\
The girl, doubled over to catch her breath, spots a familiar hulking silhouette in the distance.

——然而那并不是她想要的答案。\
But it only leaves her more bewildered.

**玛蒂尔达**：那是……先前出现在帐篷里的杰洛先生？哈！我就说，记忆超群的玛蒂尔达肯定没有记错。\
**Matilda**: Why, that is ... that is indeed Mr. Gio inside her tent? Ha, I knew my memory did not fail me.

她捏起鼻子，躲在黑色的垃圾袋旁。\
She pinches her nose and dives into a nearby pile of garbage bags.

**玛蒂尔达**：环状水星女士肯定把什么秘密藏了起来，这位先生对她而言似乎是位特殊的客人……可如果他来自重塑之手……\
**Matilda**: So she is hiding something from us, and this Gio seems special to her. But if he is from Manus ...

**玛蒂尔达**：不不，不，停止你的联想，玛蒂尔达！环状水星女士是一位还算不错的朋友……\
**Matilda**: No, stop it, Matilda! You mustn't make such rash assumptions. Mercuria could not be ...

她缩进去的肩膀，被推了推。\
Her huddled shoulders are nudged.

**玛蒂尔达**：？！\
**Matilda**: ?!

眼皮恍惚间变得沉重，四肢变得绵软。\
Her eyelids grow heavy, and her limbs go weak and limp.

**玛蒂尔达**：什……么——\
**Matilda**: What ... is ...

**环状水星**：……\
**Mercuria**: ...

**环状水星**：玛蒂尔达小姐，好好睡一觉吧。\
**Mercuria**: Sweet dreams, Tildy.

**环状水星**：……你恐怕并不明白，这条通往“乐园”的道路，只容许我一人通过。\
**Mercuria**: The road to "Elysium" is mine, and only mine.

## FT-10 再见，鼠辈 / See You, Rats

**玛蒂尔达**：呃……唔，呜哇！\
**Matilda**: Ugh ... Whoa!

床上的女孩从昏迷中惊醒过来。\
Matilda awakes from her stupor.

**玛蒂尔达**：这里……是，餐馆后的房间？\
**Matilda**: Where am I? Is this the room behind the restaurant?

被褥整整齐齐地叠放着，窗户上贴满了胶布，那是缝补的痕迹。\
The bedding is neatly pressed and folded, and the windows are covered in a patchwork of repairs.

即便是间旧房间，却没有沾上丝毫灰尘。\
Despite the age and disrepair of the room, it is clean, nearly spotless.

**玛蒂尔达**：不行，我得快点起来……！环状水星女士跟着那个家伙离开了，我必须得警告J，环状水星女士已经……背叛了我们。\
**Matilda**: I must move quickly! Ms. Mercuria left with that man. She's betrayed us. I have to warn J!

**玛蒂尔达**：庆典在即……她很有可能会泄露我们的计划。\
**Matilda**: The ceremony is coming. She'll give away our plan.

她起身，试图打开门。“咔！”\
She picks herself up and move to open the door—Click!

**玛蒂尔达**：什么，门被锁住了？\
**Matilda**: What?! It's locked?!

**玛蒂尔达**：他们把我抛在这里了吗？糟糕、糟糕……联络器还在我的箱子里……\
**Matilda**: Did they just leave me here all alone? Oh, wait, the contact device. It's still in my suitcase.

**？？？**：我给您带了份礼物，J先生。\
**???**: I brought you a gift, J.

门缝里传来了一个似曾相识的声音。\
A familiar voice slides beneath the gap in the door.

**玛蒂尔达**：外面……还有其他人？\
**Matilda**: Who's that out there?

**玛蒂尔达**：噢？这怎么刚好有个破洞？\
**Matilda**: Hm? There's a hole in the door.

门板下，一个被布遮盖得并不严实的洞孔。\
There is indeed a hole covered with a loose cloth.

她凑近去，视线穿过了破洞，将外面的一切尽收眼中。\
She leans closer, peering through the hole, taking in everything outside.

声音的主人坐在圆桌前，那是她曾在集市中见过的面孔。\
The familiar voice came from a man sitting at a round table, a face she had seen before in the market.

**玛蒂尔达**：他们……都在这里？\
**Matilda**: They're all here!

**莱格斯**：鉴于我的孩子们，曾对您进行过不礼貌的骚扰，我决定将谈判的主动权交至您的手里。\
**Legers**: As an apology for my children's poor behavior, I'd like you to take charge of this negotiation.

J迟疑了一阵，扫视一遍莱格斯的下属。\
J hesitates for a moment, scanning the ranks of Legers's subordinates.

**J**：谢谢你的慷慨，老头子，但你恐怕不明白，我们从未向外发过邀请函……\
**J**: Thanks, grandpa, but we both know we're not having a party here.

**J**：而且你那位不礼貌的孩子——杰洛，怎么没过来露露面？就算是道歉，也得有诚意，不是吗？\
**J**: And why doesn't your boy Gio come over and apologize himself?

**莱格斯**：J先生，让我给您一句忠告，少用骨头引诱有主人的家犬……把关心留给自己的人吧。\
**Legers**: Let me give you a piece of advice, J: don't go tempting dogs away from their owners. Pay attention to your own men.

**莱格斯**：或者是我误会了你们？这份礼物——霍利克先生，不属于你们的一员，对吗？\
**Legers**: Or did I misunderstand? This gift from us, Mr. Hollick, he a friend of yours?

**异种格拉瓦库斯**：嘶……&#￥！\
**Glawackus Mutant**: *roar*

他身后沉默的人墙退开了一条道路。\
The wall of people behind him part, creating a path.

魔精拖行着满身血污的男人，将他甩在了地上。\
The critter drags a bloodied man behind it, throwing him onto the ground.

**猫眼维森**：是……霍利克！\
**Cateye Wisen**: It's Hollick!

**霍利克**：噗……咳、咳……抱、抱歉，J，我去了新纪元集市。\
**Hollick**: *coughs* I-I'm sorry, J. I went to the New Age Market.

**霍利克**：咳……我、我只是想，也许能出个好主意……\
**Hollick**: *coughs* I-I just thought, maybe there was something I could do.

他的四肢犹如脱线的木偶，已支撑不起身体，浓稠的血从嘴里一呛一呛地流出来。\
His limbs hang loosely like a puppet with broken strings, unable to support his body, and thick blood gurgles in his mouth.

一杆左轮手枪，正抵在他奄奄一息的胸膛。\
A revolver is pressed down against his gasping chest.

**贝克特**：莱格斯，你这个狗**！我、我一定会把你的脑袋给敲碎，拿去喂你自己的那些狗崽子！\
**Becket**: Legers, you piece of s**t! I'll smash your head in and feed it to your dogs!

**先驱者**：别过去，贝克特！我们不能成为把柄！\
**Pioneer**: Don't do it, Becket! We already have a captive to save!

先驱者的臂膀牢牢拴住了失控的朋友。\
Pioneer holds back Becket as he rages.

**莱格斯**：你的怜悯该留给你的朋友，而不是那块不属于你的新纪元集市。\
**Legers**: You should focus on your friends. Forget about the New Age Market. It doesn't belong to you.

**J**：……\
**J**: ...

**莱格斯**：不过别担心，我尤其擅长帮犹豫不决的朋友做出决定。\
**Legers**: Don't worry. Helping people make decisions is a particular skill of mine. I can be very motivating.

他起身，拍了拍J的肩膀。\
He stands up and pats J on the shoulder.

**莱格斯**：让我们来玩一场赌局吧，你们这群大孩子都喜欢游戏，不是吗？\
**Legers**: Let's play a game. You big boys love playing games, don't you?

他指了指霍利克胸前那柄发亮的左轮手枪。\
He points to the revolver poking Hollick's chest.

**莱格斯**：盯紧了，那把满膛四发的左轮手枪里头，正好塞着四枚子弹，那就是我的筹码。\
**Legers**: Take a look. This revolver is fully loaded with four bullets. Here's how you play.

**莱格斯**：只要您答应一个条件，我就可以卸下一颗子弹——这是一场公平的赌局，直到所有子弹退膛，您就可以轻易赢得这场游戏。\
**Legers**: I give you a condition. If you accept, I remove one bullet. When all the chambers are empty, you win. If you take your chances and reject a condition ...

**莱格斯**：当然，您也可以赌赌下一发的运气……\
**Legers**: I shoot. Just know that I might bury a bullet in your skull.

**莱格斯**：我给的选择很自由，不是吗？呵呵……又或者，您想试试子弹满膛的胜率？\
**Legers**: I totally respect your freedom of choice. You're even welcome to try your luck with all four bullets loaded, if you like.

旁边的持枪者，示意般地旋转着左轮手枪的弹巢。\
The gunman spins the cylinder of his revolver.

一抹亮光闪过男孩的猫眼。\
A glint of light flashes across the boy's cat-like eyes.

**猫眼维森**：我……我能看清他旋转弹巢的动作！头儿也许可以用最小的筹码——赢得这场赌局!\
**Cateye Wisen**: I-I can see the bullets in the chamber when he rolls the cylinder! Alright, I gotta count for the boss. Gotta help him survive the game at the lowest price.

他赶忙跑向了厨房……\
He dashes into the kitchen.

**猫眼维森**：J先生，你们的杯子拿过来了……\
**Cateye Wisen**: Here's your glass, boss.

**J**：谢谢你，维森……我想我正需要来一杯。\
**J**: Thanks, Wisen. I could use a drink.

J抽开杯垫子底下的纸张，余光瞥了一眼，接着重重咳嗽了几声。\
J pulls out the paper from under the coaster, glancing at it from the corner of his eye, and then coughs into it heavily.

纸张上的文字被唾沫所湿润，渐渐糊成了一片黑。\
As he removes it, the faint black ink has smeared beyond recognition.

**猫眼维森**：我的眼睛很敏锐！我能干很多细活……我擅长数火车、数硬币，我还可以看清那些出千的发牌员，连水滴都能数清楚！\
**Cateye Wisen**: I got sharp eyes! I can do lots of stuff! Counting coins, cars, finding water drops ... I'm great at spotting cheats and shady dealers!

**J**：……\
**J**: ...

他将纸巾递回给了维森，迟疑一阵，还是点了点头。\
He hands the paper back to Wisen, hesitating for a moment before nodding.

**J**：……我很乐意陪你耍耍这场赌局，老头子。\
**J**: Alright, let's do this, grandpa.

**J**：维森小子……把吧台那瓶龙舌兰拿出来，倒杯酒，让咱们的脑袋都清醒清醒。\
**J**: Wisen, get that tequila from the bar. Need a drink to clear our minds.

**猫眼维森**：是的……头儿。\
**Cateye Wisen**: On it, boss.

男孩从吧台中拎出了酒瓶，为两人斟满了子弹杯。\
The boy pulls a bottle up from behind the bar and fills two shot glasses.

**莱格斯**：呵呵，您有一个机灵的小伙计。\
**Legers**: Heh, that's a clever kid you got there.

**莱格斯**：让我们开始吧，孩子……\
**Legers**: Alright, let's get started, kiddo.

满膛的左轮，被无意义地旋转着弹膛。\
The cylinder is spun again. Four rounds, four demands—two ways that this can end.

**莱格斯**：一，你是否愿意将不属于你的东西，交还给我们？\
**Legers**: Condition one: Return what you took from us.

**J**：当然。\
**J**: Sure.

没有丝毫的犹豫，他从兜里掏出钥匙，放置在桌面上，推了过去。\
Without hesitation, he pulls the key from his pocket, places it on the table, and pushes it forward to the elderly man.

**莱格斯**：喔，哈哈哈，您很爽快，这恐怕是我所见过的最痛快的交易，J先生。\
**Legers**: Hahaha. Continue like this, J, and this'll be the best game I ever played.

他身后的人群响起了嗤嗤的笑声。\
A snicker rises from the crowd behind him.

**“牙医”Ⅱ**：我还以为他起码会犹豫一阵，小子们，你们的头儿确实是个孬种……哈哈哈。\
**"Dentist" II**: I thought he'd hesitate, at least a little bit. Looks like you got a coward for a boss, boys! Hahaha!

第一颗子弹退出了枪膛，弹巢再次被快速地转动。\
The first bullet is pulled from the chamber, and the cylinder is spun again.

男孩正以几不可闻的声音嘟囔着。\
The boy mutters inaudibly.

**猫眼维森**：5、8、10……\
**Cateye Wisen**: Five, eight, ten, ten times.

**猫眼维森**：不……下一发仍是有子弹的一膛。\
**Cateye Wisen**: The next chamber's loaded.

男孩俯身而来，再次满上了子弹杯。\
He leans in and refills the shot glasses once more.

**J**：……谢谢你，维森。\
**J**: Thanks, Wisen.

**莱格斯**：二，让你的人都离开这里，就现在，孩子。\
**Legers**: Condition two: Get your people out of here. Now.

**莱格斯**：我们需要一个安静的空间，您的朋友聒噪过了头，令我们都心烦意乱。\
**Legers**: We need quiet. Your friends are disturbing our conversation.

**J**：……把门都打开，离开这儿，朋友们。\
**J**: You heard him, guys. Get outta here.

无人应答，所有人都站在原地。\
But no one moves.

显然这个问题的决定权并不在他的手里。\
This is a decision that falls out of his authority. Each of his crew has to make it on their own.

**先驱者**：……维森小子，照顾好你的头儿。\
**Pioneer**: Wisen, take good care of your boss.

第一位退场者出现了。\
The first to decide makes his exit.

**贝克特**：J，我宁愿跟这个杂碎一块儿死！你到底在干些什么？你什么时候成了这样的孬种了？！\
**Becket**: J, what're you doing?! I'd rather take this bastard to hell with me! When did you become such a coward?!

**J**：不，朋友……你们呆在这儿帮不上任何忙，走吧——\
**J**: No, guys. You're not helping by staying here. Just go.

贝克特踹开凳子，却仍死死盯着他。\
Becket kicks the chair fruitlessly, holding his stare.

**贝克特**：呸……！\
**Becket**: Damn it!

人群熙熙攘攘地离开，餐馆内顷刻间只剩下了另一边的人。\
Becket breaks, as he makes his exit, the rest follow, until J sits alone.

**莱格斯**：很高兴与您合作，J先生……呵呵，看来您有一个足够务实的脑袋。\
**Legers**: Hah. It's a pleasure doing business with you, J. You're a practical man.

**莱格斯**：而且，“受苦者”在上，我们都看见了您有一颗宝贵的怜悯之心……\
**Legers**: May the Sufferer bless you. There's no denying that you got a merciful heart.

“叮。”——第二颗子弹退出了枪膛，轮盘再次转动。\
"Clink"—the second bullet is pulled from its chamber, and the cylinder spins once more.

**猫眼维森**：10、18……！\
**Cateye Wisen**: Ten ... Eighteen times!

**猫眼维森**：！！！\
**Cateye Wisen**: !!!

敏锐的猫眼，洞察到了一瞬的机遇。\
The keen cat eyes a fleeting opportunity.

**猫眼维森**：这次开枪，将会连续出现两个空膛！头儿必须知道这个机会！\
**Cateye Wisen**: The next two shots are safe! I gotta tell the boss!

男孩握紧了手中的酒瓶，在J的酒杯中倾倒着——恰好止于半杯。\
The boy grips the bottle tightly as he pours its contents into J's glass, filling it only half-way.

他正打算将手缩回来——\
When just as he lifts his hand—

**莱格斯**：倒满点儿，孩子，别客气……我会替J先生给你小费的。\
**Legers**: Fill it to the top, kiddo. Don't skimp on him. I'll tip you if J doesn't.

他的手掌就像坚硬的枯木，将男孩牢牢抓住了。\
Legers's rough and firm hands grasp the boy's own.

**猫眼维森**：好的……先生。\
**Cateye Wisen**: Yes, sir.

那杯象征着机会的酒，转眼间成了一个失败的暗示。\
That had been only half of the code, he couldn't be sure that J would understand now. It is too great a risk to continue.

**莱格斯**：那么，让我向您提出第三个要求——\
**Legers**: Now, condition three ...

然而，未收到暗示的赌徒却摇了摇头。\
J shakes his head, dismissing the words before he speaks them.

**J**：你们已经输掉了这场游戏，莱格斯。\
**J**: You've already lost the game, Legers.

J的目光，从维森手臂上的红色握痕移开了。\
J's gaze shifts away from the red marks on Wisen's arm.

**莱格斯**：噢，您想试试一半的概率，是吗？——可是孩子，我从来没有说过，我们只会开一枪。\
**Legers**: Oh, so you wanna take your chances, huh? Figured fifty-fifty was close enough? But you know, kiddo, I never said I would only shoot once.

J埋下头，握住了博伊刀的柄。\
J bows his head, gripping the handle of his Bowie knife.

**J**：试试看，老头子。\
**J**: Try it, old man.

**莱格斯**：扳机。\
**Legers**: Do it.

“哒。”\
"Click."

“牙医”手里的左轮枪传来第一声空响。\
The hammer drops into an empty chamber.

**“牙医”Ⅱ**：你很走运，小子……让我们再多试试。\
**"Dentist" II**: You got lucky, kid. Now let's try that again.

J俯下身，靴子在地上发出巨大的摩擦声。\
J crouches as his boots shift loudly against the floor.

从剑鞘之中，一道寒冽的冷光如水流般划出……\
From the scabbard, a cold gleam reflects the room's dim lights, like the stars on a sheet of ice.

**“牙医”Ⅱ**：？！\
**"Dentist" II**: ?!

“哒。”\
"Click."

左轮又是一声空响。\
The cocked hammer falls and finds another empty chamber.

J的剑鞘完全褪去，露出明晃晃的剑刃。\
J's blade slides out from its sheath.

星点的火花震颤而出——\
Sparks fly, trembling in the air—

**“牙医”Ⅱ**：幸运小子，来见见血吧——\
**"Dentist" II**: Eat lead, you lucky bastard!

“嘣——！”\
"Bang—!"

震耳的枪声响彻餐馆。\
The deafening gunshot echoes against the walls.

**霍利克**：咳、咳咳……J……！\
**Hollick**: *coughs* J!

**J**：如你所见。\
**J**: See what happens when you mess with me?

墙壁上多出了一个洞孔。\
A new hole appears in the wall.

一只抓握着手枪的手臂，掉落在地。\
And the revolver falls to the ground, still gripped by a severed arm.

**“牙医”Ⅱ**：呃啊……！\
**"Dentist" II**: Ugh! No ...

**J**：老头子，咱们的赌局到此为止了。\
**J**: Game's over, grandpa.

**莱格斯**：J先生，我们选择加注……\
**Legers**: Oh, but we'd prefer to continue.

**莱格斯**：孩子们，把他们的脸撕下来。\
**Legers**: Kids, rip his face off.

博伊刀指向了他的喉头。\
The Bowie knife is pointed at his throat.

**J**：如你所愿，老头子。\
**J**: If that's the way it's gotta be, let's do this, old man.

**J**：现在，天平向我们倾斜了。\
**J**: But this time, we got the upper hand.

**J**：你要不要，送回从我们手里拿走的东西，乖乖带着你的狗崽子爬回你的老巢？\
**J**: Now, give back what you took, and I'll let you and your little lackeys go.

**J**：或者——\
**J**: Or ...

刃尖刺破脖颈的皮肤，血从中点点渗出来。\
The blade's tip pierces the skin of his neck, and blood trickles from the wound.

莱格斯耐人寻味地盯着J，就像赌局之外的旁观者。\
Legers surveys J with a pensive stare.

**莱格斯**：您为我展示了聪明的脑袋，J先生。但您显然欠缺失败的经验，我很荣幸能为您上这一堂课。\
**Legers**: You're a smart kid, J, but apparently, you need a lesson in failure. I'll be glad to give it to you.

**莱格斯**：赌局之外，另有一场赌局……枪膛的每一发子弹，都不是虚发的。\
**Legers**: We were actually playing two games just now. Those "missed" shots? They had a purpose.

**莱格斯**：那两颗没能射穿他胸膛的子弹，自然会“射”向其他地方……\
**Legers**: They may not have hit you, but they did hit our second target.

“砰！”\
"Boom!"

剧烈的爆炸声震荡，滚滚的火焰迸发而出。\
An explosion shakes the room, erupting with a surge of flames.

**猫眼维森**：头儿，那是……霍利克的修车铺……还有你的车子？！\
**Cateye Wisen**: Boss, that's Hollick's garage. And your bike!

**莱格斯**：把刀抬下去……孩子，这还只是场外的小筹码，为了让你明白，这还不是结束。\
**Legers**: Put down the knife, kiddo. That was just a warning, to let you know the game isn't over yet.

**莱格斯**：接下来，你还会答应我最后一个条件——目送我和孩子们离开这里。\
**Legers**: Now, I got one last condition: Let us leave in peace.

**莱格斯**：你同意吗？\
**Legers**: So? What do you say?

**贝克特**：伙计们，快过来帮帮忙！……该死的，这是霍利克唯一吃饭的活计了！\
**Becket**: Guys, help me out! Hollick needs this place to live, damn it!

门外的人们奋不顾身地扑打着火焰，而火焰却愈燃愈烈。\
People outside desperately beat at the flames, but the fire grows fiercer despite their efforts.

**莱格斯**：我也可以把整条海特街都变成黑炭，只要您乐意。\
**Legers**: I can turn all of Haight Street to ashes if you want me to.

博伊刀被抬了下去。\
The Bowie knife is lowered.

**莱格斯**：很好，J先生，谢谢你的合作。\
**Legers**: Good boy.

**莱格斯**：另外……呵呵，换把刀子吧，它还不如这些狗崽子的牙齿硬实。\
**Legers**: By the way, get yourself a better knife. I got butter knives sharper than that thing.

“嘣——！”\
"Bang—!"

没有任何反应时间，枪口迸出火焰——\
Without any time to react, the gun's muzzle flares.

博伊刀分崩离析。\
His Bowie knife shatters into pieces.

**莱格斯**：这是对你乱丢骨头的一点点小警告。\
**Legers**: A warning, for trying to take my men.

**J**：……\
**J**: ...

火焰舔舐着焦黑的残骸，贝克特失神地跪坐在地上。\
Flames lick at the charred debris, as Becket sits dazed on the ground.

海特街的人们，沉默地望着这场大火，望着这最后的通牒。\
The people of Haight Street gather silently, watching the fire, seeing their final ultimatum unfold.

于是，第一个人从跪坐中起来，走向了J。\
Then, the daze lifts, and Becket rises with an outburst.

**贝克特**：我和霍利克在街头刚认识你的时候，你还不是个孬种……J。\
**Becket**: What happened to you, J? You were fearless when Hollick and I first met you.

**贝克特**：那时候，咱们就像几只卑贱的野狗，翻着垃圾桶，到处游荡……除了一副顽固的硬骨头，口袋空空，什么也不剩下……可咱们还是走到了现在。\
**Becket**: We were like a pack of stray dogs, rummaging through the trash cans and sleeping on the street. All we had were clothes on our backs, but we still made it this far.

**贝克特**：我他*甘愿把血流干，把骨头折断，也不会求饶一声……可现在，你在想什么，J？\
**Becket**: I'd rather break my bones and shed my last drop of blood than beg for mercy. But look at you, J. What were you thinking?

**贝克特**：我是跟了一个孬种吗？我们的头儿是个孬种吗？\
**Becket**: Are you a coward, Boss?

他啐了一口痰，搀扶起地上的霍利克。\
He spits on the ground as he helps the bloodied Hollick to his feet.

徽章被鄙弃地丢到了垃圾桶中。\
He holds J's gaze as he unpins his badge and tosses it into the trash.

**霍利克**：这不怪他，都是我。咳、咳……贝克特，留下来，求求你留下来。\
**Hollick**: Don't blame him, Becket. It's my fault. *coughs* Please don't go.

**霍利克**：……J，我、我会回来帮你的！\
**Hollick**: J! I-I'll come back to help!

拉扯着他的贝克特，抑制不住怒火。\
Becket pulls at Hollick, unable to contain his anger any longer.

**贝克特**：你要是真的明白这事儿是因为你而起，就别再他*瞎逞能帮忙了！\
**Becket**: Oh, come on, Hollick! You just said that this is your fault. So do me a favor and shut up.

**贝克特**：你还不明白就是因为你，才变成现在这个局面的吗？！但凡你的脑袋长点记性，也不会被人抓住把柄！\
**Becket**: You know you're the one who got us into this mess, right?! If you'd learned your damn lesson, none of this would have happened!

**贝克特**：闭嘴吧！\
**Becket**: So just shut up!

霍利克垂下了头，那是无法反驳的责怪……\
Hollick hangs his head, dejected and quiet.

贝克特硬拽走了沉默的伤员。\
Becket forcibly drags the wounded giant away.

**J**：……\
**J**: ...

旋即是人群中的第二个人——\
Then, another from the crowd.

**乞丐布莱恩**：J，对不起……我只是想找个能够睡觉的铺盖，我、我还没想过要把命都搭在这里……\
**Brian the Beggar**: S-sorry, Mr. J. All I wanted was a safe place to sleep, not all this. I-I don't wanna get killed.

他逃也似的，如同恐惧瘟疫一般，丢下第二个徽章。\
He leaves behind the second badge and fearfully makes his way from the street.

第三个、第四个……他们瑟瑟发抖，他们心怀不甘——他们知道自己是微不足道的芸芸众生之一。\
The third and fourth ... They tremble, reluctant, feeling their own smallness in the crowd.

火苗渐熄，灰烬如同群鸟飘荡。\
The flames dwindle, and ashes hang in the air.

人群溃散，留下了空荡荡的街巷，一切宛如废墟。\
The crowd breaks apart slowly and wordlessly, until they've left only an empty, burned-out street.

**猫眼维森**：头儿，我……我去把贝克特他们劝回来！他们，还有这一切……\
**Cateye Wisen**: Boss, I'll, I'll get them to come back! We'll get everything back!

**猫眼维森**：嘿、嘿……！\
**Cateye Wisen**: Hey! Hey!

他跑向溃散的人群，背影如此单薄。\
He runs out to catch the crowd, but soon he too grasps his vulnerability.

仿若落了单的鸟儿。\
Like a straggling bird, left out from the flock.

## FT-11 炉火与铁砧 / Ingle and Anvil

少许的灰烬飘浮在空气中，让人们内心的恐惧浮浮沉沉。\
The club's air is thick with smoldering ash and smoke.

“开业中”的招牌在门口孤零零地晃悠着，路过的人们行色匆匆，唯恐在店门前驻留。\
The "Open" sign swings forlornly at the door. Those few that still pass it on the street do so quickly, as if running past a graveyard.

餐馆前所未有的冷清。\
Even in the heart of the city, it feels remote.

**玛蒂尔达**：是的……我现在正位于海特街379号待命。我已经嘱托了赶回基金会的两名职员，他们随后将带领你们过来……\
**Matilda**: Yes. I am awaiting orders at 379 Haight Street now. I have sent two investigators back to the branch. They'll show you the way.

**玛蒂尔达**：碍于事发突然……我会提前赶到那里，并向你们发送我最新的坐标位置。\
**Matilda**: Since time is limited, I will go to the target location in advance and update you on my coordinates.

**联络器**：这也许将是我们剿灭重塑之手的又一个新节点……玛蒂尔达小姐，您为我们提供了一个至关重要的讯息。\
**SPF-I**: This mission will bring us one step closer to eliminating Manus Vindictae. You have provided us with vital information thus far, Ms. Bouanich.

**联络器**：请时刻保持联系……紧急援助小队将很快赶来。\
**SPF-I**: Please stay in touch. The reinforcement squad will arrive soon.

**玛蒂尔达**：另、另外……我还需要补充另一则消息……\
**Matilda**: And, one more thing.

她欲言又止，但还是说了下去。\
She stops, but eventually cannot help but continue.

**玛蒂尔达**：我们其中一位神秘学家朋友有可能已经叛投了重塑之手，唔……圣洛夫基金会的支援恐怕会被他们有所防范……\
**Matilda**: One of our arcanist friends may have defected to Manus Vindictae. I believe they'll be expecting us and the reinforcements.

**玛蒂尔达**：这是我个人的疏忽，我希望允许我事先探路，为后续的支援提供帮助……\
**Matilda**: This was my personal oversight, so I hope you will allow me to scout ahead. That way, I can provide optimal support for the following operation.

联络器的另一端沉默片刻，响起了一阵喧嚣。\
The other end of the line is silent, until a staticky clamor breaks through.

随后，是一个斩钉截铁的答复。\
It comes with a resolute reply.

**联络器**：请务必遵守命令，在新纪元集市等待支援，玛蒂尔达调查员。\
**SPF-I**: Your current mission is to wait for reinforcements at the New Age Market. Please follow your orders, Investigator Bouanich.

**玛蒂尔达**：好的……我明白。\
**Matilda**: Understood.

她咬紧嘴唇，沮丧地将联络器收回了口袋中。\
She bites her lip, disheartened, and puts the device back into her pocket.

增援的消息已经抵达，但她却无论如何也难以平复那焦躁的内心。\
It is good news, but she can't calm the turmoil within her.

**先驱者**：我听说，环状水星女士今早去了莱格斯的地界……\
**Pioneer**: I heard Ms. Mercuria went to Legers's place this morning.

**先驱者**：……玛蒂尔达小姐，我们已经做到了力所能及的一切——这并非你的过错。\
**Pioneer**: Ms. Bouanich, we've done everything we can. It's not your fault.

她摇了摇头，已无心答复这些安慰。\
She shakes her head, no longer in the mood to respond to any words of comfort.

**玛蒂尔达**：莱格斯和那帮神秘学家已经让新纪元集市脱离了轨道，我现在更需要保证的是你们的安全……\
**Matilda**: Legers and those arcanists have made a total mess of the market. The people's safety is our top priority now.

**玛蒂尔达**：从今早开始，J那个家伙就不见了人影……等基金会到达的时候，他必须得在这里……\
**Matilda**: J's been away since this morning. He has to be here when the reinforcements arrive.

**玛蒂尔达**：他去哪儿了？\
**Matilda**: Where did he go?

假人耸了耸肩。\
The mannequin shrugs.

**先驱者**：他哪儿也没去……玛蒂尔达小姐，他就在这儿。\
**Pioneer**: Nowhere, Ms. Bouanich. He's right there.

他指了指厨房的后门。\
He points to the back door of the kitchen, held slightly ajar.

虚掩着的后门中，传来循序渐进的敲击声——\
From behind it comes a rhythmic, metallic sound.

“叮——”\
"Clink—"

“叮、叮——”\
"Ding, ding—"

“叮、叮——叮！”\
"Ding, ding—ding!"

她走上前去，穿过拥挤的厨房，穿过满目的酱汁、生面包片、脏盘子……\
She steps forward, moving through the cluttered kitchen, past sauces, grills, and towers of unwashed plates.

**玛蒂尔达**：他在……干什么？\
**Matilda**: What's he doing?

端着杯子的假人摇了摇头，拒绝了回应。\
The mannequin turns his head to the door, giving no response.

她打开了虚掩的门，步入其中。\
She pushes the door open and steps inside.

……\
...

**J**：哈，说实话，我以为自己这辈子都不会再把这脏兮兮的东西拿出来了……\
**J**: Hah, to be honest, I thought I'd never use this thing again.

他的锤子，犹如巨人的脚掌一般，重重砸在滚烫发红的金属上。\
His hammer strikes down heavily on the glowing, red-hot metal. Something tells her they fell harder than they should.

**J**：我还记得那天，我老爸在客厅，神神秘秘地跟所有朋友说，他在那次旅行中，找到了世界上最了不得的宝物——自从我的母亲去世以后，谁也没见他那么高兴过。\
**J**: I remember that day. Dad was in the living room with his friends, boasting about this awesome treasure he found on his trip. Hadn't seen him smile like that since Mom died.

**J**：人们都以为他从那堆光秃秃的土堆底下找到了什么好东西，巴结着他。\
**J**: Heh. His friends all sucked up to him. Thought he dug up some good stuff.

**J**：那时候我还是个乳臭未干、爱垂头丧气的小子，谁见了也不痛快。\
**J**: I was just a whiney little kid back then. No one liked me.

**J**：等人们走光了，他让我穿上一身紧巴巴的制服，就像要才艺表演似的，领着一脸苦相的我去了天鹅绒餐厅……\
**J**: After his friends left, Dad put me in a suit and tie, like I was some kind of stage performer, and took me to the Velvet Restaurant.

**J**：他牵着我的手，接着把另一个小姑娘带到我面前——说：“嘿，小伙子。我为你找了个妹妹。”\
**J**: When we got there, he brought this little girl to me and said, "Hey son, I got you a little sister."

**J**：我第一次见到了保利娜和她的母亲，我知道他没有撒谎，他确实为我们带来了宝物——一段慢悠悠的，踮着脚尖吃甜品，快活得能飘起来的日子。\
**J**: That was the first time I met Paulina and her mom. I realized that he wasn't lying about the treasure. The days after were sweet, like eating dessert on cloud nine every day.

火星在他的瞳孔中，迸溅。\
Sparks fly across his eyes.

**J**：但作为一个穷困潦倒的保险推销员，从世代铸剑的维兰德家族里溜出来的私生子……他的野心太大，而力量又太小。\
**J**: But it didn't last long. My dad was nothing but a broke insurance agent after he ran away from the Wayland family. He had big dreams, but he was too weak to realize them.

**玛蒂尔达**：维兰德……家族？我在第一防线学校编纂的《秘学与金属》里听过这个家族。\
**Matilda**: The Wayland family? I've read about them in the Arcanum and Metal, compiled by the SPDM.

**玛蒂尔达**：他们世代都是秘学冶金工匠，其中尤以铸剑盛名……可、可这个家族不是早已经在战争中灭亡了吗？\
**Matilda**: They've been arcane blacksmiths, famous for their sword-making, for generations. But the book says the family perished in the war.

**J**：不管哪个时代，小家伙……那些弱小的人都会躲到阴暗的洞里面，学会隐藏自己的力量，只在真正需要它时，才去使用。\
**J**: No matter what generation, Frenchie, weak people cower in dark holes, learn to hide their power, and only use it when they really need it.

**J**：不够“胆小”的人，是无法存活的……老爸去世以后，我就比谁都明白这个道理。\
**J**: Being reckless can kill you. I've learned that better than anyone since my old man died.

**J**：那些巴结他的人猜对了，他靠着家族留下来的“所罗门的手稿”，从遗迹底下翻出了一坨看上去一文不值、黑不溜秋的铁块儿。\
**J**: And, you know what? His friends were right. He followed Solomon's Manuscript, a document left behind by his family, and dug up something from under the ruins. A worthless piece of black iron.

**玛蒂尔达**：“所罗门的手稿”？……可这在圣洛夫基金会属于机密信息，不可能有其他人知道……你们把那个铁块儿藏在哪了？\
**Matilda**: Solomon's Manuscript? That document holds top-secret information, only available to certain members of the Foundation. How did he get it? And what have you done with the iron?

**J**：一大半呢，早就成了我背上的那把东西，而剩下的余料……\
**J**: Most of it became this thing strapped to my back, and the rest ...

**J**：就在你眼前，小家伙……如今，跨越了这么长的时间，我才理解了我老爸，这确实是块好料子……\
**J**: Well, you're looking at it, girl. I didn't get why Dad said it was good stuff until now.

**J**：就像那些吉普赛巫婆，从听见孩童的第一声啼哭，就能断定他的一生是战士还是祭司一样——\
**J**: You know those witches who can tell at a glance whether a kid'll be a warrior or a priest?

**J**：即便只是一块余料，但从我瞧见它的第一眼起，它也将注定是一把好刀。\
**J**: When I looked at this scrap of metal, I had the same feeling. It was destined to be a killer knife.

**J**：而这会是它作为利刃的第一次出场。\
**J**: And now, it's gonna make its debut.

女孩瞥见了他脚底下的布袋，以及——远处一辆老旧却擦得瓦亮的摩托车。\
The girl catches sight of the cloth bag at his feet and, further away, a weathered but polished old motorcycle.

**玛蒂尔达**：……圣洛夫基金会的支援马上就要赶到，而且我已经破解了那把钥匙的术法……\
**Matilda**: Reinforcements will arrive soon, and I have decoded the spell on the key.

**玛蒂尔达**：J，你得好好呆在这里。\
**Matilda**: You have to wait, J.

**玛蒂尔达**：环状水星女士……已经加入了他们，我们无从得知她将会泄露什么情报……\
**Matilda**: Ms. Mercuria, she's joined Manus Vindictae. We have no way of knowing what information she's given them.

他摇了摇头。\
He shakes his head.

**J**：小家伙，我会亲自把我的朋友带回来……\
**J**: I don't need their help. I can bring my friends back myself, French Fry.

**J**：那帮疯子的庆典将至，我不打算眼睁睁地看着生我养我的这条街分崩离析……同样，我也不打算等你姗姗来迟的朋友。\
**J**: Those crazies are holding the ceremony soon. I'm not gonna let them destroy my birthplace. I'm not gonna wait for your little friends to arrive, either.

**玛蒂尔达**：你听我说，你根本没有任何必要以身犯险，圣洛夫基金会的支援很快就会到达，我们能最大程度地减小可能出现的伤亡。\
**Matilda**: Please, J, there's no reason to risk your life! The reinforcements will arrive in no time. Then we can finish this with minimum casualties.

**玛蒂尔达**：记住了，阅历丰富的调查员玛蒂尔达·布翁尼要教给你一个道理——准备万全才能把事情干得漂亮啊！\
**Matilda**: Take this lesson from the experienced Investigator Matilda Bouanich: preparation is the key to success!

年轻人畅快地笑起来。\
The young man laughs hard and steadily.

**J**：哈哈哈，你说得没错，小家伙……\
**J**: Hahaha, I guess you're right.

**J**：从我在街头摸爬滚打的日子来说，等一位警察、庇护人、老大——像是救世主那类的大人物——总是最优的选择，它能让我们避免无谓的流血与挨揍。\
**J**: When I was a scrawny little street kid, I'd look to a savior, like a cop or a boss, anything to avoid a beating.

**J**：我们都知道，怎么聪明地绕过麻烦。\
**J**: We all got the smarts to stay outta trouble.

**J**：我们会瞻前，与顾后。\
**J**: We just gotta look both ways before we make our move.

“叮——”\
"Clink—"

**老乞丐**：那是我所有的财产了，我恳求你们……那个空钱包对你们来说没有任何用处，里面就只有我妻子和女儿的照片。\
**Old Beggar**: This wallet is all I have, please! There's nothing in it! Just a photo of my wife and daughter!

**地痞Ⅰ**：来呀，老不死的家伙……有种就自己过来把你的东西拿回去——哈哈哈，接住，伯顿！\
**Rascal I**: C'mon, you old fogey. Take it back if you got the guts! Hahaha, Berton, catch!

**地痞Ⅱ**：过来，在这边，在这边，老头……噢？！别挡道，你这个臭熏熏的狗杂种。\
**Rascal II**: Over here, old man. Hey! Get out of the way, you stupid bastard!

**乞丐布莱恩**：……\
**Brian the Beggar**: ...

**老乞丐**：帮帮我，布莱恩……\
**Old Beggar**: Help me, Brian.

**乞丐布莱恩**：抱歉，抱歉……朋友……\
**Brian the Beggar**: I'm sorry. I'm sorry, friend.

他甩开老人哆哆嗦嗦的手，却始终没有迈开逃走的第一步。\
He shakes off the old man's trembling hand as if preparing to run.

**J**：我们忍让又谦逊。\
**J**: We show tolerance and modesty.

“叮——”\
"Clink—"

**修车铺老板**：霍利克，告诉我，你妈妈生你的时候是不是把你的脑子忘了？如果你再把昂贵的清洁剂用在这种破车上，半个子儿你都拿不到！\
**Garage Owner**: Hollick, tell me, did your brain slip outta your skull? Don't you know how expensive this cleaner is? Spray it on this piece of crap one more time, and you ain't getting a cent next month!

**霍利克**：可、可是……先生，顾客花钱买了这瓶清洁剂。\
**Hollick**: B-but, sir, the customer paid us to use this cleaner.

**修车铺老板**：我还花钱雇了你这个蠢家伙呢！你是要听我的，还是滚回去陪你那个烧焦的修车铺白日做梦？\
**Garage Owner**: And I pay you to work for me, you idiot! Either listen to me, or go back to daydreaming in that burnt-down garage of yours!

他胆怯地垂下头，望着自己空荡荡的口袋，欲言又止。\
He timidly glances downward, feeling at his empty pockets, struggling to find words.

**J**：谨慎又迟疑，量力而行，见好就收。\
**J**: We know our limits. Do what we can and give up when we have to.

“叮——”\
"Clink—"

**贝克特**：咳、咳……呸……\
**Becket**: *coughs and spits*

**裁判**：10、9、8、7……\
**Judge**: Ten, nine, eight, seven ...

**赌局庄家**：嘿、嘿，别再站起来了，蠢货！我保证，这局比赛结束后，肯定让你湿湿嘴！\
**Oddsmaker**: Hey, hey! Just stay down, you idiot! You'll get paid after the game, I promise!

**赌局庄家**：你这个没卵蛋的家伙！躺下去，咱们谁都能赚个盆满钵满！\
**Oddsmaker**: Oh c'mon! You think you're a tough man? Just stay down, and we'll make a fortune!

他的身躯已经竭尽了气力，但拳头仍紧紧握着。\
His body is exhausted, pushed over hard, yet his fist remains tightly clenched.

“叮——”\
"Clink—"

“叮、叮——叮！”\
"Ding, ding—ding!"

**J**：但如果你试过给这些剑淬火，就会明白，犹豫只会徒增裂纹。\
**J**: But if you've ever tried to temper a sword, you'd know that hesitation ruins the work.

滚烫的刀身坠入水中，瞬间涌起了无数气泡。\
The searing-hot blade plunges into the water, producing a hissing burst of bubbles and steam.

**J**：只有最闪烁的火遇上水，才能造就最好的钢——这个世道，还有另一种选择，另一种生活方式。\
**J**: You gotta be brave, decisive. That's how you make a great sword. That's how you live a great life.

**J**：它不需要你谨言慎行，不需要你万事俱备。\
**J**: You don't gotta be too careful about what you say and do. Don't gotta be prepared for everything.

他从水中拎出冷却好的剑身，置于柔软的裹布里。\
He pulls the cooled blade from the water and places it into the soft wrapping cloth.

这是一把新的博伊刀。\
A new Bowie knife.

**J**：因为——那些会颤抖的拳头，才拥有真正的力量。\
**J**: Because a brave and decisive fist ... Well, that's unstoppable.

**J**：我不会等待一切都准备好的，永远不会。你明白吗？\
**J**: I won't just stand back and wait like a coward. Never. You understand?

她踟蹰着。\
She hesitates.

**玛蒂尔达**：……呃，也许你说的是有些道理。但这已经严重违反了基金会此前下达的命令……\
**Matilda**: Perhaps you're right, but this would be a serious violation. You'll be going against the direct orders of the Foundation!

那焦躁的内心深处，一个答案已缓缓浮现。\
Deep within her restless mind, an answer is slowly emerging.

**玛蒂尔达**：因此……作为你的监督者，玛蒂尔达会牢牢跟紧你，防止你做出预料之外的蠢事！\
**Matilda**: Therefore, as your supervisor, I will keep an eye on you wherever you go, just in case you do something stupid.

一个头盔划过半空，丢到她的手中。\
